tāvat pūjyaṃ prayatnena yāvat kāryaṃ tu siddhyati |  
vyavahāra jayaṃ nāma vivāde vijayastathā ||  
  
rājñāṃ kule vivāde ca jayennātra saṃśayaḥ |  
mānonnatirbhavet tasya yaṃtrarājaprasādataḥ ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
yadicchedvaśagaṃ kartuṃ yāvajjīvaṃ varānane |  
tadā yaṃtraṃ prakurvīta gāṇapatyaṃ tu siddhidaṃ ||  
  
bhūrjapatraṃ samānīya viśṛtaṃ chidravarjitaṃ |  
anāmāraktasaṃyuktaṃ dviradasyamadaṃ tathā ||  
  
yāvakasya rasaṃ caiva rocanāṃ ca tathaiva ca |  
etaccatuṣṭayaṃ yojya jāti kāṣṭhena vai likhet ||  
  
hrīṃkārāḥ saptasaṃlekhyāḥ pūrvapaṃktau varānane |  
adhaḥpaṃktau tu saṃlekhyaṃ kro& hrī& klī& klī& tathaiva ca ||  
  
sādhyanāma tathāgaṃdha tataḥ paṃktau tṛtīyage |  
klī& hrī& karti vījāni hrī& hrī& tathaiva ca ||  
  
ekapaktau caturthaṃ tu hrīṃkārāṇāṃ catuṣṭayaṃ |  
evaṃ saṃlikhya vījāni dvāviṃśati samānakaṃ ||  
  
paścāntaṃ veṣṭayet samyak pūrvapaścima uttare |  
prāṅmukhāstu susaṃlikhyā gakārāstrīśasaṃkhyakāḥ ||  
  
sukṣetrāttu samānīya mṛttikāṃ kṛṣṇavarṇikāṃ |  
tathā gaṇapatiṃ kṛtvā yaṃtraṃ tasyodare kṣipet ||  
  
saṃpūjyagandhapuṣpādyairimaṃ maṃtramudīrayet |  
imaṃ maṃtraṃ mudāvaśyaṃ yāvajjīvaṃ kuru prabho ||  
  
idaṃ maṃtraṃ samuccārya hastamātraṃ likhatya ca |  
kṣiptvā tatra gaṇādhvasaṃ pūrayitvā ca mṛttikā ||  
  
yāvajjīvaṃ bhavedvaśyo gaṇarājaprasādataḥ |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi janavaśyakaraṃ paraṃ ||  
  
71b)  
  
madhye nāma likhitvā tu īkāraṃ vilikhedadhaḥ |  
oṃ namo namo lekhyaṃ paścime pūrvake dale ||  
  
oṃ ajite ajite caiva likhedakṣiṇa uttare |  
rājavaśyakaraṃ nāma yaṃtrarājaṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
tridinaṃ pūjayennityaṃ brahmacarya ratonaraḥ |  
hemaṃ ca rājataṃ vāpi paṭṭasūtraṃ viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
yaṃtrasya dhārayet pṛṣṭhe vāhumūlegaletha vā |  
sarveṣāṃ caiva yaṃtrāṇāṃ vidhireṣa prakīrtita ||  
  
śubhago darśanīyaśca svajanānāṃ ca vallabhaḥ |  
yaṃtrasya dhāraṇād devī sa bhavennātrasaṃśayaḥ ||  
  
karpūrakuṃkumairlekhyaṃ rocanā gurukeśaraiḥ |  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
jagadvaśyaṃ mahāyaṃtraṃ śṛṇu devī suśobhanaṃ |  
karpūro mṛganābhiśca candano rocanā tathā ||  
  
jātikāṣṭhena saṃlikhya yaṃtrato vījapaṃcake |  
paṃktau tṛtīye saṃlekhyaṃ ṭhakāraṃ tadanantaraṃ ||  
  
ukāraṃ ca jagannāma ṭhakāraṃ tadanantaraṃ |  
hrīṃkāraṃ ca tataḥ śānte evaṃ vai vījapaṃcake ||  
  
tasyāpi vilikhennūnaṃ ṭhakāraṃ tu caturthake |  
evaṃ vījāni saṃlikhya catuḥkoṇaṃ tu sthāpayet ||  
  
dvirekhāyā mahākāyaṃ jagadvaśyakaraṃ paraṃ |  
triloha veṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā dhārayed vāhu madhyataḥ ||  
  
jagadvaśyaṃ bhavet tasya yaṃtraṃ yāvacca tiṣṭhati |  
saṃpūjya nityamevādau yaṃtradevārcanādiṣu ||  
  
yadātabhṛtyaḥ krūddhe syāt yata sarvaṃ prakāśate |  
na śakyate nirākartuṃ deśakālavalena tu ||  
  
tathā ca mohanārthoyaṃ svasyārthasya ca siddhaye |  
yaṃtra paiśācakaṃ nāma kartavyaṃ ca vicakṣaṇaiḥ ||  
  
madhye nāma likhitvā tu vartulaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
caturdalaṃ prayatnena vījayuktaṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
hrīṃkārāścatvāro lekhyādalamadhye caturdiśaṃ |  
lekhanyābhūrjapatreṇa rocanayā likhennaraḥ ||  
  
tatastaṃ dadhimadhye tu kṣipedyantraṃ varaṃ śubhaṃ |  
sa vaśo jāyate nūnaṃ yaṃtrarāja prasādataḥ ||  
  
yaṃtrapiśācikā nāma bhṛtyavaśyakaraṃ paraṃ |  
  
72a)  
  
na deyaṃ yasya kasyāpi svayaṃ rudreṇa bhāṣitaṃ ||  
  
krūra prakṛtikaḥ svāmī yadā saṃsevyate janaiḥ |  
sevyamānopi hi sadā krudhyatyeva durāsadaḥ ||  
  
kharaiḥ parivṛto nityaṃ durācāro mahīpatiḥ |  
uttamo vādhvamo vāpi mleccho vā paṭutāṃ gataḥ ||  
  
yaṃtraṃ kālānalaṃ kuryāt tasya vaśya prasiddhaye |  
sādhyanāmākṣarā lekhyā hrīṃkāraṃ garbhamadhyagāḥ ||  
  
yāvat tasyā kṣarānāmnītā vṛtta eva hrī& tathā |  
ikāramaṃtraṃ saṃlekhyaṃ rocanā bhūrjapatrake ||  
  
trirāvṛtta catuṣkoṇaṃ dīrghagaṃ phūlavat kṛtaṃ |  
rājikā pratimāṃ kuryāt tatpādaśya ca pāṃśunā ||  
  
hṛtmadhye prakṣipet tasyā yaṃtraṃ kālānalaṃ mahat |  
saṃpūjya pratimāṃ tatra cūlhī pārśve nikhanya tu ||  
  
ajāraktena saṃmiśraṃ bhaktadhūpaṃ tathaiva ca |  
balidānaṃ pradātavyaṃ digpāla prītaye tadā ||  
  
oṃ mahākālāya svāhā ||  
  
iti maṃtreṇa juhuyādaṣṭottaraśataṃ tathā |  
tadaiva bhaktaṃ sājyaṃ tu rakta puṣpaistu miśritaṃ ||  
  
yaṃtrakālānalaṃ nāma tridaśairapi pūjitaṃ |  
vāṇijyārthaṃ tu vāṇijya lābhārthaṃ vāvatāmapi ||  
  
teṣāṃ madhye yadā kopi praduṣṭo jāyate janaḥ |  
mādeśa prabhūrvāpi tadā yaṃtraṃ prakalpayet ||  
  
hrīṃkārodara madhye tu sādhyanāmākṣaraṃ likhet |  
upariṣṭāt tataḥ kuryāccaturdikṣu krameṇa tu ||  
  
paścādveṣṭaya yaṃtraṃ ca catukoṇaṃ dvirekhayā |  
koṇe triśūlau dvau dvau tu caturdikṣu prakalpayet ||  
  
evaṃ yaṃtravaraṃ kṛtvā pūjayitvā tu prayatnataḥ |  
svaraktena tu saṃmiśraṃ rocanābhūrjapatrake ||  
  
vilikhya yaṃtravat kṛtvā svarahasi kṣipet tataḥ |  
tatkṣaṇājjāyate vaśyaṃ mahākrūropi mānavaḥ ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
yadā mahāvalaḥ śatruḥ parikartu hi vāṃchati |  
tadātatsānu kūlyārthaṃ yaṃtraṃ kurvīta kaṃcukaṃ ||  
  
72b)  
  
sādhyanāmalikhenmadhye caturdalena veṣṭayet |  
ikārāśceti kāraśca visagāṃtaṃ caturdiśaṃ ||  
  
ekaṃ kādyaṃ likhitvā tu vartulaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
śmaśānabhasmanālekhyamarkapatradvayopari ||  
  
saṃpuṭaṃ melayitvā tu vedhayet kaṃṭhakaistataḥ |  
likhanyāt pūjaye yaṃtraṃ śmaśāne niśi pūjitaṃ ||  
  
validānaṃ pradātavyaṃ bhūtale prayato naraḥ |  
tatkṣaṇājjāyate śatruḥ sānukulo na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
kaṭukākhyaṃ mahāyaṃtraṃ duṣṭasya mohanaṃ paraṃ |  
yathā śaktyā dakṣiṇā ca kālarātriśca priyatāṃ ||  
  
suhṛdvaṃdhavako vāpi śatrurvā kruddhate yadi |  
tadā kopaśāntyarthe kuryādyaṃtraṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu vedhayet kaṃṭhakairataḥ |  
upayedhaścottare ca dakṣiṇe ca viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
viṃducaryaṃ caturdikṣu veṣṭayitvā likhet tataḥ |  
huṃkāraṃ tu likhed garbhe viṃdu madhye tu yatnataḥ ||  
  
dakṣiṇe cottare caiva prasādhyaṃ nāmaveṣṭayet |  
aṃte huṃkārasaṃyuktaṃ madhyaṃ cedyaṃ prasādataḥ ||  
  
etadyaṃtre tu saṃlekhyaṃ tatra yaṃtra suvistare |  
kaṃṭake nāyasāne ca vilikhet somavāsare ||  
  
kulālamṛttikā madhye yaṃtraṃ kṣiptvā tu gorakaṃ |  
pūjāṃ kṛtvā vidhānena yasmātkopaṃ praśāmyati ||  
  
yāmadagdhaṃ mahāyaṃtraṃ sadyaḥ kopa haraṃ paraṃ |  
akrodhana satyavādī jamadagnirdṛḍhavrataḥ ||  
  
rāmasya janakaḥ sākṣāt satvamūrte namostute |  
evaṃ maṃtraṃ samuccārya pūjāṃte nityameva hi ||  
  
evaṃ saptadinaṃ kāryaṃ pūjopaharaṇaṃ paraṃ |  
saptame hanibhoktavyā brāhmaṇāvedapāragaḥ ||  
  
naivedyaṃ ca pradātavyaṃ māsamahāsvarṇayet |  
krodhastu hṛdayādi dvā prasanno jāyate kṣaṇāt ||  
  
ekapaṃktau tu saṃlekhyaṃ hrīṃkāratritayaṃ śubhe |  
tasyādhastātsamālekhyaṃ nāmavairamanasya ca ||  
  
tataḥ paṃktau tṛtīye syāt hrīṃkāra tritayaṃ punaḥ |  
tatastaṃ veṣṭayet samyak catukoṇaṃ tu lekhayā ||  
  
tataścāṣṭadalaṃ kuryādvījamāsaṃ prakalpayet |  
hrī& trayaṃ dalamadhye tu caturdikṣu prakalpayet ||  
  
73a)  
  
koṇe koṇe dalaṃ nyasya hrī&kāraṃ ca vicakṣaṇaḥ |  
rocanā kuṃkumaṃ caiva mṛganābhiṃ tu candanaṃ ||  
  
ekīkṛtya likhedyaṃtraṃ bhūrjapatresu vistṛte |  
dadhodasyāṃ śite pakṣe sādhakaścottarāmukhaḥ ||  
  
tadyaṃtraṃ pūjayennityaṃ rātraurātrau varānane |  
bhogairnānauvidhaiḥ puṣpairvastrālaṃkārabhūṣaṇaiḥ ||  
  
evaṃ saptadinaṃ kṛtvā tadaṃte ca catuṣṭayaṃ |  
striyaṃ saubhāgyasaṃyuktā bhojayet saptasaṃkhyayā ||  
  
śaṃkarasya priyā devī lalite priyatāmiti |  
rūpaṃ dehi yaśo dehi saubhāgyaṃ dehi vāṃchitaṃ ||  
  
etat maṃtraṃ samuccārya tataścāsya visarjayet |  
tadyaṃtraṃ cātunāveṣṭā svakaṇṭhe dhārayet tataḥ ||  
  
śubhagārūpasaṃpannā patipriyatarā bhavet |  
lalitākhyā mahāyaṃtraṃ strīṇāṃ saubhāgyakārakaṃ ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devī prayatnena yaṃtraṃ tṛtīyasādhanaṃ |  
yaṃ likhya priya nāmāni saṃkīrapuṭitaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
adhopari tathā lekhyaṃ sākāradvitayaṃ śubhe |  
tatastaṃ veṣṭayet samyak vartulaṃ lekha ekayā ||  
  
tasyoparidalānyaṣṭau hrīṃkārasahitān likhet |  
rocanā kuṃkumeṇaiva bhūrjapatre samālikhet ||  
  
tridinaṃ pūjayen nityaṃ rātrau rātrau tu pūrvavat |  
tatasnātvā caturthehni pūjayet śubhagātrayaṃ ||  
  
anaṃga vallabheddevī tvaṃ mesaṃ priyatāmiti |  
evaṃ priyamahāvaśyaṃ kartuṃ me smara vallabhe ||  
  
etanmaṃtraṃ samuccārya pūjayitvā ca tāḥ striyaḥ |  
tadyaṃtraṃ dhātu saṃyuktaṃ kṛtvā kaṇṭhetha dhārayet ||  
  
patirdāso bhavet tasyā yaṃtrarājaprasādataḥ |  
saubhāgyamatulaṃ tasyā jāyate nātrasaṃśayaḥ ||  
  
sa patniṃ na gaṇā yāti sarvasaubhāgyamandritā |  
ekāsuvāsinī pūjyā caturdaśyāṃ śite tare ||  
  
pakṣe pakṣe rati prityai pūjyaṃ yaṃtraṃ tu nityaśaḥ |  
yāsāṃ tāsāṃ na dātavyaṃ yaṃtraṃ saubhāgya vardhanīṃ ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
yoṣidvaśyaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu devī suśobhanaṃ |  
  
73b)  
  
rocanā kuṃkume naiva śrīkhaṇḍa mṛganābhinā ||  
  
bhūrjapatre tu saṃlekhyaṃ jāti kāṣṭhena yaṃtrakaṃ |  
ai& hrī& klī& ca tato nāma ai& hrī& klī& tathaiva ca ||  
  
evaṃ saṃpuṭitaṃ kṛtvā catukoṇaṃ tu veṣṭayet |  
uparyadhopi saṃlikhya dve vījānya prayatnataḥ ||  
  
ai& hrī& klī& ca tathākṣiṃ ca aiṃ cāṃte ca punastathā |  
koṇepi diśya vījāni ai& hrī& klī& ca tathaiva ca ||  
  
dalākṛtistu kartavyā madanasya tu kāṣṭhakaiḥ |  
tasya madhye tu nikṣipya yaṃtraṃ sarveṣu pūjayet ||  
  
bhogaiśca vividhairgaṃdhairdhūpairdīpaiḥ phalai śubhaiḥ |  
rātrau rātrau prakurvīta dināṃte pratyahaṃ śubhe ||  
  
evaṃ kṛte tu sā nārī dāsī nūnaṃ prajāyate |  
yaṃtraṃ śrīkāmarājākhyaṃ yo vidvaśyakaraṃ paraṃ ||  
  
saṃpūjyāścandane nātra rājikā pratimānaraiḥ |  
kāmo naṃgaḥ paṃcaśaraḥ kaṃdarpo mīnake tanaḥ ||  
  
śrīviṣṇutanayo devaṃ praśanno bhava me prabho |  
evaṃ maṃtraṃ prakartavyaṃ yāvat sā vaśyatāmiti ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devī pravakṣyāmi mānināṃ mānamardanaṃ |  
yaṃtraṃ pradurlabhaṃ loke mānināṃ khyāti mardanaṃ ||  
  
turaṃgasya tu raktena rocanā bhurjapatrakaiḥ |  
praṇavaṃ ca tathā hrī& ca sādhyanāmākṣaraṃ pṛthak ||  
  
nāmākṣarāṇi sarvāṇi hrī&kāra puṭitāni ca |  
aṃtādyaṃ praṇavaṃ lekhyameka paṃktau tathaiva ca ||  
  
tatastadveṣṭayet samyak catuṣkoṇaṃ ca rekhayā |  
uparyadhaśca saṃlekhya pūrvavadvījasaṃpuṭaṃ ||  
  
tiryag bhāge dvi paṃktau tu pūrvavat taṃtrasaṃpuṭaṃ |  
koṇe dalākṛtiṃ kṛtvā madanot kṛti madhyataḥ ||  
  
evaṃ yaṃtraṃ susaṃlekhya madana pratimāṃ śubhāṃ |  
mane desya tu kāṣṭhena kṛtvā hṛdi vinikṣipet ||  
  
sa raṃdhra hṛdayaṃ kuryāt tathā yaṃtraṃ su tiṣṭhati |  
saṃveṣṭya prakṣipet nūnaṃ yaṃtraṃ tasyorasi sphuṭaṃ ||  
  
raktacandanamālyaiśca pūjayetyahaṃ tataḥ |  
ekaviṃśati dinaṃ yāvat sā tasya vakṣyatāmiyāt ||  
  
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi rājastrī vaśyakārakaṃ |  
yathā tat dṛṣṭiṃ pātena kāmavāṇa kṛtā iva ||  
  
74a)  
  
pataṃti sahasā dṛṣṭvā maninyo mada vihvalāḥ |  
rocanā kuṃkume naiva bhūrjapatre likhennaraḥ ||  
  
karpūreṇa samaṃ yaṃtraṃ jātikāṣṭhe vidhānataḥ |  
ṣaṭkoṇasya tu madhye tu tasya nāma pratiṣṭhitaṃ ||  
  
krī&kāraṃ sarvato lekhyaṃ koṇopari tu sarvataḥ |  
pūrvakoṇaṃ tarāle tu hrī&kāraṃ dvitayaṃ likhet ||  
  
koṇamadhye likheccaivaṃ hrīṃkāraṃ pūrvasaṃsthitaṃ |  
tatsarvaṃ veṣṭayet tasya vartulaṃ lekhayāt śubhaṃ ||  
  
dakṣiṇe tridalaṃ kuryādī?śānepi dalaṃ tathā |  
hrī&kāraṃ dalamadhye tu krameṇa pravilekhayet ||  
  
evaṃ saṃlikhyata yaṃtraṃ pūjayed bhaktibhāvanaḥ |  
gaṃdhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ sutai vedyaiḥ śuklāṃvaradharaḥ svayaṃ ||  
  
cintayet tāṃ striyaṃ rātrau yaṃtrasya purataḥ sthitāṃ |  
evaṃ saptadinaṃ kuryāt tadante brāhmaṇa trayaṃ ||  
  
saṃbhojya vividhairbhojyaiḥ kāmākṣā priyatāmiti |  
śaktyā ca dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād bhojayet sādhakastrīyaṃ ||  
  
trilohaveṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā vāhumūletha dhārayet |  
taṃ dṛṣṭvā rājaramaṇī kaṃdarpojjvalapīḍitā ||  
  
svayaṃ saṃprāthayennityaṃ kākathetara yoṣiti |  
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi nijamekaṃ mahāphalaṃ ||  
  
taṃ yo dhārayate nityaṃ strīṇāṃ priyataro bhavet |  
yā strī dhārayate bhaktyā sā saubhāgyavati bhavet ||  
  
saubhāgya jananaṃ vījaṃ nṛṇāṃ caiva viśeṣataḥ |  
etadvījākṣaraṃ gopyaṃ na deyaṃ yasya kasyacit ||  
  
sakāraṃ ca hakāraṃ ca kakāraṃ ca tathaiva ca |  
rakāraṃ ca dakāraṃ ca ikārāntaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ krameṇa saṃyojyaṃ akṣarāṇāṃ ca ṣaṭkakaṃ |  
ikārasvara saṃyuktaṃ bindunā pariśobhitaṃ ||  
  
rocanā nīrayuktena bhurjapatre likhennaraḥ |  
tridinaṃ pūjanaṃ kṛtvā hemena veṣṭayet tataḥ ||  
  
puruṣo vāhu mūle ca nārī ca galake punaḥ |  
dhārayet vījarājāṃ yata sphuṭaṃ daurbhāgyanāśanaṃ ||  
  
mahāsaubhāgya jananaṃ śrīśivena puroditaṃ |  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi yaṃtraṃ saubhāgyadāyakaṃ |  
strīnāmeva samuddiṣṭaṃ yaṃtraṃ karaṇasaṃjñakaṃ ||  
  
74b)  
  
asyaivadhāraṇāddevī vaṃdhyā garbhavatī bhavet |  
mṛtavatsā tu yā nārī sāpyenaṃ yaṃtramuttamaṃ ||  
  
dhārayejjāyate devī jīvaputrā na saṃśayaḥ |  
rocanā kuṃkumeṇaiva bhūrjapatre likhet tataḥ ||  
  
praṇavaṃ tu likhet pūrvaṃ hrīṃkāraṃ tadanantaraṃ |  
tato ramananānāthaṃ hrīṃkārāntaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ ||  
  
hakāraṃ ca caturdikṣu dalamadhye vinirdiśet |  
uparyadhopi vilikhet krauṃkāramekamekakam ||   
  
hakāraṃ ca caturdikṣu dalamadhyeṣu vinyaset |  
oṃkāraṃ ca tathā hrīṃ ca yakāraṃ ca tathā likhet ||  
  
dalamadhye punarlekhya metadvīja catuṣṭayaṃ |  
koṇe koṇe dale lekhyaṃ madhyadeśe tu sādhaka ||  
  
evaṃ yaṃtraṃ ca saṃlekhya pūjayecca dinatrayaṃ |  
bhojayet mithunaṃ caikaṃ lokeśaḥ prīyatāmiti ||  
  
paścāt taṃtu sanāveṣṭana suvarṇena viśeṣataḥ |  
vartulamavaniṃ kṛtvā hāramadhye tu dhārayet ||  
  
dhāraṇājjāyate devi saubhāgyamatulaḥ mahat |  
jīvavatsā bhavennūnaṃ vaṃdhyātvaṃ ca prasāmyati ||  
  
kāmalākhyaṃ mahāyaṃtraṃ sṛṣṭaṃ tu brahmaṇā punaḥ |  
na deyaṃ yasya kasyāpi sādhakena varānane ||  
  
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi yaṃtramātrasya darśanaṃ |  
raktacaṃdanamiśreṇa svaraktairbhūrjapatrake ||  
  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu vartulaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
caturdalaṃ tataḥ kuryād vījaṃ yuktaṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
hu&kāraṃ dalamadhye tu pratyekaṃ vilikhet kramāt |  
evaṃ yaṃtraṃ suracyātha valipuṣpairmanoharaiḥ ||  
  
prakṣipet ghṛtamadhye tu ākṛṣṭistridinād bhavet |  
etadyaṃtraṃ mahāgopyaṃ rakṣanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ ||  
  
na deyaṃ yasya kasyāpi yadicchetsiddhimātmanaḥ |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi yaṃtraṃ traipurakaṃ mahat ||  
  
rocanānīrayuktena bhūrjapatre likhennaraḥ |  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu huṃkāra puṭitaṃ śubhaṃ ||  
  
ṣaṭkoṇaṃ vilikhet tasya nāmagarbhamanoharaṃ |  
saukārāt vilikhet koṇe madhyena bindubhūṣitān ||  
  
evaṃ yaṃtraṃ susaṃpūjya ghṛtamadhye vinikṣipet |  
pratyahaṃ saṃjapennityaṃ prārthayet tripurāṃ punaḥ ||  
  
75a)  
  
ākarṣayen mahāvegā devadattaṃ mama priyaṃ |  
tripure deva deveśī stubhyaṃ vāsya prayacchatu ||  
  
prārthayet manunānena tripurāyaṃtraṃ sādhayet |  
evaṃ kṛte saptamehni ākṛṣṭirjāyate śubhe ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi māninī karṣaṇaṃ śubhaṃ |  
rahasyaṃ sarvayaṃtrāṇāṃ tatkṣaṇāsiddhidāyakaṃ ||  
  
na vācyaṃ yasya kasyāpi yaṃtrarājaṃ suduṣkaraṃ |  
dakṣiṇā nāmikāraktena vāme karatale likhet ||  
  
praṇavaṃ ca tathā klī& klī& etat paṃktau likhennaraḥ |  
tasyā hyeti tritayaṃ traṃyaṃ bhūtasyādho likhet kramāt ||  
  
tasyāpyadho likhennāma ramanyāścaiva suvrate |  
trikoṇaṃ veṣṭayet paścād vījānāmuparo priye ||  
  
evaṃ kṛtvā tu saṃpūjya tatraiva kusumai śubhaiḥ |  
yāmamātreṇa sā nārī samāyāti na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
yaṃtraṃ śrīkāmarājākhyaṃ devānāmapi durlabhaṃ |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi yaṃtraṃ vai devamātṛkāṃ ||  
  
karṣaṇaṃ naranārīnāṃ śṛṇu devī mahāphalaṃ |  
lākṣārasaṃ haridrāṃ ca maṃjiṣṭhāṃ bhurjapatrake ||  
  
lekhanīyaṃ prayatnena ekānte yaṃtramuttamaṃ |  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu trikoṇaṃ veṣṭaye tataḥ ||  
  
taccāpi veṣṭayet paścād vartulaṃ yatnataḥ priye |  
tasyopari svarālekhyā ākārādyāśca ṣoḍaśa ||  
  
tatastaṃ veṣṭayet sarvaṃ lekhayā netra saṃkhyayā |  
tasyaiva pādadhūlyātha prakuryācchālabhaṃjikāṃ ||  
  
tasyā yonau tu saṃkṣipya yaṃtrarājaṃ supūjitaṃ |  
evaṃ kṛte tu kṛṣṭā sā samāyāti na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
vahunātra ki muktena patināsamamā nayet |  
yaṃtrarājaṃ mahāgopyaṃ deva mātṛka saṃjñakaṃ ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devī mahāyaṃtraṃ stambhanaṃ sarvavairiṇāṃ |  
vivāde vyavahārāṇāṃ mukhastaṃbhī bhaved dhruvaṃ ||  
  
yadākāla vaśā devī kalahaḥ saṃprajāyate |  
tadā kuryān mahāyaṃtraṃ jihvāvedhanakaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
rocanā bhūrjapatreṇa sulekhyaṃ suvicarcitaṃ |  
ṣaṭkoṣṭhakaṃ prakurvīta rekhādvitayakena ca ||  
  
75b)  
  
koṣṭhamadhye likhed vījaṃ yāti kāmi sahaikakaṃ |  
hakāraṃ ca sakāraṃ ca lakāraṃ tadanantaraṃ ||  
  
vakāraṃ ca rakāraṃ ca yakārāṃtaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ |  
ukārasvarasaṃyuktaṃ mastake rephabhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
vindumātrārddhasaṃyuktaṃ saṃyoge varṇaṣaṭkakaṃ |  
svaradvitayasaṃyuktaṃ bindunā paribhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ saṃjāyate vījaṃ mukhastaṃbhanasaṃjñakaṃ |  
koṣṭhe koṣṭhe tu saṃlekhyamekaikaṃ vījamuttamaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ vījāni saṃlekhya rekhā dvitīyake na hi |  
vījoparigatāṃ kṛtvā koṇaśede caturdiśaṃ ||  
  
vāhyarekhorddhvato lekhyā triśūlā mastakoparī |  
sarvato lekhayā cānte triśūlātvilikhe kramāt ||  
  
evaṃ dvāviṃśa saṃkhyakāstriśūlāgre pratiṣṭhitāḥ |  
śūlāṃtarāle sarvatra tathopari likhet kramāt ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi yātrā staṃbhaṃ tu suṃdarī |  
śirā saṃpuṭe saṃlekhyaṃ pītadravyena śobhanaṃ ||  
  
rocanā haritālaṃ ca haridrā ca manaḥśilā |  
kuṃkumeṇa samāyuktaṃ pītadravyaṃ pracakṣyate ||  
  
kuṃbhamohani vījāni ekapaṃktau likhennaraḥ |  
tasyāpyadho likhennāma mohanāṃte pratiṣṭhitaḥ ||  
  
tatastadveṣṭayet samyak catuḥkoṇaṃ tu lekhayā |  
koṇe koṇe triśūlaṃ tu madhye madhye tathaiva ca ||  
  
evamaṣṭha triśūlāni kṛtvā yaṃtroparisthitān |  
saṃpūjyapītakusumaiḥ yaṃtrarājaṃ suśobhanaṃ ||  
  
dhūpairdīpaiśca naivedyairnānābhakti samanvitaiḥ |  
evaṃ saṃpūjyataṃ yaṃtraṃ bhūmi madhye kṣipet tataḥ ||  
  
mṛdāpūryaśame deśe yaṃtrasyopari yatnataḥ |  
gamanaṃ staṃbhayatovamiti kāryaṃ vicāraṇāt ||  
  
yathā ropita bhāṇḍāpi nāyatvavapi me sadā |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi vācāṃstaṃbhan tu sundari ||  
  
prativādi mukhastaṃbhaṃ yaṃtraṃ khyātaṃ tu bhūtale |  
pītadravyena saṃlekhya śilāsaṃpuṭa madhyataḥ ||  
  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu trikoṇaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
tatastadveṣṭayet samyag vartulaṃ lekhayā punaḥ ||  
  
76a)  
  
tasyoparidalānyaṣṭau prakurvīta tataḥ paraṃ |  
dalamadhye nyased vījaṃ lakāraṃ bindubhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ cāṣṭadale lekhyaṃ pūjayet kusumaiḥ śubhaiḥ |   
pītavarṇaistathā dhūpa dīpanaivedyakaiḥ śubhaiḥ ||  
  
brāhmaṇaṃ bhojayeccaikaṃ pāyasena guḍena ca |  
tato niṣanya bhūmau tu sthāpanaṃ pūrvavat tataḥ ||  
  
prativādi mukhaṃ staṃbho jāyate nātra saṃśaya |  
etadyaṃtraṃ mahādevī sugopyaṃ kathitaṃ tava ||  
  
karṇikāraṃ kulatthaṃ ca caṃpakaṃ svarṇaketakīṃ |  
dhattūraṃ pītavahidrāṃ nāgakeśarameva ca ||  
  
tadā yaṃtraṃ prakurvīta sugamaṃ phalasiddhidaṃ |  
khaṭikapātu saṃlekhya svabhīttau vegataḥ priye ||  
  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu śatrostu vidhivat priye |  
tasyopari sthitā rekhā vasusaṃkhyāyate kramāt ||  
  
lekhā tu triśūlaṃ tu tallikhecca digaṣṭake |  
tatraiva tu susaṃpūjya svetaṃ puṣpaiḥ phalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ||  
  
anyaiśca  svetagandhaiśca śvetavastrairmanoharaiḥ |  
brāhmaṇaṃ bhojayeccaikaṃ sa śivaḥ priyatāmiti ||  
  
vivādepi sabhāyāṃ ca mukhastaṃbhaṃ karotvayaṃ |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi vahnistaṃbhaṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
divyakāle prakurvīta yaṃtrarājaṃ suśobhanaṃ |  
pītadravyena saṃlikhya bhūrjapatre varānane ||  
  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu kroṃplāmādyaṃ tu saṃpuṭaṃ |  
uparyadhopi vilikhet kroṃkāraṃ sumanoharaṃ ||  
  
tatastaṃ veṣṭayed devī catuṣkoṇaṃ tu lekhayā |  
tasyopari caturlekhaṃ lekhanīyā prayatnataḥ ||  
  
koṇāntarāle saṃlikhya lakāraṃ bindubhūṣitaṃ |  
evaṃ catuṣṭayaṃ lekhyaṃ lakārāṇāṃ tu vījakaṃ ||  
  
koṇāṃte tvaṣṭasaṃlekhyā triśūlāssarvathā priye |  
evamaṣṭatriśūlāni likhedatha prapūjayet ||  
  
saṃpūjya brāhmaṇaṃ bhojya yaṃtraṃ bhūmau vinikṣipet |  
vahamānodayamānena madhye yaṃtraṃ vidhāya ca ||  
  
yāvat tasyopariyāti salilaṃ trakhacaṃḍinī |  
tāvaddagdho mahāstaṃbho jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
divyasaṃ staṃbhanaṃ nāma yaṃtraṃ devaiḥ supūjitaṃ |  
  
76b)  
  
na deyaṃ yasya kasyāpi yadicchetsiddhimātmanaḥ ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devī pravakṣyāmi yaṃtraṃ vahninivāraṇaṃ |  
yasmin gṛhe sthitaṃ yaṃtraṃ tatranāgni bhayaṃ kvacit ||  
  
yasya haste sadā nityaṃ yaṃtrarājaṃ manoharaṃ |  
svapnapyagni bhayaṃ tasya kadācinnopajāyate ||  
  
valātkāreṇa kartavyamagni grahaṇakaṃ priye |  
vidyamāne tathā yaṃtre auṣadhi vā valādhike ||  
  
pādaspṛṣṭo yathā sarpo daśatyevananyamati |  
tathā staṃbhopi deveśi vatvātkāreṇa vā janaiḥ ||  
  
apamṛtyuṃ yadā devī haredvai vaidyako rasaḥ |  
tathā yaṃtropi deveśi apāṃtarabhayaṃ haret ||  
  
śrīkhaṇḍarocanā himena tu leṣanīyaṃ yaṃtraṃ tu bhūrjevavidhivaccatu   
suvisṛtena | nāma svakīyaṃ pravilikhya madhye suveṣṭayedvarttulaṃ lekhayāthā |  
  
tasyopari dalaṃ nūnaṃ cakāraṃ bindubhūṣitaṃ |  
  
pūrve ca dakṣiṇe caiva paścime cottare punaḥ |  
etatsarvaṃ tu saṃveṣṭya catuḥkoṇaṃ tu lekhayā ||  
  
trilohaveṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā vāhumūlegalathavā |  
athavā vāhumadhye tu kṣīramadhye viniḥkṣipet ||  
  
saṃpūjya ca nityamevaṃ devavadvijayapradaṃ |  
agneḥ sakāśāt bhītiryāsāsya kvāpi prajāyate ||  
  
brāhmaṇaṃ bhojayedekaṃ yaṃtrarājasya tuṣṭaye |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi priya staṃbhana kārakaṃ ||  
  
yadā kopi valāyāti śaritopi varānane |  
tadā tat staṃbhanaṃ kuryād yadā hyasu smito bhavet ||  
  
pīta draveṇasaṃmiśraṃ yatphalaṃ kaṣṭa?saṃbhavaṃ |  
khaṭikāyāṃ likhedyaṃtraṃ karake kāṣṭhasambhave ||  
  
yakāraṃ garbhamadhye tu sādhyanāma pratiṣṭhitaṃ |  
tatastaṃ veṣṭayet samyak catuṣkoṇaṃ tu rekhayā ||  
  
tasyopari catuṣkoṇaṃ dvitīyaṃ vilikhedbudhaḥ |  
koṇedalākṛtiṃ kuryāt madhyadeśe kvacit kvacit ||  
  
dalamadhye lakāraṃ tu vinduyuktaṃ likhet priye |  
evaṃ vilikhyasaṃpūjya vidhivadyaṃtramuttamaṃ ||  
  
77a)  
  
adhomukhaṃ nibadhniyāt karakaṃ gṛhamadhyataḥ |  
tatra stambho bhaved devī nātrakaryāvicāraṇā ||  
  
tathāpi ca tato yattu gatvāpi vasamātyasau |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi vairiṇāstaṃbhanaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
khaṭikayāsu saṃlekhya śilāsaṃpuṭa madhyagaṃ |  
hrīṃkāraṃ garbhamadhye tu sādhyanāmapratiṣṭhitaṃ ||  
  
tatastaṃ veṣṭayet samyak catuṣkoṇaṃ tu lekhayā |  
evaṃ yaṃtraṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ likhitvā yaṃtrakaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
aṃte koṇe tu śūlāni caturdikṣuḥ catuścatuḥ |  
vilikhet pūjayed yaṃtraṃ vidhivat kusumaiḥ śubhaiḥ ||  
  
saṃpuṭe vilikhitvā tu sthāpayed yaṃtrakaṃ śubhe |  
tatkṣaṇājjāyate śatrormukhastaṃbhaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi yaṃtraṃ picchūnamuttamaṃ |  
śatrostaṃbhayate vācaṃ gatiṃ buddhiṃ varānane ||  
  
rocanā bhūrjapatreṇa likhed yaṃtraṃ suśobhanaṃ |  
krokārai puṭitaṃ kāryaṃ akṣaraṃ nāmasaṃbhavaṃ ||  
  
hrīṃkāra puṭitaṃ paścādvitīyamakṣaraṃ punaḥ |  
nāmākṣarāṇi yāvanti tāvat saṃpuṭitāni ca ||  
  
tatastaṃ veṣṭayet sarvaṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ tu lekhayā |  
koṇe koṇe dalaṃ kuryād dirghavījena saṃpuṭaṃ ||  
  
yakāraṃ ca makāraṃ ca rakāraṃ ca tathaiva ca |  
ikāraṃ ca vakāraṃ ca yakāraṃ tadanantaraṃ ||  
  
evaṃ krameṇa saṃyojyamakṣarāṇāṃ tu ṣaṭkakaṃ |  
ukārasvarasaṃyuktaṃ mastakoparibhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
bindunādasamāyuktaṃ vilikheddala madhyataḥ |  
evaṃ tu dale tu saṃlekhya vījaṃ vai surapūjite ||  
  
dalāntarāle saṃlekhyaṃ kroṃkṣaścaiva caturdiśaṃ |  
evaṃ saṃlikhya yaṃtraṃ tu pūjayed rakta candanaiḥ ||  
  
raktapuṣpaistathā vastraiḥ svaraktena ca sundarī |  
yathā śaktyā pradātavyā dakṣiṇāṃ brahmasaṃbhave ||  
  
brāhmaṇān bhojayet paścāt vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kārayet |  
paścādyaṃtraṃ likhanyāsu bhūmimadhye vinikṣipet ||  
  
buddhistaṃbhaṃ gatistaṃbhaṃ vākstaṃbhaṃ ca varānane |  
piśunastatkṣaṇāddevī jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
77b)  
  
śrīdevyuvāca ||  
  
tvaritāṃtāna kīṃ dṛṣṭyā nihataṃ rāvaṇaṃ yuddhiḥ |  
pūjitā rāmacandre sātvaritāṃ tāṃ namāmyahaṃ ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇudevī prayatnena yaṃtraṃ daurbhāgya varddhanaṃ |  
vivāde naranārīnāṃ yena saṃjāyate sadā ||  
  
rocanā kuṃkume naiva bhūrjapatre varānane |  
likhed yaṃtraṃ mahādevī nānā saubhāgyanāśanaṃ ||  
  
kuryāt tīryagānā rekhāḥ pūrva paścima saṃsthitāḥ |  
dīrghā vai koṣṭake kuryādaṣṭasaṃkhyā suci smite ||  
  
tatmadhyoparibhāge ca ekaikaṃ vilikhet kramāt |  
madhye nāsākṣaraṃ devī dvivāraṃ tu punaḥ punaḥ ||  
  
tanmadhye cakrame naiva te naiva vilikhet tataḥ |  
ajite tyuparilekhyaṃ svāhāntaṃ praṇavādikaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ saṃvilikhet yaṃtraṃ gacheccaiva śarittaṭe |  
ubhayo kūlayorgrāhyā mṛttikāmauninā śubhā ||  
  
tayā gaṇapatiṃ kṛtvā yaṃtraṃ tasyodare kṣipet |  
godugdhaiḥ stapanaṃ kuryāt gaṇarājasya sundarī ||  
  
arcayedvividhaiḥ puṣpairmodakairvahubhistataḥ |  
saṃpūjya vālakān bhakṣyairgaṇeśaḥ priyatāmiti ||  
  
evaṃ saṃpūjya deveśaṃ gaṇarājaṃ śucismite |  
śarāvasaṃpuṭe kṣiptvā saṃpuṭoparivinyaset ||  
  
aghoreti amogheti vinyaset saṃpuṭopari |  
bhūmisthaṃ saṃpuṭaṃ kuryānnikhanyātha prapūjayet ||  
  
daurbhāgyamatulaṃ prāpya nārīsīdatyaharniśaṃ |  
puruṣeṇa sahaitāṃtu surūpāmapi suvrate ||  
  
puṃliṃge yojitaṃ yaṃtraṃ nārī na sahate bhujā |  
daṃpatyordveṣaṇaṃ devī rahasyaṃ paramaṃ sadā ||  
  
nānyatra saṃprayoktavyaṃ yaṃtrametanmama priye |  
na deyaṃ yasya kasyāpi viparitaṃ prajāyate ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi śatru vidviṣaṇaṃ paraṃ |  
paraspara mahādveṣaṃ śatrūṇāṃ jāyate paraṃ ||  
  
vidveṣite na yuktena lekhanyā kākapicchayā |  
śmaśāna karpaṭe lekhyaṃ caturdaśyāṃ varānane ||  
  
78a)  
  
hrīṃkāraṃ ca akāraṃ ca biṃduyuktaṃ tataḥ paraṃ |  
hrīṃkāraṃ ca tṛtīyaṃ ca ekapaktau likhet tataḥ ||  
  
adhaḥ paṃktau tato nāma caturdalaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
caturdalaṃ tataḥ kuryāt dveṣo dvitaya bhūṣitāṃ ||  
  
daramadhye tathā lekhyaṃ madhyadeśe tathaiva tu |  
ajāraktena saṃmiśraṃ raktaṃ naivedyakaṃ bhavet ||  
  
valipuṣpaiḥ prapūjyātha yaṃtraṃ rātrau varānane |  
yoginīṃ bhojayeccaikāṃ guruṃ saṃpūjya yatnataḥ ||  
  
udveṣe śivagehe ca sthāpyaṃ yaṃtra na saṃśayaḥ |  
śmaśānepyathavā sthāpyaṃ gṛhe na kadācana ||  
  
śatrūṇāṃ jāyate dveṣaṃ kramenaiva na saṃśayaḥ |  
sarvaśatruṃ saṃdveṣaṃ na nāma yaṃtrarājaṃ mahāphalaṃ ||  
  
ekānte karaṇāyaṃ vilokāntena kadācana |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣāmi vandhuvidveṣaṇaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
śmaśāna karpaṭe lekhyaṃ lekkhanyā kākapicchayā |  
meṣasvarūdhire naiva ghṛṣṭāṃgāraṃ smaśānajaṃ ||  
  
sādhyanāmalikhitvā tu trikoṇaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
adhopari ca rephorddhaṃ saṃlekhyaṃ bhūtarātriṣu ||  
  
tatastaṃ veṣṭayet samyak catuṣkoṇaṃ tu rekhayā |  
koṇe koṇe triśūlānāṃ saṃlekhyaṃ ca catuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
caturdikṣu samaṃ lekhyaṃ caturlekhyoparisthitaḥ |  
evaṃ saṃlikhayedyaṃtraṃ saṃpūjya pūrvavat punaḥ ||  
  
saptāṅgulirlikhanyātha pūrayedbhūmi madhyataḥ |  
yātrāsu teṣāṃ mārge ca tatraiva prakṣipet tataḥ ||  
  
parasparaṃ mahādveṣo vandhunāṃ saṃprajāyate |  
yasya pāde patatyeva sāpi daurbhāgya bhājanaḥ ||  
  
jāyate nātra saṃdeho yaṃtrarāja prabhāvataḥ |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣāmi vidveṣaṃ svānibhṛtyajaṃ ||  
  
viṣeṇa raktamiśreṇa lekhanyā kāpi kacchayā |  
śmaśane karpaṭe lekhyaṃ caturdaśyāṃ mahāniśi ||  
  
sādhyanāmalikhedgarbhaṃ vartulaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
  
78b)  
  
tasyopari adhobhāge rakāratritayaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
yakāraṃ purato lekhyaṃ tīryagbhāgye dvivījakaṃ |  
yakāraṃ ca rakāraṃ ca visargāntaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ saṃlikhya yaṃtraṃ ca vartulaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
evaṃ yaṃtraṃ tu saṃlekhyaṃ teṣāṃ mārge nikhanya tu ||  
  
sa jāyate mahādveṣaḥ svāmi sevaka yoḥ sadā |  
yāvat yaṃtraṃ tu bhūmisthaṃ dvaya dveṣaḥ pravarttate ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi jagadveṣakaraṃ paraṃ |  
yaṃtraṃ bhayānakaṃ nāma daurbhāgyasya vivarddhanaṃ ||  
  
kākolūkasya raktena riśabhuraktena vā punaḥ |  
daurbhāgya lekhanāthaśca lekhanyā kākapicchayā ||  
  
vilekhedbhūrjapatre tu sādhyanāma niśi priye |  
kṛṣṇāṣṭamyā caturdaśyāṃ likhedyaṃtraṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
sādhyanāma likhenmadhye ṭhakāra pariveṣṭitaṃ |  
ṭhakārāṇāṃ ca saṃkhyāstri viṣamaṃ veṣṭayet sadā ||  
  
tatastu vartulaṃ veṣṭya durbhagāṣma? veṣṭayet |  
etadyaṃtraṃ susaṃsthāpya bhūmau vā tṛṇa madhyataḥ ||  
  
yāvad gṛhe hi tad yaṃtre sopi tadgṛhagaḥ sadā |  
tāvadvisvaśya śatruḥ saṃjāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
pūjākramastu pūrvoktāṃ yaṃtra devī nṛṇāṃ sadā |  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi yaṃtraṃ śatru sumāraṇaṃ |  
etadyaṃtraṃ susaṃlekhya kapāle tu narasya ca ||  
  
śmaśānaṅgārakaṃ ghṛcchā dhatūrakarasena tu |  
śmaśāne caiva saṃlekhya sādhakaḥ sthiramānasaḥ ||  
  
trikoṇaṃ veṣṭayet paścādraṣādvitaya śobhitaṃ |  
ūrdhvarekhā tu kartavyā sarvatrāpi varānane ||  
  
sarāva saṃpuṭe kṣiptvā yaṃtraṃ taṃ saṃprapūjayet |  
valimāṃsaṃ toya hāraistu svaraktena viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
etadyaṃtraṃ tu tatraiva nikhanyādyatra prapūjayet |  
krameṇaiva mahāvyādhistato vai maraṇa bhajet ||  
  
ekajīvaṃ valiṃ datvā uddhṛte jīvate hi saḥ |  
nocaidyamapuraṃ yāti nātra kāryā vicāraṇāt ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
79a)  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi yaṃtraṃ śatrupranāśanaṃ |  
māraṇaṃ pravalasyāpi śatrormṛtyurna cānyathā ||  
  
viṣeṇa haritālena bhūrjapatre likhennaraḥ |  
sādhyanāmalikhitvā tu lekhanyā kākapīcchayā ||  
  
lekhane vidhirekaiva pūrvoktamāraṇe hitā |  
vāraṃ vāraṃ kimuktena graṃthavistārakāraṇaṃ ||  
  
hrī&kāraṃ garbhamadhye tu sādhyanāma pratiṣṭhitaṃ |  
tatastaṃ veṣṭayet samyak trikoṇaṃ pūrvavattriyā ||  
  
koṇe koṇe triśūlena vilikhyātha prapūjayet |  
pūjane vidhiryaḥ proktaḥ sarvatrāpi ca māraṇe ||  
  
manuṣyāṅghri nali madhye kṣiped yaṃtraṃ supūjitaṃ |  
kṣiptvā śmaśāna bhūmisthāṃ nalikāṃ tu sayaṃtrikāṃ ||  
  
akasmāt maraṇaṃ tasya jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ |  
anugrahaṃ pūrvoktaḥ sarvatrāpi ca māraṇe ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi māraṇaṃ dūradeśajaṃ |  
śmaśānāṃgārakaṃ ghṛṣṭā ajāraktaṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
viṣaṃ caiva tu saṃghṛṣya kṣipennara kapālake |  
saṃpuṭe caiva saṃlekhya lekhanyā kākapicchayā ||  
  
sādhanāmalikhenmadhye hu&kāra puṭitaṃ śubhaṃ |  
tataścāṣṭadalaṃ kuryād gṛhe saṃsthāpayed yathā ||  
  
caturdiśaṃ tu saṃlekhya hu& phaṭ dalamadhyataḥ |  
tatastadveṣṭayet samyak vartulaṃ vai dvirekhayā ||  
  
hu&kārairveṣṭayet paścād viṣakteḥ sarvataḥ priye |  
tatastaṃ saṃpuṭaṃ mele bhasmanā pūrayecchubhe ||  
  
agre rūpari saṃsthāpyaṃ pūrayitvā yathoditaṃ |  
deśāntara gatasyāpi śatroḥ saṃjāyate jvare ||  
  
pratyahaṃ jvalanīye tu stokaṃ stokaṃ tu sundarī |  
dine ekānta viṃśat ca sarvatra jvalayen niśi ||  
  
tasmiṃneva kṣaṇe śatrurmaraṇaṃ jāyate priye |  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi māraṇaṃ sarvadehināṃ |  
rudhireṇa manuṣyasya śmaśānāṃgāra vṛkṣayet ||  
  
viṣeṇa ca tathā lekhyaṃ karpaṭe vai śmaśānaje |  
sādhyanāmalikhitvā tu hu& phaṭ dyutitayaṃ tathā ||  
  
79b)  
  
evaṃ trivāraṃ saṃlikhya tripaṃktau tu varānane |  
tatasvadveṣṭayet samyak vartulaṃ tu trirekhayā ||  
  
rājikā pratimāṃ kuryāt śatroścaraṇapāṃśunā |  
hṛtmadhye yaṃtrakaṃ kṣiptvā śanaistāpya tu puta?līṃ ||  
  
śatroḥ kramakrameṇaiva dāhaṃ śokaṃ ca jāyate |  
śiro yathā ca mahati tṛtīyehni prajāyate ||  
  
hastapādāṃ gadāhaḥ syāt maraṇaṃ saptame dine |  
jāyate nātra saṃdeho vimukto na ca saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi māraṇaṃ sarvadehināṃ |  
  
yaṃtraṃ strīpuruṣasya ca |  
  
vibhītakasya tu patre tu śmaśānabhasmanā likhet ||  
  
ṛturaktaṃ tu saṃmilya lekhanyā kākapicchayā |  
sādhyanāmalikhenmadhye stambhe sābhani saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
tatastrikoṇaṃ saṃveṣṭya paṃcakoṇaṃ tathopari |  
manuṣyaṃ narake kṣiptvā naraṃ saṃpūjya sūtrayā ||  
  
tatsūtra śaktyā yā devī tatastatpūjyapūrayet |  
bhūmadhye'tha nikhanyātha śmaśānetha yato niśi ||  
  
tataḥ saṃyatanāt paścāt śatruḥ mitrasya vīkṣaṇāt |  
mriyate saptarātreṇa mokṣa pūrvokta eva hi ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi śatrohamuccāṭanaṃ paraṃ |  
anāmāraktasaṃlekhya bhūrjapatre varānane ||  
  
gaṇapati vijāniyā prahitaṃ praṇavādikaṃ |  
ekapaṃktau samālekhya huṃgaṃ ca nāmameva ca ||  
  
paṃktau dvitīya saṃlekhyaṃ tṛtīya vilikhet tataḥ |  
hu&gaṃdhaḥ svāheti likhitvā kramaso naraḥ ||  
  
tatastadveṣṭayet saṃyak catuḥkoṇaṃ dvirekhayā |  
raktāmbaradharo devī raktagandhā tu lepanaḥ ||  
  
caturdaśyāṃ sādhakastu mahārātrau likhet kramāt |  
pujanaṃ raktakusumaiḥ raktagandhaiḥ phalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ||  
  
kumārī bhojanaṃ rātrau yathā śaktyā tu dakṣiṇā |  
dhyānastu deva devasya gaṇanāthasya sundarī ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi sadya uccāṭanaṃ paraṃ |  
  
80a)  
  
viṣeṇatālake naiva likhet kākaṃ tu pannake ||  
  
śmaśānajeṃ tu lekhanyā kapiccha samudbhavā |  
sādhyanāmalikhet paścād vāyasodara madhyataḥ ||  
  
pūjane lekhane caiva pūrvoktastu vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |  
adhomukhaṃ tu taṃkākaṃ lavamātraṃ tu dakṣiṇe ||  
  
vibhītakasya dakṣeṣu vandhayet prayato niśi |  
evaṃ kṛte tṛttīye hrīṃ sthānāduccāṭanaṃ bhavet ||  
  
yādayaṃtraṃ tu tatrasthamudvignastāvaṃ deva hi |  
naro ca na gṛhe tasya sukhaṃ na labhate kvacit ||  
  
videśagamanaṃ tasya saṃśayena ca jivītaṃ |  
  
śrībhairava uvāca |  
  
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi uccāṭanaṃ sarva dehināṃ |  
kākolūkasya raktena bhūrjapatre likhennaraḥ ||  
  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu vartulaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
caturdalaṃ tataḥ kuryāt drekhatritaya śobhitaṃ ||  
  
yakārodara madhye tu viśargāṃtaṃ pratiṣṭitaṃ |  
pūjākramaṃ tu pūrvoktaṃ dhyānādeva vivarjitaṃ ||  
  
khaṇḍaṃ kṛtvā tu tadyaṃtramucchiṣṭodana miśritaṃ |  
dīyate bhakṣaṇārthaṃ ca vāyase dhyo dine dine ||  
  
deśaṃ saṃtyajya yātyeva grāmañcaiva tu kākathā |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi yaṃtramuccāṭanaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
nimbapatrarasairlekhyaṃ lekhanyā kākapicchayā |  
bhūrjapatro parikṣiptaṃ vidhiḥ pūrvokta eva hi ||  
  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu vartulaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
caturdalaṃ tataḥ kuryāt vījayuktaṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
ravauha iti vījāni dalamadhye pṛthak pṛthak |  
saṃpūjya pūrvavat paścān nikhanyātha prapūjayet ||  
  
adhomukhaṃ tu tadyaṃtraṃ pūrvokta vidhinā tataḥ |  
evaṃ kṛte saptamehni uccāṭayati nānyathā ||  
  
bhrāmyadeśaṃ videśaṃ ca tṛṇavat parībhūyate |  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devī pravakṣyāmi yaṃtramuccāṭanaṃstriyaḥ |  
  
80b)  
  
gardabhasya tu raktena lekhanyākākapicchayā ||  
  
phalake ca likhitvā tu vartulaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
tataścāṣṭadalaṃ kāryaṃ vījayuktaṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
khakāraṃ tu viśargāntaṃ hrī&kāraṃ tadanantaraṃ |  
evaṃ yaṃtraṃ susaṃlekhya pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ ||   
  
nikhanya bhūmau saṃpūrya pūrvavaccāpyadhomukhaṃ |  
uccāṭayati sthānāt tu calate vāyu parṇavat ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devī pravakṣyāmi trailokyoccāṭanaṃ paraṃ |  
kṛṣṇakukkuṭa raktena bhūrjapatre likhennaraḥ ||  
  
sādhyanāmalikhitvā tu trikoṇaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
punastrikoṇaṃ saṃlikhya dvitīyantu varānane ||  
  
tatopari vibhāge ca hrīṃkārāṇāṃ catuṣṭayaṃ |  
etadvibhāgaṃ saṃlikhya vījānāṃ ravisaṃkhyayā ||  
  
tato vartulaṃ saṃlekhya pūjayet pūrvavat punaḥ |  
evaṃ kṛtvā tu tadyaṃtraṃ vadhnīyācca suto gale ||  
  
yathā saṃkhyāśca varjita tathā loke kṣaṇāta hi |  
uccāṭayenna saṃdehastatkṣaṇāt surasandarī ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi yaṃtra uccāṭanaṃ paraṃ |  
niśācara rasairlekhyaṃ bhūrjapatre na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
sādhyanāmalikhitvā tu vartulaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
tasyāścāṣṭadalaṃ kṛtvā vījayuktaṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
tataśca lekhyaṃ phaṭ iti pratyekaṃ dalamadhyataḥ |  
tatastaṃ veṣṭayet samyak vartulaṃ lekhayaikayā ||  
  
saṃpūjya vidhivat paścād yaṃtraṃ saṃcūrṇayet tataḥ |  
khāne pāne pradātavyamuccāṭo jāyate dhruvaṃ ||  
  
yaḥ pūrvaṃ jānakādeśā daraṇyaṃ samapadyataḥ |  
nistīrya prāptavān śītāṃtaṃ rāmaṃ praṇatosmyahaṃ ||  
  
adhikāramahaṃ vakṣye sarvopadravanāśanaṃ |  
saptamyāṃ pīṭhikāyāṃ tu śānti puṣṭikaraṃ sukhaṃ ||  
  
śāntirakṣākaraṃ nāmā khyātaṃ sarvatra durlabhaṃ |  
na deyaṃ yasya kasyāpi yadicchet siddhimātmanaḥ ||  
  
śṛṇu devī paraṃ guhyaṃ yaṃtraṃ rakṣākaraṃ paraṃ |  
  
81a)  
  
vālastrī puruṣāṇāṃ ca mahārakṣākaraṃ smṛtaṃ ||  
  
kāṃśya pātretha yaṃ lekhyaṃ sutithau śobhane dine |  
rocanā kuṃkume naiva karpūreṇa viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
mṛganābhi samāyuktairjāti kāṣṭhairlikhennaraḥ |  
ūrdhvaṃ aṣṭau rekhāsti yatra sthitāścatācasi ||  
  
evaṃ bhavaṃti cet koṣṭhā ekona paktyā tu saṃjñakāḥ |  
akārādi svarālekhyā upalikhya tathaiva ca ||  
  
vyaṃjanāḥ kramato lekhyā te naiva kramataḥ kramāt |  
evaṃ saṃlikhya vījāni triśūlāni likhet tataḥ ||  
  
pratirekho pare nūnaṃ caturdikṣu kramāllikhet |  
kroṃkārāḥ ṣaṭdyaṃ lekhyāḥ pūrve caiva tu paścime ||  
  
evaṃ saṃlikhya tadyaṃtraṃ pūjayedbhaktibhāvataḥ |  
puṇḍarīkairśitāṃ bhojaiḥ śatapatrairmanoramaiḥ ||  
  
mālatī yūthikābhiśca ketakairmallikaistathā |  
vakulaiśca yathā lābhaṃ phalakeyai phalodbhavaiḥ ||  
  
nirgandhaṃ raktavarṇe tu puṣpaṃ yatnena varjayet |  
sa karpūraiśca tāṃvulairdhūpairgandhaiḥ śitotparaiḥ ||  
  
evaṃ dina trayaṃ pūjya naivedyairvividhaiḥ priye |  
japet saptaśati nityaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ tu dinatrayaṃ ||  
  
saṃbhojya pāyase naiva yatheṣṭhena ghṛtena tu |  
tridinaṃ bhūmisāyi syāt bhojanādgandhalepanāt ||  
  
uddhṛtya guṭikāṃ kṛtvā trilohairveṣṭayet tataḥ |  
taccheṣaṃ caiva pāṇiyaṃ pāṇiṃścaiva varānane ||  
  
vālasya jāyate kṣobho vidyayā vai niyojitaḥ |  
guṭikāṃ dhārayed devī vāhumūle galethavā ||  
  
dhāraṇāt tasya yaṃtrasya upasargaḥ praṇasyati |  
alakṣmīḥ kalahaścaiva daurbhāgyaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
yatpareṇa kṛtaṃ kiṃcit tatsarvaṃ vipraṇaśyati |  
śāntikaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ nāma devānāmapi durlabhaṃ ||  
  
prathamaṃ yaṃtrarājākhyaṃ sarvapratyayakārakaṃ |  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
śṛṇu devī pravakṣyāmi yaṃtraṃ cauranivāraṇaṃ |  
sarpavyāghrabhayaṃ nāsti yaṃtre karatale sthite ||  
  
81b)  
  
lekhanavidhiḥ pūrvokto dravyaṃ pūrvoktameva hi |  
sarvatra śāṃtike devī vidhiranyāna vidyate ||  
  
pūjanaṃ caiva pūrvoktaṃ nijamasyāpi tādṛśaḥ |  
bhūrjapatre tu saṃlekhya dvitīyaṃ yaṃtramuttamaṃ ||  
  
hrī&kāraṃ garbhamadhye tu sādhyanāma pratiṣṭhitaṃ |  
tasyā devi tu saṃyojyamakāraṃ tadanantaraṃ ||  
  
lakāraṃ ca yakāraṃ ca yakāraṃ ca pratiṣṭhitaṃ |  
ūkāraṃ svarasaṃyuktaṃ śānti vīja manoharaṃ ||  
  
tatastaṃ veṣṭaye samyak catukoṇaṃ dvirekhayā |  
triloha veṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā vāhumūle galetha vā ||  
  
sarpavyāghrabhayaṃ hanti caurabhayaṃ haraṃ tathā |  
vividhoya dravaṃ haṃti nātra kāryā vicāraṇāt ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca |  
  
śṛṇu devī pravakṣyāmi yaṃtraṃ daurbhāgya nāśanaṃ |  
nārīṇāṃ ca viśeṣeṇa narānāṃ caiva sarvadā ||  
  
lekhane vidhiḥ pūrvokto dravyaṃ pūrvoktameva ca |  
lekhanī pūrvamuddiṣṭā bhūrjapatre likhennaraḥ ||  
  
sādhyanāmalikhitvā tu trikoṇaṃ tu dvirekhayā |  
tasyopari catuṣkoṇaṃ rekhādhi traya śobhitaṃ ||  
  
koṇe koṇe triśūlantu pūrvokta vidhinā tataḥ |  
trilohaveṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā vāhu mūle galetha vā ||  
  
dhārayed vidhi pūrvantu nārī vā puruṣotha vā |  
vividhopadravaṃ haṃti tasyāgarbhaṃ ca dhārayet ||  
  
saubhāgyamatulaṃ poṣyaṃ devavatmodate sadā ||  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi jvaravināśanaṃ paraṃ |  
bhūtajaṃ tu jvaraṃ hanti vidyate vaidikoditaṃ ||  
  
kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ pūrvavannikhanet tataḥ |  
śmaśāne tu divaiva syānnirāhārena mānavaḥ ||  
  
catuṣkoṇo parilekhet koṇabhavamaṣṭadalaṃ yathā |  
madhye nāmalikhitvāt narakārasya tu saṃpuṭaṃ ||  
  
dalamadhyeṃtarāle tu rakāraṃ saṃpratiṣṭhitaṃ |  
evaṃ viṃśanti? rephāḥ syuḥ sarvataṃtra krameṇa tu ||  
  
saṃpūjya bhūme saṃpūjā valipuṣpairmanoharaiḥ |  
tatkṣaṇādyāti tadbhūta jvararūpaṃ ca dāruṇaṃ ||  
  
82a)  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi vālānāṃ śāntikārakaṃ |  
yaṃtraṃ rakṣākaraṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sarvopadravanāśanaṃ ||  
  
pūrvokta vidhinā lekhyaṃ dravyairpūrvoditaiḥ kramāt |  
bhūrjapatro paridevī pūrvoktavidhinārcanaṃ ||  
  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu vartulaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
tataścāṣṭadalaṃ kāryaṃ vījayuktaṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
sakārānta visagāṃtāḥ? dale pratyekasau nyaset |  
saṃpūjyavidhivat paścād vāhu mūle galetha vā ||  
  
dhārayed yaṃtraṃ jatunā lohatritaya veṣṭitaṃ |  
śākinyo cātha ḍākinyo vālagrahāstathā pare ||  
  
gachanti vālakaṃ muktvā yaṃtra rājasya dhāraṇāt |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi tṛtīyaṃ jvaranāśanaṃ ||  
  
pūrvokta vidhinā lekhyaṃ bhūrjapatre suśobhane |  
sādhyanāma likitvā tu yakārasya tu saṃpuṭaṃ ||  
  
trikoṇaṃ veṣṭayitvā tu nyased vījānī coparī |  
evaṃ saṃlikhya saṃpūjya vadhnīyādṛkṣi kare ||  
  
jvaravālesu kāryeṣu valyārthe dadhi bhaktikaṃ |  
vālovāpyathavā vṛddho jvarān mucyeta tatkṣaṇāt ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi vālajvaravināśanaṃ |  
pūjayitvā vidhānena sarvajvaranivāraṇaṃ ||  
  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu vartulaṃ veṣṭayet tataḥ |  
ūrdhvaṃ yonya gataḥ pṛṣṭhe vakārasya tu saṃpuṭe ||  
  
tataścāṣṭadalaṃ kāryaṃ vījaṃ yuktaṃ tu sarvataḥ |  
pratyekaṃ dalamadhye tu nakāraṃ vindubhūṣitaṃ ||  
  
dalākare tu hrī&kārāṃ * * * * *?  vinyaset |  
evaṃ saṃlikhya saṃpūjya sīta toye vinikṣipet ||  
  
mucyate tridinād yogni jvarād dvadvānnasaṃśayaḥ |  
uṣṇodakena saṃkṣipta saṃkṣiptaṃ jvaraṃ naśyati ||  
  
hastamūle tu tadvaddhaṃ jvaraḥ velāsamudbhavaṃ |  
nāśayen nātra saṃdeho bhūtayaṃtraṃ surasundarī ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi vālānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ sadā |  
yaṃtraṃ jvaraṇarakṣākhyaṃ āyurvṛddhikaraṃ paraṃ ||  
  
82b)  
  
pūrvoktaḥ vidhinā lekhyaṃ dravyaiḥ pūrvoditaiḥ śubhaiḥ |  
bhūrjapatre tu saṃlekhya sādhyanāma tu madhyataḥ ||  
  
tatastaṃ veṣṭayet samyak catuṣkoṇaṃ tu lekhayā |  
tasyopari catuṣkoṇaṃ triśūlau koṇato likhet ||  
  
koṇāntare likhed vījaṃ vakāraṃ bindubhūṣitaṃ |  
uparyaḥ tarale tu hrī&kāraṃ vilikhedbudhaḥ ||  
  
evaṃ saṃlekhya tadyaṃtraṃ pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ |  
trilohaveṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā vadhnīyāt kaṃṭhamadhyataḥ ||  
  
tayopasargā ye kecid yogāḥ śarīramānasāḥ |  
īrṣyā kopastathā rekhā dantanā saṃbhavet punaḥ ||  
  
na vādhate vālakasya stanyadoṣaṃ kadācana |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi bhūtā pasmāra nāśanaṃ ||  
  
śākinī bhūtavetālairgṛhīto vāpi vāruṇaiḥ |  
tadāta mocanārthāya kuryādyaṃtraṃ manoharaṃ ||  
  
svasthasya tu prakurvīt śatrudoṣairna gṛhyate |  
dravyaiḥ pūrvoditairlekhyaṃ pūrvokta vidhinā tataḥ ||  
  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu bhūrjapatre varānane |  
vartulaṃ veṣṭayet saṃlekhyaṃ tasyopari valāṣṭakaṃ ||  
  
hrī&kāraṃ garbhamadhye tu pratyekaṃ vilikhet punaḥ |  
evaṃ saṃlikhya saṃpūjya lohatritaya veṣṭitaṃ ||  
  
suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ trilohaṃ paricakṣate |  
vālānāṃgalake dhāryaṃ yaṃtraṃ tripurabhairavaṃ ||  
  
mucyate vālako rogairapasmārādvarānane |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi sarpāsaṃrakṣaṇaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
sarpādibhiryathā vālaḥ prauḍho vāpi viśeṣataḥ |  
na daśyaṃte yathā devī pramādādaghriyati te ||?  
  
pūrvoktavidhinā lekhya pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ |  
madhye nāma likhitvā tu vartulaṃ tu dvirekhayā ||  
  
saṃveṣṭya ca dalānyaṣṭau haṃsavīja yutāḥ pṛthak |  
trilohairveṣṭayitvā tu vāhumūle tu dhārayet ||  
  
naśyaṃti darśanāt tasya daṃdaśūkāścaturdiśaḥ |  
pramādāt patitāḥ pāde tiṣṭhaṃti staṃbhitā iva ||  
  
atha daṃṣṭaḥ pramādena viṣaṃnaivādhirohateḥ |  
  
83a)  
  
sarpānāṃ staṃbhanārthāya yaṃtraṃ garuḍabhāṣitaṃ ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi ḍākinī trāśanaṃ paraṃ |  
bhūtapretapiśācādyai ḍākinī brahmarākṣasaiḥ ||  
  
yadā śatrurnaraḥ kopi nārī vā vīrakopi vā |  
tadā yaṃtraṃ prakurvīta nāśārthaṃ bhūtarākṣasāṃ ||  
  
khaṭikayā likhitvā tu karpaṭe tu stāne? śubhe |  
tīryagrekhā caturastu adhastāt paṃktirekhayā ||  
  
evaṃ bhavāṃ kāṃti koṣṭhā dvādaśaiva varānane |  
hrī&kāraṃ pratikoṣṭhe tu vilikhya tu prapūjayet ||  
  
valipuṣpopahāraiśca tato dhūlyāḥ prapūrayet |  
saṃsthāpyāgrai cārūpāṇi jvalayet khadirā nale ||  
  
rudantaṃ ca mahābhūtaṃ copamānaṃ palāyate |  
tatkṣaṇādvālakaṃ muktvā deśatyāgena gacchati ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi jvaravināśanaṃ paraṃ |  
tāmbūlapatre saṃlekhyaṃ caṃculasyeta kaṃṭhakaiḥ ||  
  
sādhyanāmalikhitvā tu kroṃkāra puṭitaṃ śubhaṃ |  
ṣatkoṇasya tu madhye tu koṇeṣu praṇavanyasyet ||  
  
koṇopari tu hrī&kāraṃ sarvato vilikhet kramāt |  
tāmvulaṃ bhakṣaṇārthaṃ ca pūjayitvā pradīyate ||  
  
yaṃtrasya bhakṣaṇāddevī jvaro yānti na śaṃsayaḥ |  
ekāntaraḥ kṣaṇādeva nātrakāryāvicāraṇā ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi garbharakṣākaraṃ paraṃ |  
gajamaddena saṃlekhyaṃ bhūrjapatre suśobhane ||  
  
gajasya tu madābhāvāt kaṃṭhoṣṭhaṃ sarvataḥ kṣipet |  
madhye nāma likhitvā tu catuṣkoṇaṃ dvirekhayā ||  
  
saṃveṣṭyakarṇikāḥ kāryā vartulāttu caturdiśaṃ |  
yakāraṃ ca rakāraṃ ca visargāntaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ||  
  
karṇikā madhyato lekhyaṃ pūrvavat pūjayet kramāt |  
lohaikena tu saṃveṣṭya garbhinyāḥ kaṇṭhato nyaset ||  
  
sukhātyu sūtirbhavati chalachidraṃ ca naśyati |  
  
83b)  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi antarvatnī surakṣaṇaṃ |  
yaṃtraṃ yoni yathā yāti cāraṇaṃ bhūtanāśanaṃ ||  
  
pūrvokta vidhinā lekhyaṃ dravyaiḥ pūrvoditaiḥ kramāt |  
bhūrjapatre vidhānaṃ ca madhyadeśe vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
praṇavaṃ ca yathā hrī& ca ādyaṃtaṃ nāmato likhet |  
vartulaṃ ca catuṣkoṇaṃ dīrghaṃ saṃveṣṭya lekhayā ||  
  
uparyadhopi tridalātkoṇekaika pratiṣṭhitaṃ |  
hrī& kṣaṃ ca tathā hrī& ca koṇe dala gataṃ likhet ||  
  
evaṃ saṃlikhitaṃ yaṃtraṃ sarvakāryena saṃśaya |  
yoniśūlaṃ śīraḥ śūlaṃ bhūtadoṣaṃ pranaśyati ||  
  
sukhaṃ prasūtirbhavati vyathā varjena saṃśayaḥ |  
rahasyeyaṃ samākhyātaṃ yaṃtrarājaṃ mahadbhūtaṃ ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi tṛtīyaṃ jvaranāśanaṃ |  
dravyaiḥ pūrvoditairlekhyaṃ bhūrjapatre varānane ||  
  
madhye nāmalikhitvā tu trikoṇaṃ veṣṭayet punaḥ |  
catuṣkoṇaṃ śikharākāraṃ tasyoparilikhedbudhaiḥ ||  
  
yakāraiḥ sa viśargāntairviṣamairveṣṭayet tataḥ |  
saṃpūjya tasya velāyāṃ vadhnīyāddakṣiṇe kare ||  
  
jvaro yāti na saṃdeho bhūtajastu tṛtīyakaḥ |  
rogayonaivasamāyātyeva vanaṃ yojyaṃta caikadā ||  
  
iti te kathitaṃ devī yaṃtrasādhanamuttamaṃ |  
samāsena mahādevī indrajālamataḥ śṛṇu ||  
  
  
iti śrīhāhārāvataṃtre atharvasaṃhitāyāṃ yaṃtrasādhano nāma paṭalaḥ ||  
  
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi senāstambhanamuttamaṃ |  
bherīmṛdaṃgapaṭahastaṃbhaṃ nānāṃ ca lakṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
śilāyāṃnvitamekhyātaṃ tapanāyat svayaṃbhuvā |  
anurādhā tripuṣyārdrānnatitrayajayāsu? ca ||  
  
ravivindu? śukracandrādervāsare śukrapakṣake |  
dhanatrikona kendrasthāḥ śubhāḥ pāpābhavatrigāḥ ||  
  
bherīmṛdangapaṭaha tāḍiteṣu ca karmayet |  
  
84a)  
  
susuddhe nāyase lagne karmakārī vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
yatkuryāt sadṛḍhaṃ vṛttaṃ nirmalaṃ jayavardhanaṃ |  
gavāgnirāmaniśithe muktakeśi ca lagnataḥ ||  
  
pārodivī diśaṃ gatvā carmakāri purādvahiḥ |  
samyak carmāvavaddha kuryāt sūrya svarodaye ||  
  
taṃ maṃdadhvani nādena paraṃ śatru palāyanaṃ |  
raktadhattūramūlaṃ vā kaṃdaṃ vālāgalo bhavaṃ ||  
  
kadalīkaṃdasaṃyukta citi bhasma ca peśayet |  
savītamarkaṭī padmaṃ madalagnāmamadhyagā ||  
  
kuryāddīrgha praṇādaṃ tu śrutvā senāpalāyate |  
lāṃgalī gṛhagodhā ca vātāli yātanaṃ śivaṃ ||  
  
cūrṇayet sarṣapaiḥ sārdhaṃ svagātraṃ tena lepayet |  
taṃ dṛṣṭvā dharaṇīśa araṇyamānaṃ parasparaṃ ||  
  
iti para senāstambhanaṃ ||  
  
atha khaḍgastambhanaṃ ||  
  
ketakī mastake netre tāluyūle mukhe kṣipet |  
khaḍgena caraṇe hṛcche khaḍgastaṃbha prajāyate ||  
  
etāni triṇimūlāni cūrṇitāni ghṛtaiḥ pibet |  
ahorātrau tataḥ śastrairyāvajjīvaṃ na vādhyate ||  
  
śirīṣamūlaṃ puṣpārkaṃ grāhayet peṣayejjalaiḥ |  
arddhāhāroddhṛtaṃ paścājjalaṃ cārdhake pibet ||  
  
yāvaddhitāni tatpātaṃ tāvadvastrairna vādhate |  
tanmūlaṃ ca gale vaddhvā khaḍgairmeṣairna vādhate ||  
  
puṃkhīpuṣpoddhṛtaṃ sūtraṃ varadāyodare kṣipet |  
ṭaṃvarāṭaṃ karaṃ yasya phalaṃ madhye vinikṣipet ||  
  
tatphalaṃ mukhamadhyasthaṃ śastrastaṃbhanakaṃ paraṃ |  
graste ravau samuddhṛtya śarapuṃkhī samanvitaṃ ||  
  
vaktreyo dhārayenmaunī na sa khaḍgena bhidyate |  
samūlapatraṃ śākhāntu viṣṇukrāṃtāṃ prapūrṇayet ||  
  
tailapakvaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā tenāṃgāni vimardayet |  
khaḍgādi sarvaśastrāṇāṃ bhavedyuddhe nivāraṇaṃ ||  
  
vajramātrakakaṃ tāpyaṃ kāṃtabhasmasamanvitaṃ |  
madyaṃjaṃ vīrajairdrāvaiḥ saptakhaḍge tataḥ punaḥ ||  
  
84b)  
  
brahmavṛkṣasya vījāni karmamātrānirājikāṃ |  
vadhyā vayaṃ ca viṃvāṃ ca piṣṭvātaṃ maṃgalaṃ kuru ||  
  
pūrvaṃ yanmarditagolaṃ laghumattapuṭaiḥ pacet |  
taddhauraṃ dhārayedvaktre śastrastaṃbhakaraṃ paraṃ ||  
  
sarveṣāmuktayogānāṃ kumbhakarṇaṃ smareddhṛdi |  
āyudhaṃ saṃmukhaṃ śastraṃ samurddha ca nivārayet ||  
  
oṃ ahokuṃbhakarṇa mahārākṣasakaikasi garbhasaṃbhūta parasainya   
bhaṃjanaparasainya bhaṃjana mahāsacān rudrośāpayati svāhā ||  
  
sarvayogānā anena maṃtreṇa aṣṭottara sahasre japte siddhiḥ |  
atra sarvoṣadhayaḥ uttarābhimukhaḥ samutpāṭayet? ||  
  
iti khaḍga staṃbhanaṃ ||  
  
athāgni staṃbhanaṃ ||  
  
kumāryā kolavṛkṣasya raso meṣavasānvitaḥ |  
liptamātronaṃ? rasyene? vahni madhyena dahyate ||  
  
nalukāpāṭalī mūlaṃ rauvālakusumaṃ samaṃ |  
mandūkavasayā piṣṭvā liptagātro na dahyati ||  
  
śvetaguṃjārasai naiva sarvāṃgalepano na vai |  
aṃgārarāśi madhye tu bhramamāso na dahyati ||  
  
athāgni staṃbhaguṃṭikā ||  
  
vāmapādaṃ vāmahastaṃ kṛkalāsasya pūrvavat |  
saṃgṛhya siddhakai veṣṭaṃ vahnistaṃbho mukhe sthitaṃ ||  
  
pādalepanāgni saṃcaraṇaṃ   
  
udghāṃtapannanirmālyamaipyaṃ? paribhadrakaṃ |  
maṇḍakaṃ vasayā sārddhaṃ pṛṣṭvāmṛdvagnināpacet ||   
  
tena pādapralepana bhramedaṃgāraparvate |   
bhṛṃgarāja kalikaṃrdamaṃḍūka vasayā pacet ||  
  
mṛddhagninā tato lepāt pādayoḥ pādake caret ||  
  
gālūvartitamasṛsājaśaikasāhi? liptaye |  
sparśena kṛti jāyante tuṣārakaraśītalā ||  
  
athānna pākastaṃbhanaṃ   
  
dagdhvādau tulasī kāṣṭhaṃ śālyālyā vātha secayet |  
kharamūle tadaṃgāraṃ jvala cūlyāṃ niveśayet ||  
  
kāṣṭhabhāraśate nāpi annapāko na jāyate |  
  
athāṃgārabhakṣaṇaṃ |  
  
pippalīṃ mariṣṭvaṃ śuṇṭhī pitvā punaḥ punaḥ |   
  
85a)  
  
diptāṃgāraṃ narobhuṅkte na vaktre dahyate kvacit |  
  
atha gṛhadāhastaṃbhanaṃ ||  
  
saptadhā himavan maṃtraṃ japtvā toyena tāḍitaḥ |  
vahniḥ śāmyati raudropi dahyamāne gṛhe sati ||  
  
oṃ himālayasyottare pārśve mārico nāma rākṣasaḥ |  
tasya mantra purīṣābhyāṃ hutāsanaṃ staṃbhayāni svāhā ||  
  
atha saptadīvya staṃbhīni |  
  
śirīṣamūlamādāya ravivāre tu pūrvagaṃ |  
udakenaṃ samaṃghṛṣṭvā lalāṭe tilake kṛte ||  
  
taptadīvyajayo bhavet |  
  
kumārī sūtraṇaṃ piṣṭvā lipta hastakaro bhavet |  
diptāṃgāraistaptalohairmantra yukto na dahyati ||  
  
aṣāḍhe navamaṃḍūkavasayālepayet karau |  
dhārayet tapta lohaṃ tu vahnistaṃbhanamuttamaṃ ||  
  
taptaghṛtastaṃbhanaṃ |  
  
kāminī kuṣumosīśrīkharajalaṭṭihibhadduḥkhasamāsya bhaktaṃ |  
karamūle spṛśati kvāthitaṃ ghṛtatailaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ spṛśanna dahyate ||  
  
tadanu viṣadivyastaṃbhanaṃ |   
  
saṃjātamātrago vatsa viṣṭā grāhyātaro tataḥ |  
  
bhakṣayitvā viṣaṃ khāde dviṣadivya jayo bhavet |  
putraṃ jīvaphalāmajjā niṣkamātre tu bhakṣite ||  
  
prātasūptaviṣaṃ khāde dviṣadivya jayo bhavet |  
  
atha tanduladivyastaṃbhanaṃ ||  
  
maricaṃgadhircetvāṃ carvitvā gilite sati |  
ravi tandulaje divya kṛta doṣopi śuddhyati ||  
  
syādvārāhi śikhi mūlaṃ kṣīreṇa saha pesitaṃ |  
staṃbhayet taṃdulaṃ divyamavarohayavyadyadi ||  
  
athāśanistaṃbhanaṃ ||  
  
ravivāre mṛtā yāsauḥ kīlāstasyāḥ pravadhyate |  
caturdikṣu catuḥkīlān gṛhītvā cihnayet svayaṃ ||  
  
rakṣayet nāt? prayatnena rudramaṃtreṇa maṃtritān |   
caturṇāṃ dāpayeddhaste ye dhāvanti ca vegataḥ ||  
  
aśaniḥ śalabhāmedyāyāṃti varyopalāḥ svayaṃ |  
yāvad gachaṃti te dūraṃ tāvad vādhāna vidyate ||  
  
85b)  
  
gatyante saṃsthite tatra vyāmamātraṃ japet manuṃ |  
kīlakānnikhanet tatra pratyāga sasvamaṃdiraṃ ||  
  
kīlakān prātarādvāya rakṣayet svagṛhaṃ sadā |  
vajrapātena tatrāsti tadgrāme nagarepi vā ||  
  
vaddhaṃ yathā tathā yāvat tāvat kāryaṃ puraśceteḥ |  
  
asya prayogasya maṃtraḥ ||  
  
oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya uḍḍāmare svarāya sarvaduṣṭānme niṣūdayā śaniṃ   
nāśaya bhaṃjaya svāhā | ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ atha jalastaṃbhanaṃ |  
  
rājiraśiraḥ sthitvā tatmaniṃ ca samāharet |  
tadvaktre nikṣipeddhīmān jalastaṃbhanamuttamaṃ ||  
  
trilohaveṣṭitaṃ hṛstaṃ kṛṃkalāśasya dakṣiṇaṃ |  
sa maṃtraṃ dhārayed vaktre svecchayā saṃcarejjale ||  
  
samudrepi na saṃdeho narasto yena vādhyate |  
  
asya prayogasya maṃtraḥ ||  
  
oṃ agnaye udara svāhā |   
  
kṛkalāśasya pittena rocanenāṃ japedvṛśau|  
jālāṃtara sthitaṃ sarvaṃ dṛśyate maṇi śuktikaṃ ||  
  
atha buddhistabhanaṃ ||  
  
bhṛṃgarājāyamārgai ca siddhārthā saha devikā |  
tulyaṃ tulyaṃ vacā śvaitā dravameṣāṃ samāharet ||  
  
lohapātre vinikṣipya dvidināṃte samuddharet |  
tilake sarvaśatrūṇāṃ buddhistaṃbhakaraṃ bhavet ||  
  
triniṣkaṃ mṛtanāgaṃ tu muṃḍaṃ vā kāṃtameva ca |  
pibedārdrastu payasā vacaḥ staṃbhakaraṃ nṛṇāṃ ||  
  
pūrvatrayeṇa yogena jīvedmacaṃdratārakaṃ |  
samyak kāṃsya maye pātre dhātṛ cūrṇaṃ śitāṃvunā ||  
  
rātrau palaikaṃ saṃlehya prātaruthāya bhakṣayet |  
vali palita nirmukto vatsarān mṛtyujīd bhavet ||  
  
brahmavṛkṣasya paṃcāṃgaṃ chāyāśuṣkaṃ sucūrṇitaṃ |  
madhvājyābhyāṃ likhet karṣaṃ kanajalājalet ||  
  
jīvedvarṣasahasraikaṃ divyakāyo mahāvalaḥ |  
brahmavṛkṣasya puṣpāṇi chāyāśuṣkāṇi kārayet ||  
  
triśatpalaṃ tu taccūrṇaṃ caturviṃśat palaṃ ghṛtaṃ |  
ekīkṛtya kṣiped bhāṇḍe taṃ ruddhvāya rāśigaṃ ||  
  
86a)  
  
kṛtvā māsān samuddhṛtya bhāgān kuryāccaturdaśa |  
bhāgaikaṃ bhakṣayennityaṃ bhuṃjiyāt tāmra bhājane ||  
  
evaṃ māsatrayaṃ kuryād vajrakāyo bhaven naraḥ |  
tasya mūtrapurīṣeṇa tāmraṃ bhavati kāṃcanaṃ ||  
  
brahmavṛkṣasya vījāni cūrṇitāni pṛtaiḥ sahaḥ |  
pūrvavaddhānya madhye tu kṣiptvā māsaṃ samuddharet ||  
  
palaikaṃ tu sadā khāde dūnmarān mṛtyujid bhavet |  
valipalitanirmukto jīvedbrahma dina trayaṃ ||  
  
śveta pālāśa paṃcāṃgaṃ cūrṇitaṃ madhunā sahaḥ |  
varṣaikaṃ bhakṣayen nityaṃ māsāmṛtyujarāpahā ||  
  
brahmāyurjāyate siddho varṣaikaṃ bhakṣayet sadā |  
śarīraṃ bhasmanāmargha ṣaṭmāsā mṛtyujid bhavet ||  
  
jīvedbrahmayugaṃ yāvad divyakāyo bhaven naraḥ |  
  
atha vīryastaṃbhanaṃ ||  
  
kavālaṃgamasi kṛtvā padmasūtreṇa veṣṭayet |  
dhārayet kaṭi deśe tu vīryastaṃbhana kṛdbhavet ||  
  
ekaliṅgaṃ samādāya chāyā śuṣkaṃ tu kārayet |  
apakva madhunāsārdhaṃ mardayitvā pradāpayet ||  
  
ātmaliṃgaṃ tato marghaṃ ratikarma samācaret |  
atimātraṃ bhavatyāsu mūrchā bhavati tatkṣaṇāt ||  
  
kṛṣṇamārjāravālaṃ tu saṃgṛhītaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ |  
dhārayet kaṭideśe tu vīryastaṃbhanamuttamaṃ ||  
  
kanyākartitasūtreṇa vaddhaṃ kaṭitaṭe dṛḍhaṃ |  
śvetaguṃjā tato mūlaṃ vīryastaṃbhanamuttamaṃ ||  
  
dehadaṃ kāla mūlaṃ tu haridrākuṃkumaṃ śaśi |  
locanaṃ sahadevī ca sarvaṃ tulyaṃ vicūrṇayet ||  
  
viṣamuṣṭyattha tailena cūrṇaṃ māloḍya lepayet |  
liṃgaṃ tena ramedrāmāṃ cīraṃ vīryasthiraṃ bhavet ||  
  
śvetārka tulikā karti divyasūkara me daśā |  
yāvajjalati dīpoyaṃ tāvadvīryasthiro bhavet ||  
  
iṃdravāruṇikā mūlaṃ puṣpaṃ nagnaḥ samuddharet |  
bhūṣaṇaiśca gavāṃkṣīraiḥ piṣṭvā kuryād dṛṭaṃvaṭīḥ ||  
  
chāyāśuṣkā sthitā vaktre vīryastaṃbhakarī nṛṇāṃ |  
  
86b)  
  
raktāpāmārgamūlaṃ tu somavārenimaṃtrayet ||  
  
bhaume prātaḥ samuddhṛtya kaṭyāṃ vadhvā ca vīryadhṛk |  
duṃdubho nāmasya suryaḥ kṛṣṇavarṇastamāharet ||  
  
tasyāsthi dhāraṇāt kaghāṃ? naro vīryaṃ na muṃcati |  
tanmuktā mucyate vīryaṃ siddhayogī udāhṛtaḥ ||  
  
saha devīya mūlaṃ tu tatsamaṃ padmakeśaraṃ |  
piṣṭvāmaṅ dhvājya saṃyuktaṃ lepānnābhau tu vīryadhṛk ||  
  
śleṣmānta tasya kulasya vīryaṃ yujyā samāharet |  
ajākṣīreṇa saṃpiṣṭvā bhuktvā ca sarvavīryadhṛk ||  
  
sūraṇaṃ tulasī mūlaṃ tāmbūlaṃ saha bhakṣayet |  
na muṃcatī naro vīryaṃ karṣakena pṛthak pṛthak ||  
  
preṣayedvālikāmūlaṃ umantā yasya sūtrataḥ |  
tena liṃga pralepena naro vīryaṃ na muṃcatī ||  
  
karpūraṃ ṭaṃkanaṃ sūtraṃ munipuṣparasaṃ madhuḥ |  
mardayitvā nipātena liṃgaṃ yāmaṃ tataḥ punaḥ ||  
  
jalaiḥ prakṣālayelliṅgaṃ bhavedrāmā yathocitaṃ |  
vīryaṃ cetpuṃsāyāmamātraṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
kṛṣṇadhattūramūlena pāradaṃ gharṣayed dinaṃ |  
trilohaṃ veṣṭitaṃ vadhvā kapāntaṃ vīryavad bhavet ||  
  
paśupati jalaṃ piṣṭvā vānarī mūla lepitaṃ |  
kartitaṃ liṃga nayati karakīra tasyatāditi ||  
  
saptāhaṃ chāgasalila bhāvitaṃ karavāruṇi |  
goḍhāvartanavidhinā karoti ratasādhanaṃ ||  
  
siddhaṃ kuśuṃbha tailaṃ ca bhūmilatā varṇamiśritaṃ |  
caraṇābhyaṃgena ratīlau? karoti naraṃ varaṃ kharotsāhaṃ ||  
  
nīlotpala sītapaṃkaja na kesaramadhuśarkarā valikena surate ciraṃ kriḍati   
dṛḍhaliṃgonābhivivaraṇe ||  
  
atha vaśīkaraṇabhedāḥ ||  
  
bhūtāla vaṭamūlaṃ tu jalena saha peṣayet |  
vibhūtyā saṃyuto maṃtrī tilako loka vaśya kṛt ||  
  
atha rājavaśyam ||  
  
devadāru paripelavakuṣṭaiścandanāguru |  
  
87a)  
  
bhujaṃga keśarai ||  
  
kuṃkumena madhunā ca nirmito dhūpa eva ca ||  
  
kṛte nṛpa vaśyaḥ ||  
  
kuṃkumaṃ candanaṃ caiva rocanā śaśimiśritaṃ |  
gavāṃkṣīreṇa tilakaṃ rājavaśya karaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
cakramardasya mūlaṃ tu hasta ṛkṣe samuddharet |  
rājadvāre bhaved vaśyo haste vadhvā ca vādajit ||  
  
pūrvaphālguṇi nakṣatre grāhaṃ dāḍima vījakaṃ |  
kare vaddhvā bhaved vaśyo yadi rājā puraṃdaraḥ ||  
  
aśleṣāyāṃ gṛhītantu nāgakeśaracandanaṃ |  
vare vaddhe bhaved vaśyo yo rājā pṛthivīpati ||  
  
atha strīvaśyakaraṇaṃ ||  
  
triśatyamātmato(?) yena mardayitvā vilepayet |  
pūgīphalaṃ pradātavyaṃ vaśyamāmaraṇāntikaṃ ||  
  
eṇakoṇaṃ svavīryeṇa marddayitvā pralepayet |  
saṃmohanaṃ bhavet kṣipraṃ yāvajjīvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
kapiliṃgaṃ samādāya mardayedātmatejasā |  
cūrṇena sahadātavyaṃ kāminījanamohanaṃ ||  
  
śaraṭaṃ mithunibhūtaṃ hatvā tacchalyamāharet |  
ātma toyena dātavyaṃ kāminījanamohanaṃ ||  
  
ātma toyena saṃdhṛṣya dadyāt paṃca palaiḥ saha |  
cūrṇena saha dātavyaṃ vaśyamāmaraṇāṃtikaṃ ||  
  
kapi pittamātma vījaṃ mṛganābhyāthamardayet |  
guṭikāṃkārayet tena daṃdyāduttama yoṣitam ||  
  
vaśī bhavati sā sādhyā śarīrena dhanena ca |  
prāṇeśvaraṃ vihāyāsau na jīvatī na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
caṭakāsthira cūrṇena dadyāt mohana kṛd bhavet |  
tatmāṃsamātmavījena mardayitvā pradāpayet ||  
  
ṣaṇmāsakaṃ bhaved vaśyaṃ kāmadaṃ harṣakārakam |  
pūrvoktamātmano yena gharṣayet pakṣa varjitaṃ ||  
  
yathā pūrvaṃ pradātavyaṃ mohanaṃ maraṇāntikaṃ |  
tatpakṣa cūrṇapānena tatpakṣo vikalo bhavet ||  
  
kaṭu trayena tatmāṃsaṃ bhakṣayed goghṛtena tu |  
kāmasaṃdīpanaṃ tasya bhave deva na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
87b)  
  
tastimātmavījena mardayitvā pradāpayet |  
khāne vā yadi vā pāne mohanaṃ maraṇāntikam ||  
  
atha ṭiṭṭībhaśalyena tatpittaṃ parimardayet |  
enaṃ rocana yā sārddhaṃ dadyāt paṃca palaiḥ sahaḥ ||  
  
yoṣito vasamāyāṃti sādhakasya na saṃśayaḥ |  
khaṃjarīṭasya paṃcāṃgamantardhūpena dhārayet ||  
  
aṃjayannayane netraṃ lokaika vasamuttamaṃ |  
bhāradvājasya picchena svavījaṃ dhūrta vījakaṃ ||  
  
mardayitvā pradātavyaṃ cūrṇena vaśakṛd bhavet |  
gharāvatasya(?) hṛccakṣuḥ svaraktaṃ locanaṃ tathā ||  
  
jihvāmalasamāyuktaṃ aṃjane strī vasā bhavet |  
śaraṭasya vāmanetraṃ madhutailena cāṃjayet ||  
  
yāṃ paśyati narorāmāṃ tatkṣaṇāt sāvaśā bhavet |  
tasyaiva dakṣiṇaṃ netraṃ sauvīramadhunā sahaḥ ||  
  
aṃjitākṣasya sā vaśyā yā strīrūpābhi garvitā |  
svetārkaṃ navanītaṃ ca ajāraktena miśritaṃ ||  
  
aṃjayet netra yugalaṃ rāmāvaśyakaraṃ paraṃ |  
manaḥśilāṃ priyaṃguṃ ca nāgakeśararocanaṃ ||  
  
aṃjitākṣonarorāmāṃ dṛṣṭvā * *? vati dhruvaṃ |  
triṃśatkanakavījāni ṣoḍaśendu yavāstathā ||  
  
godantaṃ naradattaṃ ca piṣṭvā śukrena loḍhayet |  
lalāṭe tilakaṃ kṛtvā vaśī kuryāt tilottamāṃ ||  
  
kaṃṭakaṃ madhuyaṣṭīṃ ca rocanāṃviti bhasma ca |  
kākajihvāṃ samaṃ kṣaudraṃ tilake strī vaśā bhavet ||  
  
puṣpe puṣpaṃ tu saṃgrāhyaṃ bharaṇyāṃ ca phalaṃ tathā |  
śākhāṃ caiva viśākhāyāṃ haste patraṃ tathaiva ca ||  
  
mūle mūlaṃ tu saṃgṛhya kṛṣṇonmattasya ca kramāt |  
piṣṭvā karpūra saṃyuktaṃ kuṃkumaṃ rocanaṃ samaṃ ||  
  
tilake strī vaśaṃ yāti yadi sākṣādaruṃdhati |  
indravāruṇīkā mūlaṃ puṣpe nagnaḥ samuddharet ||  
  
kaṭu trayeṇa vā kṣīraiḥ piṣṭvā tadgālakī kṛtaṃ |  
candanena samāyuktaṃ tilakaṃ strīvaśaṃkaraṃ ||  
  
88a)  
  
karaviṃkaśirastu tulyaṃ svetārkasya tu mūlakaṃ |  
maṃjiṣṭhā bhakṣapāne ca dante romāṃ vaśa nayet ||  
  
raktamūtrapurīṣi ca śravaṇānnayanātmalāṃ |  
miśrikṛtya pradātavyaṃ bhakṣapāne vaśaṃkaraṃ ||  
  
śilāṃtamālapatraṃ ca kuṃkumaṃ rocanāmapi |  
piṣṭvā natikṛte kṛtvā liptadehothavāṃjanaṃ ||  
  
naranārī nṛpājñānāṃ nityaṃ premāspadaṃ bhavet |  
saṃghṛṣya kalikāminī pittage rocanāmapi ||  
  
vāmahastakaniṣṭhānta tilakasya vaśā bhavet |  
viṣṇukrāntā śvetagiri karṇikā markaṭī jaṭā ||  
  
sahamūlena devyāśca rocanā raṃjitāvunā |  
peṣayitvā kanyakāyātatmaye tilake kṛte ||  
  
vaśī karoti nikhilaṃ jagannāstyatrasaṃśayaḥ |  
tamālapatrāṃ janapadma candana priyaṃgubhīrocanayā samāṃśakaiḥ ||  
  
kṛtāṃjanenāṃjita locanaḥ pumān yamīkṣayentaṃ |  
kurute vaśaṃ janaṃ lākṣāpānaṃjitavāso vahuśaḥ śukla cā sṛjā ||  
  
bhavitaṃ śoṣayitvāśca tena kurvīta vartikāṃ |  
saurājanaṃ śuṣkaṃ ca vicūrṇaṃ gatā ca vartulāṃ ||  
  
varāhasteha bharite dīpapātrebhidheyatāṃ |  
prajvālya kajjalaṃ tasmād gṛhītvā tanayo naraḥ ||  
  
aṃjitā kṣobhavet tasya sakarāḥ sarvaśāstrayaḥ |  
sa priyaṃgu vacā kuṣṭaṃ sūkṣmelā nāgakeśaraṃ ||  
  
saśarjarasasiddhārtha dhūpaḥ sarvārthasiddhidaḥ |  
jaṭāmāṃsī bhṛṃgarājenakhakuṇḍarūśīkalaiḥ ||  
  
lākṣā kṛṣṇāṃgurū spṛktā gandhapadmai samāsakaiḥ |  
dhūpaḥ sugandha nāmādau māraṇārāvasaṃnibhaṃ ||  
  
vaśīkaroti trailokyāmiti pūrvamudāhṛtaṃ |  
karpūramadhūkallola śuklasaṃlikasādhanā ||  
  
gāṃbhīramatī hṛdayaṃ tāsāṃ tiṣṭhati saṃtatam ||  
  
iti strīvaśyaṃ |  
  
atha pativaśyakaraṇaṃ |  
  
mālati puṣpasaṃyuktaṃ kaṭutailaṃ supācitaṃ |  
etalliptabhagā rāmā ratau mohayate patiṃ ||  
  
88b)  
  
khaṃjarīṭasya māṃsaṃ tu madhunā saha peṣayet |  
anena yoni lepena patirdāsau bhavet punaḥ ||  
  
karpūraṃ devadāruṃ ca sa kṣaudraṃ pūrvavat phalaṃ |  
saiṃdhavena tilairbhāvyaṃ saptavāraṃ punaḥ punaḥ ||  
  
tatpiṣṭā lepayed yoniṃ ratau dāsaḥ patirbhavet |  
paṃcāṃga dāḍimaṃ piṣṭvā śvetasarṣapa saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
yoni lepe patiṃ dāsaṃ karot pati sudurbhagā |  
rocanaṃ matsya pittaṃ ca pṛṣṭhā tu tilakī kṛte ||  
  
vāmahaste kaniṣṭhāyāṃ patirdāso na saṃśayaḥ |  
svayonau ratikāle tu rocanaṃ nikṣipet punaḥ ||  
  
svapuṣpaṃ bhāvayet tena tilakaṃ pati vaśyakaṃ |  
sumetā? kaṃṭhakāryaśca mūlaṃ ca girikarṇikā ||  
  
tāṃbūlena pradātavyaṃ dāsavat kurute patiṃ |  
samūlāṃ cūrṇayet dhātrīḥ vastre vaddhā nidhāpayet ||  
  
svayonau ṛtukāle tu tridinānte samuddharet |  
navanītena nikṣiptaṃ taccūrṇaṃ pācayed ghṛtaṃ ||  
  
tatghṛtaṃ bhojayedevaṃ patirdāso bhavat palaṃ |  
  
atha gajavaśyakaraṃ ||  
  
uttarāyāṃ samādāya prātarasvattha candakaṃ |  
pṛthagevaṃ kare vaddhvā gajavaśya karaṃ nṛṇāṃ ||  
  
aṃkolaṃ tailasaṃmiśraṃ kuryāddudrānta cūrṇikaṃ |  
anena spṛṣṭamātreṇa mahāhasti vaśo bhavet ||  
  
varāha karṇi saṃcūrṇaṃ akālītala bhāvitaṃ |  
te naiva spṛṣṭhamāteṇa mahāhasti vaśo bhavet ||  
  
atha vājikaraṇaṃ ||  
  
svarase bhāvitaṃ dhātri cūrṇaṃ sītājyapi madhumiśritaṃ |  
kṛtvā tu piyadugdhena tṛpyaṃt strīśatairapi ||  
  
gokṣurakaṃ kṣuraṣṭaḥ śatamūlī vānarī nāgavalāti valā ca |  
cūrṇamidaṃ payasā niśīpeyaṃ yasya gṛhe pramadāśatamasti ||  
  
yavakalamamāṣa cūrṇaistulyago madhūmamāgadhisahitaiḥ |  
pālikā ghṛta pakvaṃ tu bhuktvā kṣīraṃ saśarkaraṃ pītaṃ ||  
  
89a)  
  
ghṛtamadhusahadevānvita sarojakalipta nāmekavāraramamānasyana tṛpyaṃti   
manaḥ ||  
  
tenāpi ramatīṇāṃ vījaṃ kṣurakaṃkakaṃ |  
  
cūrṇikṛtena sakalaṃ ||  
  
nipīya payasā rātrau naraḥsyā vurjayoratau ||  
  
pippalilavanopetācchāgade kṣirasarpisā |  
sādhitāṃ bhakṣayed yastu sa gacchet pramadā śataṃ ||  
  
mocakasya phalaṃ tulyaṃ sarpiṣā madhunā mamaṃ |  
liṭṭāni pīyadugdhaṃ ca prāpnoti ratimuttamā ||  
  
yadyaśca gandharividāri gokṣuraṃ vārāhīmāṣaṃ ca śatāvarī ca |  
guñjāphalaṃ cāmalakaṃ sālmalī niryāsamete tu saśarkarānvitā ||  
  
niṣkatrayaṃditamukhamalālehyaṃ rātrau pibet kṣīrayutaṃ ca tadvarat |  
māsārddhamātreṇa sahasra yoṣitāṃ dine dine bhogasamṛddhidā bhavet ||  
  
śuddhaṃ sūtaṃ samaṃ gandhaṃ vadīrī citra kaṭṭavaiḥ |  
mahyakāṃ caurajaindrā vai stri dinaṃ tacca golakaṃ ||  
  
sadyokṣatājamāṃsasya piṇḍaḥ neṣṭhaṃ viśeṣayet |  
tatpiṇḍaṃ tilatailena lohapātre śanaiḥ pacet ||  
  
yāvat māsaṃ raktavarṇaṃ tataḥ sūtaṃ samuddharet |  
tridinaṃ muśalī kvāthe bhāvitaṃ śītayā yutaṃ ||  
  
niṣkaikaṃ bhakṣayennityaṃ rasoyaṃ madaneśvaraḥ |  
vidālī kandacūrṇaṃ tū kṣīrājyena palaṃlihan ||  
  
ramestrīṇāṃ śataṃ nityaṃ ratyagā tatvamāpnuyāt |  
dhātrī phalasya taccūrṇaṃ bhāvayet tatphala dravaiḥ ||  
  
ekaviṃśati vārācaiḥ śoṣyaṃ paśya punaḥ punaḥ |  
tatpādāṃ saṃtmṛtaṃ lohaṃ madhvājya śarkarāyutaṃ ||  
  
palaikaṃ bhakṣayen nityaṃ niśīkṣīraṃ pivedanu |  
dhātrīlohaprabhāvena ramayet kāminī śataṃ ||  
  
śuddha sūtaṃ samaṃgandhaṃ karaktotpaladaladravaiḥ |  
yāmārdhaṃ ca punargandhaṃ rasārdhaṃ tatra nikṣipet ||  
  
pūrvadrāvairdinaṃmargha rasārdhaṃ gandhakaṃ punaḥ |  
datvā taddinaṃ saṃmarghakāca kuryānniveśayet ||  
  
89b)  
  
dinaikaṃ vālukā yaṃtre suṣkamuddhṛtya cūrṇayet |  
bhūkuṣmāṇḍa kaṣāyeṇa bhāvayedvitasaptakaṃ ||  
  
chāyāyāṃ tāsitātulyaṃ niṣkaikaṃ bhakṣayet sadā |  
valāmūla svavījaṃ ca muśalī śarkarāsamaṃ ||  
  
gavāṃkṣīraiḥ parārddha caira? tu rātrau sadā pibet |  
anantaṃ vardhate vījaṃ rasoyaṃ madanodayaḥ ||  
  
mṛtaṃ tu pārada svarṇaṃ tulyaṃ marghaṃ dina trayaṃ |  
muśalī triphalā kvāthairvājigandhakaṣāyakaiḥ ||  
  
kadalī kaṃdajairdrāvaistadgolaṃ cādine puṭe |  
bhūdhare dinamātraṃ tu samuddhṛtyātha mardayet ||  
  
dinaikaṃ pūrvavidrāvaistadvadhvāmapacet puṭe |  
punaḥ marghaḥ punaḥ pācyaṃ evamaṣṭapuṭaiḥ pacet ||  
  
śalmalī gī?taniryāsairbhavaśarkarasāsaha |  
khādenniṣkasya nityaṃ dhārayedvyaya niścitaṃ ||  
  
gokṣīraṃ markaṭī vījaṃ pālārddhe pācayedanu |  
sarvo godharttanaṃ kuryāt saṃpacaiḥ śālmalī rasaiḥ ||  
  
rasakāma kalākhyeyaṃ mahāvīrya karī nṛṇāṃ |  
prāraṃbhe rajāsā strīṇāṃ mardayedbhasmasūtakaṃ ||  
  
mṛtaṃ tāmraṃ ca tāraṃ ca gandhakaṃ ca samārdataḥ |  
śitāmadhvājyasaṃyuktaṃ niṣkaṃbhakṣyāya yaḥ pibet ||  
  
ratikāma ratī nāma kāminīramaṇehitaḥ |  
śuddhasūtaṃ samaṃgaṃdha ahaṃkharjura tai dravaiḥ ||  
  
marditaṃ cārditaṃ paścād yāmasaikata yaṃtrake |  
raktagastya dravairbhāvyaṃ dinaikaṃ tatsitā yutaṃ ||  
  
niṣkamātraṃ sadākhādedrasomadanavardhanaḥ |  
ajasya vṛṣaṇaṃ kṣīraiḥ pakvatilasitāyutaṃ ||  
  
yathecchaṃ bhakṣayedyotu ramayait kāminī śataṃ |  
paladvayaṃ śuddhasūtaṃ gandhakaṃ ca rataḥ śubhaṃ ||  
  
karṣakaṃ māritaṃ svarṇaṃ palaikaṃ tu mṛtābhrakaṃ |  
raupyaṃ bhasmaja tu niṣkaṃ sarvaṃ paṃcāmṛtairdinaṃ ||  
  
mardyarūdhvādinaṃ pacyādbhūdhare ca samuddharet |  
  
90a)  
  
piṣṭvā paṃcāmṛtaiḥ khādairguṭikāṃ vadarā kṛti ||  
  
anaṃga sundarīkhyātā rāmānāramayecchataṃ |  
śālmalī mūlacūrṇaṃ tu madhvājya śarkarāyutaṃ ||  
  
ekaikaṃ bhakṣayeccānu sītākṣīraṃ ca pācayet |  
śālmalyubhya dravairmadyaṃ palaikaṃ śuddhapāadaraṃ ||  
  
śuddhagandhaṃ trisaptāhaṃ mardayetta dravaiḥ pṛthak |  
samavetauḥ punarmadya ghṛtairyāma catuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
tadgolaṃ vandhayedvastre ghṛte yāmadvayaṃ pacet |  
tatastaṃ śālmalī drāvairmardayed divasa trayaṃ ||  
  
nikṣipet kācakuryāt tat vālukā yaṃtrake pacet |  
kṣiptaṃ ca śālmalī drāvaiḥ kupigarbhe dināvadhi ||  
  
sarvamevaṃ samuddhṛtyamiśrayet sītayāsamaṃ |  
niṣkamātraṃ sadākhoderasāyaṃ madanāyakaṃ ||  
  
muśalīsaśitākṣīraupalaika pācayedanu |  
kāminī vāṃ sahasraikaṃ kṣobhayennimiṣāṃtare ||  
  
śuddhasūtaṃtrayo bhāgāḥ bhāgaikaṃ tāmravarṇakaṃ |  
kṛtvā piṣṭāni rūdhvādharaṃ bhākaṃdāvale punaḥ ||  
  
mṛttasaṃcopitaṃ paścād dinaikaṃ karī cāgninā |  
evaṃ saptadinaṃ paṃcyādekaṃ ekaṃ dinaṃ dinaṃ ||  
  
uddhṛtyavandhayedvastrairdṛḍhe caturguṇe punaḥ |  
kṣudrasaṃcūkamāsānte chāgīraktagatāṃ pacet ||  
  
olāyāṃ ca ahaṃ yathā evaṃ raktaṃ punaḥ punaḥ |  
guḍucyā kāka pippalyāṃ kadalyāḥ kokilākṣakaiḥ ||  
  
gokṣīrodvānarīmūlaiti mūlasya tvacondravaiḥ |  
pāyasai tatkaṣāyairtado?lā yaṃtre dinaṃ trayaṃ ||  
  
tataḥ kṣīre sitā yukte tadvadvalyādi nāvadhiḥ |  
uddhṛtya murālī kvāthairmadyayārme catuṣṭayaṃ ||  
  
rasapūrṇe tu nāmoyaṃ khādenmāṣasitāyutaṃ |  
gokṣīrī vānarī vījāṃ guḍucīrgajapippalī ||  
  
kokilākṣasya vījāni marjākārpāsa vījakaṃ |  
  
90b)  
  
satāvarī caraṃ bhavā phalaṃ madhusamaṃ bhavet ||  
  
sarvatulyāsitā yojyā madhunā lolitaṃ lihet |  
palārdhamanupānaṃ syāt tajaḥ peyaṃ gavāṃ payaḥ ||  
  
kāminīnāṃ sahasrāṃte ramayestu mahāvalī |  
bhūrje kūrmaṃ samālikhya tārakena ṣaḍāṅgulaṃ ||  
  
pṛṣṭhe tuṣṭānsamālikhya sādhakaṃ madhyato likhet |  
bhūrjapatre samālikhya kuṃkuṃmena triśūlikāṃ ||  
  
na paśyaṃ sa yathāṃ dhvastu buddhorno phalati dviṣaḥ |  
mālāmaṃtrodhunā vācyo yathā sarvajña bhāṣitaḥ ||  
  
yathā pūrvamayākarma yathādho trihināgaṇāḥ |  
nikṣipya sannito corddhaṃ tathā tadyaṃtritedhunā ||  
  
kṛtvā tu bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ mālāmaṃtraṃ samālikhet |  
oṃ śatrumukhastaṃbhani kāmarūpa āḍili karī ||  
  
hrī& hra& phaṭkāriṇī mamaśatrūnāṃ devadattādīnāṃ mukhaṃ   
staṃbhayavijṛṃbhaya mama sarvavidveṣiṇāṃ mukhastaṃbhanaṃ kuru 2 hrī&   
hreṃ phaṭkāriṇī svāhā |   
  
idaṃ hi staṃbhane śreṣṭhaṃ sadya pratyaya kārakaṃ |   
bhairavī rauravāmaṃtrādā kṛṣya viduṣāmayā ||  
  
iti mukhastaṃbhanaṃ ||  
  
pāṭalīmūlamāgṛhya puṣpāṣṭamyāṃ yathāvaraḥ |  
abhimaṃtre mahāmaṃtre māyābhistaṃ triśūlakaiḥ ||  
  
vāhuvandhaṃstataṃ kṛtvā khaḍgai vai staṃbhaye dhruvaṃ |  
vajraṃ kaṃkāriṇī māye variṇī āyekara khaḍgaṃ tu khaṃḍini bhaṃjanitāḍani   
khukhulī ye svāhā ||  
  
iti khaḍgastaṃbhanaṃ ||  
  
triśūlaṃ ca kuṭhāraṃ ca jarāṃ caiva tu sarvaraṃ |  
guṭikāṃ vatturāṃ caiva sarvāstān dhvaṃśaye manuḥ ||  
  
oṃ hrī& huṃ jalamaṃkuṭhāramaṃ sarvalamaṃtulāṃ maṃguṭikāmaṃ evaṃ   
bhūrje samālikhyaṃ paṃca bījena saṃyutāḥ ||  
  
pāṃcālyāḥ pūjanaṃ kṛtvā dagdhāṃvujāvunā pivet |  
advaita cittamālaṃvya nirviśaṃ kona saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
japet sarvaṃ mahādivyaṃ divyājñāyāḥ prabhāvataḥ |  
oṃ jalajalasamayī dhātū dharaṇīga aṇanamayī ||  
  
91a)  
  
iti paṃcāliya svāhā ||  
  
evamutvā saptavārān lākṣāṃ likhitvākṣarāṃ dahet |  
staṃbhanoyaṃ samākṛṣṭaḥ satvataṃtrā tu bhairava ||  
  
iti ṣaṭ divyastambhanaṃ ||  
  
rājādistuṣyate yena na bhayaṃ ca nṛpāditaḥ |  
siṃhoragamahāvyāghra yakṣavāta bhayantathā ||  
  
uktānuktaṃ ca yat sarvaṃ bhaya sadyo vinaśyati |  
  
oṃ hrī& staṃbhanī sāvarī harasāranalikṣā hu& phaṭ ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ   
sitakākālikānetraṃ bhelasī ca tripatrikā |   
  
mohannaguṇa puṣpā ca vicakṣu ṛṣa eva ca |  
ekīkṛtvā japeccakṣustadā cakṣurnivandhayet ||  
  
indrajālaṃ mayākhyātaṃ dṛṣṭi stambhanamuttamaṃ |  
naiva paśyati paśyantaṃ paśyaṃte na tadyathā ||  
  
yaṃ yaṃ darśayate bhāvaṃ taṃ taṃ loko hi paśyati |  
iti cakṣuḥ staṃbhanaṃ kiṃ jalkaṃ sita padmasya vījaṃ sākhoṭakasya ca ||  
  
śāpuṃkhāśataṃ netre nābhilepā sthiro haraḥ |  
śukrasya staṃbhanaṃ hyetat senaketu samāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
candraloke nirodhaṃ ca ye manasyaṃ ca vibhramā |  
  
iti śukrastaṃbhanaṃ ||  
  
śitikāmayamākṛṣya khuragopāthabhūlatā |  
varatī deha cūrṇaṃ tu tṛṇasya nalukā tathā ||  
  
ekīkṛtya kṣiped yonau yonistaṃbhanamuttamaṃ |  
pittaṃ rohita mīnasya tathā caitatpalūtikāḥ ||  
  
keśarājasamāyuktaṃ peyaṃ bhakṣaṃ kriyānvite |  
staṃbhayedviṣasaṃbhūtaṃ palitaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
iti valipalita staṃbhanaṃ ||  
  
vanamūlakamaṃtrī ca tathā pānāṃgamastrakaṃ |  
eṣāṃ kṛttiṃ samādāya yathā lābhena buddhimān ||  
  
pūjayet tu malaṃ mūtraṃ veṣṭayet kaṃpi taṃtutā |  
nihite mriyate bhūmau nirodho malamūtrayoḥ ||  
  
eṣa yogavaro dṛṣṭo guhyakālikamaṃtrake |  
  
91b)  
  
iti malamūtra staṃbhanaṃ |  
  
paṭehanuṃ samālikhya garjayaṃtaṃ mahāvalaṃ |  
nāgaṃ vai saṃlikhed dakṣe kare uccāṭite tava ||  
  
tatra maṃtra likhet ghoraṃ staṃbhanaṃ hara nirmitaṃ |  
saṃgrāme darśayed rājā dhvaje vijayamicchayā ||  
  
staṃbhayet sarvasainyāni nātrakāryāvicāraṇā |  
  
oṃ hu& phaṭ mahābhairava rūpiṇī sarvaśainyāni staṃbhaya svāhā |  
  
iti senāstaṃbhanaṃ |  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mohanaṃ yogamuttamaṃ |  
yena yojitamātreṇa mohayet sakalaṃ jagat ||  
  
harapriyā sahadevī vījamekaika eva ca |  
madhvājo na samāyojya tilakaṃ mohanātmakaṃ ||  
  
eṣa yogavaro divyaḥ śaktivījasamanvitaḥ |  
  
iti naranārī staṃbhanaṃ |  
  
oṃ namo bhagavatī bhagamālinī visphura 2 nityaklinne drava 2 hrī&   
kārākṣarekṣarakṣaktī& hsau svāhā ||  
  
anenaiva tu maṃtreṇa abhimatryatriḥ peṣayet |  
tilakaṃ kārayedvidvān yadiśenmohitaṃ jagat ||  
  
mohayaṃcāṃgakaṃ piṣṭvā liptaliṃga prayatnataḥ |  
tatastu śukrassutaṃ sāpita ṣaḍet parikīrtitaḥ ||  
  
pratyakṣa niyato yogo bhagamālinī saṃjñakaḥ |  
raktamohāhite catrī svāsaścādhenu maṃtrayet ||  
  
iti jagatmohanaṃ ||  
  
śitobhānuḥ sitāguṃjā gṛhasya caṭakastathā |  
kuṣṭhaṃ syāṃgā sṛjāyuktaṃ tilakaṃ mohanātmakaṃ ||  
  
puṣpena yojayennityaṃ sadyaḥ pratyayakārakaṃ |  
  
iti naranārī mohanaṃ ||  
  
uktāmohātmakā yogā dṛṣṭoyaṃ svayameva tu |  
tilake bhakṣaṇe vāpi lepane vāpi yojayet ||  
  
nārī ṛtumatī vālā taruṇī prauḍhīkā tathā |  
sīmante cātha sragdhupairgaṃdhaistāṃvūla cailakaiḥ ||  
  
vījane sthāpayet tatra kṛtvā tu snāna karma ca |  
japet puṣpa vihṛdyāṃ sa āhatasya golakaiḥ ||  
  
mohayaṃ cāṃgasaṃyuktā vaṭīṃ pranvitāṃ caret |  
  
92a)  
  
aṣṭottara śataṃ kṛtvā paṭṭasūtreṇa graṃthayet ||  
  
mohanīṃ ca tapentena nibhṛto rātrau nirākulaḥ |  
ayutena bhavet siddhiḥ kampate vasudhātaṃlaṃ ||  
  
yakṣagandharvakinnarya athonyā api yoṣitaḥ |  
garuḍāpsarasonāga hāṭakerśvara kanyakāḥ ||  
  
mugdhāstatra samāyāṃti muktakeśāśca vihvalāḥ |  
nagnā ghaṭitasūnāḥ dhṛṣṭāḥ kiṃ punarnarayoṣitaḥ ||  
  
gurusthānena kurvītaṃ mātrā yatrāvatiṣṭhati |  
balātsaṃgrāhayennityaṃ mugdhā vā mṛyate vasā ||  
  
gopanīyaṃ prayatnena pratyakṣaṃ suparirakṣitaṃ |  
lakṣaikena tu japtena kāmadeva samo bhavet ||  
  
gajendra dravamadhupai nārībhirveṣṭito bhramet |  
  
iti mahāmohanarājavasyam ||  
  
meṣaśṛṃgī ajāśṛgīkākamācītriśūlīkā |  
dehajaiḥ paṃcabhiryuktaṃ tilakaṃ mohanātmakaṃ ||  
  
kathyate ca mahāyogaḥ sadyaḥ pratyayakārakaḥ |  
saṃmohanaṃ bhayivide kuḍera mohe mohaniye svāhā ||  
  
evamabhimaṃtritaṃ kṛtvā saptavārān vicakṣaṇaḥ |  
dadāti pūgasaṃyogaṃ vaṭapatrakasaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
mohito niyate yatra tatra gacchati nānyathā |  
vikreśaṃ vamatiṃ dadyāt kropi hi na kupyati ||  
  
iti mahāmohinī ||  
  
svaśiracchiyate? mugdhe naiva jānāti vihvalaṃ |  
eva dhūliṃ prayogā tu sarvarīmahanirgataḥ ||  
  
gopanīyaṃ prayatnena yadi checcirajīvinaṃ |  
gopitaṃ sarvataṃtreṣu tatra vai kuhakārṇave ||  
  
yogasya satyatāṃ dṛṣṭvā utsukena mayādhunā |  
nāgarāṇāṃ hitārthāya spaṣṭametadudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
mugdhasya harsapālasya svīkṛtārājyasaṃpadaḥ |  
dinai dvādaśī muktā svavāṃchā casaṃkakarṣavaiḥ ||  
  
suyoṣita svayaṃ yogā mayā cātra na gopitā |  
latā harita varṇābhā atisūkṣmā payonvitā ||  
  
vaṭapatra samaṃ patraṃ syādrakta sannibhaṃ |  
  
92b)  
  
tasya laṃghanamātreṇa diṅmohotha prajāyate |  
bhakṣaṇena mahāmūrchāṃ śaṃkare yadi dīyate ||  
  
vaṭapatrī parijñānaṃ vahubhiḥ parikīrtitaṃ |  
  
iti mohanaṃ |  
  
oṃ sāvarīmāye puṣpamūlasānīye tu brahma pasāyeyaṃ nāmimāṃ mohamiti hu   
aninayasayatva sa cādi hi kiṇi svāhā | anena maṃtreṇa vāhya diśo nivāsita ciṃcinī   
vṛkṣatalanī śabdena mayaṃ gṛhyacauyaṃ saptābhirmaṃtrayet | tayā dhūlyāyo   
hanyet | samohito bhavati | athavā yasmin gṛhe nikṣipe tatra sarve lokāḥ suptā   
niśceṣṭāḥ saṃmohitā bhavaṃti | yadīṣṭaṃ tat kriyate svecchayā | iti   
mahāmūrchā ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi vaśīkaraṇamuttamaṃ |  
yena vijñāna mātreṇa trailokyaṃ kriyate vaśaṃ ||  
  
jāti mātaṃgīkā caiva tathā moha latātmikā |  
brahmakarparasaṃbhūtā vaśyagolaka nirmitā ||  
  
bhītāmadhuratā vāpi madhugolakamiśritā |  
cāṇḍālī rasasaṃpūrṇā vaśīkaraṇamuttamaṃ ||  
  
nāgābhelakābhītācādha puṣpī ca kroṭikā |  
haradaitya samāyuktā vaṭī nityaṃ vaśaṃkarī ||  
  
jāti caiva tu cāṇḍālī rudaṃti kṛtāṃjaliḥ |  
kākamācī samāyuktā vaśya golakayojitā ||  
  
dehajaḥ paṃcabhiryuktaṃ gorocana samanvitaṃ |  
haradaitya samāyuktaṃ pūṃgaṃ dadyād vaśaṃkaraṃ ||  
  
iti kāle ca pāretonāryāvāsāṅghriṣu kṣipet |  
sa bhaved vallabhastasyā yāvajjīvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
mohani traya yaṃtrākhyā hastinīṃ caiva mohayet |  
drāvaṇaṃ ca sadā kuryāt madhukarpūraṭaṃkaṇaiḥ ||  
  
bhūrjati jyeṣṭhakāyuktāṃ varāṃgaṃ mardayet sadā |  
yasya yasya hi yo bhāvā tena tasya samācaret ||  
  
hantakacchoditvayogāḥ sadyaḥ pratyayakārakāḥ |  
bhallāṭakasya vījāni tathāa vai gaja pippalīḥ ||  
  
aśvagandhā samāyuktaḥ sargasarpiḥ samanvitaḥ |  
etairvimardayelliṅgaṃ pakṣaikaṃ liṅgada?dvaye ||  
  
hastinī vaśyatāṃ yāti kiṃ punarvaḍavā mṛgī |  
kathitā ḍāmare tantre tathā vai guhyakālike ||   
  
sadyaḥ siddhikarā yogā prapaṃca sahitāḥ śubhāḥ |  
kṛṣṇakākāli cakṣurbhyāṃ golakena samanvitā ||  
  
aṃjalīvada saṃyuktāmarkamaṃtīni pūrayet |  
  
93a)  
  
kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ valiṃ datvā vidhānataḥ ||  
  
na lākṣamadhūnā yuktaṃ nirvāṇe tu samāhitaḥ |  
cakṣustenāṃ jayeddhīmān yadicche bhuvanaṃ vaśaṃ ||  
  
yaṃ yaṃ paśyati bhāvena yaṃ yaṃ prārthayate punaḥ |  
taṃ taṃ saṃsādhayet kṣipraṃ suparīkṣā yathā kṛtaṃ ||  
  
valimaṃtra samāveṣṭaṃ pheṃ pheṃ pheṃ kariṇī namaḥ |  
śaulipakṣasamāyuktaṃ aligolakamiśritaṃ ||  
  
sarvadikṣu valiṃ datvā sādhayet kaṃjjalaṃ sādhanam |  
pheṃ huṃ phaṃ phaṭ huṃ phaṭ phaṭkāriṇī hrīṃ jvala trailokyaṃ mohaya mohaya   
svāhā ||  
  
anena mantreṇa svāṃgalepaṃ golakena mukhābhyaṃjanaṃ tilakaṃ ca kṛtvā   
rājagṛhaṃ viśet |  
vādivarga kuryād yūte kāryanyāyasaṃgrāmādi kṛte jayaṃ kuryāt ||  
  
asya prabhāvena | iti guhyakālyāḥ prayogaḥ ||  
  
coditā vahavo yogā maṃtrataṃtra mahāvalāḥ |  
kintu siddhānate sarve durbodhapaṭṭasaṃvṛtāḥ ||  
  
tasyādyogamahaṃ vakṣye sapta taṃtu vivarjitaṃ |  
kharparasyamate dṛṣṭaṃ yadṛṣṭaṃ sāmalāmataḥ ||  
  
prāvṛti śūlinī gaṃḍīraktākhyā ca pracoditā |  
kṛtāṃjalī ca vāgeśī etāṃ dhūlī kṛtāṃvarā ||  
  
kurvaṃti satataṃ mohamekatvena niyojitāḥ |  
oṃ hrīṃ huṃ phaṭ phreṃ guṃjarīt bhramarīkaike yo puṣkasī lalajjihvī vetāli rākṣasī   
madavāhinī he avatara raha 2 kaha 2 prasphura 2 sphu 2 khetaliha kici 2 phreṃ pravasī   
ālī hu& phaṭ ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ | iti kṛtvā valiṃ datvā mālālaṃvita śira   
ānīyasthālyāṃ prakṣipya jvālayitvā nirbhṛtanidhāyayet tatra sthāne   
paṃcopacāravidhinā pūjayet | uktamaṃtreṇāṣṭottaraśatamabhimaṃtrya   
śṛṃgālāsthī kīlakaṃ nidhāpayet | tato valiṃ sarvadikṣu dadyāt |   
  
trisaṃdhyāṃ nityaṃ samāhitaḥ kāryaṃ saptāhaṃ sādhayet |  
eṣamaṃtravaraḥ proktastatraivakharpare mate ||  
  
93b)  
  
etasyaiva prabhāvena kharpareṇa ca dhīmatā |  
martye vai sādhitaṃ sarvaṃ vaśyaṃ kṛtvā naraṃ nṛpaṃ ||  
  
na paśyanti narāḥ kepi sarvasva haraṇe kṛte |  
deyā deyaṃ na jānāti dadāti sakalaṃ dhanaṃ ||  
  
svakāntāmarpayetmugdhaḥ svadehamapi cārpayet |  
vihvalā jāyate nārī kuṃjarī śivamohitāṃ ||  
  
prayāti niyate yatra krayavikraya dāyinī |  
atrasakāṃ na kurvīta mayābhikṣṇaṃ parikṣitaṃ ||  
  
brahmayā malataṃtre tu purāproktaṃ svayaṃbhuvā |  
  
oṃ hrīṃ staṃbhāmāraṇaṃ proccāṭaya hana hana raha raha hrīṃ sāravijanaje   
caurāśimārastaṃbhanaṃ nayati astra staṃbhanaṃ anaṃ ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ svāhā |   
  
etatsarvaṃ staṃbhayati śailasamūhadaṃ śudṛṣṭaṃ tadarpyase gṛhītvā |  
vṛṃhanā ūphalasya ca araphalavijanaḥ naracarmavilepena jale bhavati nirbhayaṃ ||  
  
iti jalanirbhayaṃ ||  
  
kākamācī ajāśṛṃgī triśūlī meṣaśṛṃgīke |  
dehajau paṃcake raktaṃ kuryāt tamohanātmakaṃ ||  
  
tatasto māṃsamādāya ubhayorvākyasaṃyutaṃ |  
homaṃ tu kārayet sthālyāṃ bhūtigrāhyā vicakṣaṇe ||  
  
uttarīya samaṃ kuryāt pucchayormahiṣaśvayo |  
devadattasya nāmnā ca siddhiṃ caiva vadhārayet ||  
  
oṃ vidveṣaṇī kolamukhī ghoravadane kuru 2 vidveṣa 2 troṭaya 2 toḍabhaya svāhā |   
maṃtreṇānena cakṣuṣīkākālayakāṣṭānihunet ||  
  
oṃ hrīṃ svāṃ hāṃ oṃ tathā ayamaṃtro yathā | oṃ hrīṃ hai haṃ te hraṃ hantu   
mohanī svāhā | rasakoṣā saha dadāti vā | iti maṃtreṇa tilakaṃ kuryāt mohini   
bhavati na saṃdeha |   
  
puṣpayogena kṣiptvā mukhe jale nirudhasvo sadhāraṇaṃ kapālaṃ cūrṇitaṃ  |   
kṛtvā śrīvidyā sadyo bhavati nānyathā | hastau pādau krameṇa pūgena saha   
dātavyaṃ mohanaṃ caiva kārakaṃ |   
  
vyāghra tailaṃ vakṣiptkā jagatmohanaṃ caiva kārayet |  
viṣṇukrāntā phalaṃ caiva puṣpanakṣatre utpādyayaṃ ghṛtena sahitaṃ ||  
  
94a)  
  
kajjalaṃ sanmādayutenākallena sarvajana priyo bhavati |  
keśarīṃ bhṛṃgarājaṃ dhvajayāṃ cāpya parājitāṃ ||  
  
pūṣamūlasamaṃ kṛtvā aṃjayet sarvajana priyo bhavati |  
bhṛṃgarāja gorocana tilakaṃ kṛtvā mayūraśikhāṃ mūla utpādyate   
śirasidhārayet |  
  
duṣṭo hi vaso bhavati saha devi bhramaṃ norjāta masimūlāstāsvaṣakaṃ   
samabhāgakṛtaṃ cūrṇaṃ kṛtvā vaśyaṃ bhavati mastake |  
śveta dūrvākṛṣṇavidyāṃ mūlaṃ ca raktasya ca anāmikā raktaṃ   
citrānakṣatrayā samaṃ ||  
  
paranārī bhavet tasya bhakṣite yadi dīyate |  
viṣṇukrāntā bhaven mūlaṃ pitvā pitvā bhavennaraḥ ||  
  
sūtidūṣyā bhavennārī vaśyā bhavaṃti nānyathā |  
  
cāmuṇḍe 2 janaprajana svāhā ||  
  
anena maṃtreṇa saptavāraṃ maṃtrī japed vahudhā vāmā vaśyā bhavati   
dunducchiṣṭa cāṇḍālīnī mātaṅgīnī sarvavaśīkaraṇāya svāhā ||  
  
iti maṃtreṇa saptavārātmaṃtritaṃ bhukto cchiṣṭadānāt |  
  
yasya dīyate sarva vaśyo bhavati | oṃ viśveśvarī kāmeśvarī amukīṃ vaśamānaya   
svāhā ||  
  
anena maṃtreṇa saptavārān maṃtrī jñena? yasyā dīyate sāvaśyā bhavati   
ākulā ca | oṃ hrīṃ namo bhagavatī cāmuṇḍāyaini śmaśāna vāsinī amukī   
mānaya svāhā | iti maṃtraṃ sakhāyāṃ ekaviṃśati vāraṃ japitvā saṃkhyāyāṃ   
na vaśyā bhavati | kṛṣṇasvānaṃ poṣavātri? pathe pātayitvā dakṣiṇa   
pādasyāsthi khaṃ guru ḍaṃ ekāṃgula pramāṇaṃ ravivāra ānayitvā saṃkhyā   
pārśve sthāpayitvā saptāṃgulasyā datvā āmaṃtreṇa | oṃ phreṃ phreṃ svāhā   
amukaṃ amukī oṃ aphreṃ phreṃ sahe madala iti ākarṣaḥ vaśyaṃ |   
dhattūraphalāṃtare pūgaphalaṃ sthāpayitvāḥ catuṣpathe devabhakṣyāṃ aṃdho na   
varjayet ||  
  
94b)  
  
tasapari maṃgalavārādārabhya mūtrayet | pratyahani aparamaṃgalavāreṇa cūrṇa |   
sahitaṃ dāpayet | strīpuṃso āyata bhavati | mayūraśikhā mūlaṃ piṣṭātāmvulena   
saha khāditaṃ devaṃ cūrṇaṃ saha vaśyo bhavati | manuṣaṃ choditaṃ vīyate yadi
