syānnityaṃ muṣṭhikau hastābhyāṃ dhārayitvā punaḥ saṃgṛhyatattilaṃ   
khāditaṃ deyaṃ chuṃchuṃdarī śubhadine na cānyathā yudhī deyaṃ tadā   
siddhirbhavati | tasya viṣṭhāṃ ca saṃgṛhya kajjalaṃ pātayet kapāle tilakaṃ   
kuryād vīparīte tāmeti yudhitena vaśyante skandaṃ śirasi varjitaṃ | āścaryaṃ   
kurute japtvā iti kavandhadaḥ ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi vidveṣakaraṇaṃ paraṃ |  
saṃpratyayakaraṃ yogaṃ nānātaṃtre vinirgataṃ ||  
  
kākakākāripakṣaṃ ca romacāṣaviḍālayoḥ |  
dvijātyajaśiraḥ keśaṃ roma vā putailāṣṭaviṣasaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
ekīkṛtya bhaved yogī siddhānta hṛdaye sthitaṃ |  
nivenā pūritaṃ kṛtvā vadanaṃ vā dveṣa saṃyutaṃ ||  
  
ubhayorapi samādāya nāmavākyasamanvitaṃ |  
sahasraikaṃ huned yogī muktakeśo digamvaraḥ ||  
  
homāṃte saṃgrahed bhasma viṣayuktaṃ tu kārayet ||  
  
hrī& tuṃḍe viṃḍe daṃṭe hu& ṭhaṃ tridveṣiṇī aiṃ devadattasya yajñadantena ca   
ubhayorapi vā vicheṣaṇaṃ kuru 2 svāhā | eṣamantraḥ samākhyāto mahoḍḍiśaḥ   
prakīrtitaḥ ||  
  
niyataṃ ca vahiḥ kuryād ghoraṃ vidveṣaṇaṃ paraṃ |  
niṃvakākālayaṃtītvā kicilladrana saṃtyajet ||  
  
rājikālavaṇaṃ cājyaṃ viṣaṃ siddhārthakaṃ tathā |  
ekīkṛtya kṣipet pātraṃ trāhikā cāru sādhite ||  
  
tataḥ somaṃ samādāya ubhayorvākyasaṃyutaṃ |  
homaṃ tu kārayet sthālyāṃ bhūtirgrāhyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ||  
  
uttarīya samaṃ kuryāt pucchayormahiṣāśvayoḥ |  
devadattasya nāmnā ca siddhiścaivāvadhārayet ||  
  
95a)  
  
oṃ vidveṣiṇī koṣamukhī ghoravadane kuru 2 vidveṣaya 2 troṭaya 2 toḍaya svāhā |  
  
maṃtreṇānena cakṣuṣikākālayakāṣṭāni hunet |  
vidveṣa homaśeṣasya bhasma caiva tu saṃgrahet ||  
  
āsane śayane gātre vastre vāsa gṛhe tathā |  
kṣipedveṣa samākāṃkṣī ityevaṃ kālikā mate ||  
  
nirvisakaḥ sadākuryāt saṃdeho na ca vidyate |  
mātrā putrayostu vairaṃ syāt kimanyasya tu vismayaḥ ||  
  
mukhasyāṃ sṛjamā gṛhya mārjālasya tathaiva ca |  
viṣabhagasamāyuktaṃ vimbapatre samālikhet ||  
  
ubhayorapi nāmāpi sahamaṃtra samanvitaṃ |  
paścāt saṃmohayet maṃtrī viṣasarpiryutaṃ punaḥ ||  
  
svasthāne ca kurvīta kuryānnityaṃ śmaśānake |  
nibhṛte vāpta deśe tu janasaṃkula varjite ||  
  
ubhanaṃ bhava ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ |  
  
anenaiva tu maṃtreṇa juhuyāda yutena ca |  
muktakeśaśca digvāsā niṃvalepita vigrahaḥ ||  
  
paripūrṇakapolastu nimvapatraiḥ sadārakaiḥ |  
mukhe vai tatsamāsaṣṭa tadā homaṃ samācaret ||  
  
paścime codayed bhānuryadimerūḥ prakampate |  
vahniḥ śītalatāṃ yāti sāgaro yadi suṣyati ||  
  
tathāpyayaṃ na vai yogo mithyātva mupagacchati |  
harṣabhairava maṃtrasya vidveṣaḥ kathyate dhunā ||  
  
kathyate vāpi saṃpatyā sadā vistara sādhanaṃ |  
yasya yogānu vandhena vidveṣaḥ kriyate kṣaṇāt ||  
  
asthisaṃhāramāgṛhyamatsodarī tathā punaḥ |  
āṣuviḍālayornetramekī kṛtya tu peṣayet ||  
  
śayyāyāmāsane vastre vigrahe cānulepite |  
veṣadveṣo bhaved deyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇāt ||  
  
kuṭajasya tu mūlāni śigru netra yutāni ca |  
sapharī cakṣuṣā yuktaṃ lepanaṃ vairakāraṇaṃ ||  
  
durbhagasya rajo gṛhyaṃ renuṃ mahiṣagardabhāt |  
mṛtakasya tathā puṣpaṃ nārī rajaḥ samanvitaṃ ||  
  
95b)  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi uccāṭana vidhikramaṃ |  
mṛtakasya ca puṣpaṃ ca nirmālyaṃ cailameva ca ||  
  
pretālayāt samāgṛhya yasya gṛhe nidhāpayet |  
aṣṭamyāṃ vā caturdaśyāṃ tatrasyoccāṭanaṃ yataṃ ||  
  
uddhṛtya jāyate śāntiḥ satyametadudāhṛtam |  
rajvāvadhvāhninātasya mṛtakasya śmaśānake ||  
  
rajjunitvākṣipedaṅge gṛhe tasya palāyatam |  
ubhrānta patramādāya vāyu vījaṃ tatolikhet ||  
  
dveṣṭhaṃ nāmalikheddharme māṣī viṣarasena tu |  
uccāṭanakaroyogassatyastatra udāhṛtaḥ ||  
  
kṣipecchatru gṛhe dvāri dehalī mastake budhaḥ |  
uccāṭāṃgapaṭaṃ govānāvākṣiṇaṃ ca mastakaṃ ||  
  
etāni vandhayet pāde vāhau vā vidhṛtaṃ tathā |  
śatrunāmāṅkitaṃ kṛtvā ākāśe prakṣipedbudhaḥ ||  
  
uccāṭana karasadyodyoga saṃvartakoddhṛtaḥ |  
kiṃ na vai mastake pāde athavā khaṃjarīṭake ||  
  
nivandhayed bhūrjapatre saṃpanna dveṣa keśavaṃ |  
tata palāyana kuryāt maṃtreṇānena vā punaḥ ||  
  
oṃ yaṃ yaṃ yaṃ yaṃ yaṃ yaḥ devadatta uccāṭayaḥ |  
nimbapatra bhallapatraṃ puṃnāgasaṃbhavaḥ punaḥ ||  
  
ekīkṛtya gṛhe kṣipte sadya uccāṭakārakaḥ |  
gopure ca tathā śṛṃge hayasthāpiṣure tathā ||  
  
kṛṣṇo ragaśiraḥ kṣiptaṃ gṛhe śatroḥ punaḥ kṣipet |  
satyaṃ uccāṭayatyeṣaḥ sa kuṭuṃvaṃ na śaṃsayaḥ ||  
  
homayogaṃ pravakṣyāmi mahoccāṭanakārakaṃ |  
ye noccāṭanamātreṇa dūradeśāntare vrajet ||  
  
rājikālavaṇaṃ nītvā vījakaraṃjakasya ca |  
udbhrānta kākapakṣe ca ekīkṛtya prayatnataḥ ||  
  
hunedvyāsanake maṃtrī tasya bhasma tu saṃgrahet |  
bhasmamuṣṭiṃ gṛhe kṣiptvā śīghramuccāṭanadvidhaḥ ||  
  
oṃ phaṭ dhavalamukhī svāhā | patraṃ niṃvasya saṃgṛhya ayutaikena saṃyutaṃ |  
  
96a)  
  
tasya saṃlepanaṃ kuryādvayakoṣṭa sarirajaiḥ |  
śatrornāma tato nītvā sa kule tanu bheditaṃ ||  
  
tadbhasma tu samāgṛhya kṣiped vidveṣi maṃdire |  
tasya coccāṭayedvāhyanaṃ kuryātridinena na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
oṃ hu&kūṭayaḥ vāma vāhu ucche vichalacilliṇikarahakaccorarajemokija iti ha ane   
moha devarasaṃ tatage deśāntarasarge śaśyed bhurate uccāṭaye svāhā | anena   
maṃtreṇa villinipakṣa sārdhaṃ śatadvayaṃ hunet agni nibhṛtena etena   
śatroruccāṭanaṃ bhavati |   
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi vidveṣanāma saṃnibhaṃ |  
yena bhakṣitamātreṇa tatkṣaṇātmaraṇaṃ vrajet ||   
  
daṃṣṭrā sā raktakatakhacchedāt pramadāpayet |   
atha bhallātakī yuktaṃ dāpayet madhusarpiṣā ||   
  
tatkṣaṇāt mriyate aṃge śikhāgre viṣasaṃnibhaṃ |  
nilamakṣikamāgṛhya pucchaṃ śṛṃgālakaṃ tathā ||  
  
ekīkṛtya yagedattaṃ viṣamārayate dhruvaṃ |  
gomāyu gṛdhrayorguṃjā kṣiptvā vaktre vidhārayet ||  
  
paścāduddhṛtyatāṃ guṃjāṃ bhakṣaṇe tu pradāpayet |  
jāyaṃte sphoṭakā ghorā viṣamāviṣasaṃnibhāḥ ||  
  
hanīguṃjāphalā caiva taila siddhārtha saṃbhavaṃ |  
khāne pāne pradātavyaṃ śatrormāraṇamuttamaṃ ||  
  
palāsīmūlamādāya kaṭu tailena saṃyutaṃ |  
deva priyasya vījena ekīkṛtya pradāpayet ||  
  
mṛyate nātra saṃdeho yadi śakraḥ svayaṃ bhavet |  
karavīrasiphāsadya siddhārtha tailasaṃyutā ||  
  
mohavījayutāṃ yogaḥ sadyomaraṇakāraṇaṃ |  
sphaṭikī vīja tailena bhakṣayet kanako bhavaṃ ||  
  
bhakṣaṇe dīyate yasya mṛyate nātra saṃśayaḥ |  
dugdhena dīyate yasya jihvā hālāhalasya ca ||  
  
puṭakālaṃ viśeṣeṇa sayātiyamamandiraṃ |  
vajrīkṣīra yutaṃ kṛtvā sūtikā piṣitaṃ pacet ||  
  
96b)  
  
tatkṣaṇāt mṛyate śatrurvahudhā jalpitena kiṃ |  
pūtyaṃ u? kaṭu tailena miśrikṛtya pradāpayet ||  
  
sayo bhakṣaṇamātreṇa na śevai mṛyate dhruvaṃ |  
māṇikyaṃ māṃsaṃ saṃgṛhya kaṭutailena saṃharet ||  
  
bhasmabhakṣaṇamātreṇa mṛyate nātra saṃśayaḥ |  
kṛṣṇā hi dantamūlena hemavījāni bhāvayet ||  
  
khāne pāne pradātavyaṃ śatrumāraṇamuttamaṃ |  
raktacitrakamūlaṃ tu śaṃkhaṭaṃkana cūrṇakaṃ ||  
  
ekīkṛtya pradātavyaṃ tasya vīkīra saṃyutaṃ |  
bhakṣaṇāt mṛyate sadyaḥ puruṣaḥ kāla coditaṃ ||  
  
śavalāhiṃ samāyadāpayet bhakṣaṇe sudhīḥ |  
tatkṣaṇāt mṛyate śatruḥ pratikāro na vidyate ||  
  
vitasti kāmabhakṣaṇe dadyān madhunā saha miśritaṃ |  
sadyo mṛtyumavāpnoti bhakṣako nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
taṃtunā bhakṣayed yastu mayūrajaṭharopitaṃ |  
sadya eva naro yāti anivāryāyamālayaṃ ||  
  
madhuṣarpi samāyuktaṃ yo bhakṣeredekakālataḥ |  
sadyastu mṛyate sākṣāt asādhyastridaśairapi ||  
  
viṣakoṭika tailaṃ tu lavaṇena samanvitaṃ |  
alpāyurbhakṣayedyastu mṛyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
sarpasya vadanaṃ nitvā vyāghrakuṇḍasupeṣitaṃ |  
khāne pāne pradātavyaṃ mṛyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
vyādhasyaṣṭā vanaṃ gṛhya chuchuṃdaryāḥ śakṛntathā |  
karavīra samāyuktaṃ sadyo vai māraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ ||  
  
ete yogāḥ samākhyātā nānā maṃtra samudbhavāḥ |  
sadyaḥ siddhikarāḥ sarve gopanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ||  
  
iti śrīhāhārāvataṃtre athavarṇasaṃhitāyāṃ nānāmaṃtraprayoga   
indrajālapaṭalaḥ ||   
  
śrībhairava uvāca ||  
  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahārogaharaṃparaṃ |  
sadyoroga prasamanaṃ triṣu lokesu viśrutaṃ ||  
  
ādau kuṣṭhaharaṃ samyak kathayāmi samāsataḥ |  
  
97a)  
  
saraṭaḥ ṣaṭpadaścaiva tathā karpaṭavṛścikaḥ |  
cūrṇi kṛtya kiṣipet taila paścādaṃgaṃ tu mardayet ||  
  
aṃga sra?kṣaṇamātreṇa kuṣṭhaṃ saṃ naśyate dhruvaṃ |  
śirasaḥ kṛmīmāgṛhyaḥ tāṃbūlena tu pūrayet ||  
  
mukharogo bhavet tasya hāhārāve prakīrtitaḥ |  
saṃkoca kaṃṭakaṃ gṛhya yasya madhye nidhāpayet ||  
  
tasya saṃjāyate śūlamati ghoraṃ sudāruṇaṃ |  
vanamūṣikaśca mlaviṇī hi haṃsī rūpitaṃ tathā ||  
  
ajitenya parilekhyaṃ svāhāntaṃ praṇavādikaṃ |  
aparājite nyadhobhāge svāhāntaṃ praṇavādikaṃ ||  
  
evaṃ saṃlekhya yaṃtraṃ tu gaccheccaiva śarittaṭe |  
ubhayoḥ kūlayo grāhyā mṛttikā mauninā śubhā ||  
  
tayā gaṇapatiṃ hutvā yaṃtraṃ tasyopari kṣipet |  
godugdhatarpaṇaṃ kuryād gaṇanāthasya sundarī ||  
  
arcayedvahubhiḥ puṣpairmodakairvahubhistutaṃ |  
saṃpūjya vālakānbhakṣairgaṇeśaḥ priyatāmiti ||  
  
evaṃ saṃpūjya deveśaṃ gaṇarājasucī smite |  
sarāva saṃpuṭe kṣiptvā saṃpuṭo parivinyaset ||  
  
aghoreti aghorati vinyaset saṃpuṭopari |  
bhūmisthaṃ saṃpuṭaṃ kṛtvā nikhanyā'tha prapūjayet ||  
  
daurbhāgya maṇḍalaṃ prāpya nārī sadityaharnisuṃ |  
puruṣo na sahetāṃ ca surūpāmapi suvratāṃ ||  
  
puṃliṃga yojitaṃ yaṃtraṃ nānā tu sahate tu tam |  
daṃpatyordveṣaṇe devī rahasyaṃ paramaṃ sadā ||  
  
nānyatra saṃprayoktavyaṃ yaṃtrametat mama priyaṃ |  
na deyaṃ yasya kasyāpi viparītaṃ hi prajāyate ||  
  
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi siddhimaṃtramanuttamaṃ |  
  
oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya yamarūpine kālasaṃkṣepāyaḥ ete saṃhara 2 śatruṃ 2   
nāśaya 2 amukaṃ hana 2 paca 2 ghātaya 2 hu& phaṭ svāhā | anena maṃtreṇa   
ghocaṃtā? yatkiṃcidvarṇamabhimaṃtrya śatravedayātmāraṇaṃ bhavati | oṃ   
namo bhagavate rudrāya   
  
97b)  
  
sarvabhūta hitāya ca sarakṣabhagavān sarvabhagavān devītmutāṃta śīghraṃ kuru 2   
mocaya 2 sarvarudrebhyo namostute svāhā | anena maṃtreṇa pūrvavadukta   
pratyānayanayogānteṣu prayuji tataḥ svastho bhavivati | oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya   
śivarūpine śikhāṃ vandhaya sarvāsāṃ sarveṣāṃ śivamastu vaḥ nara 2 rakṣa 2   
sarvabhūtabhayaṃ kuru 2 muru 2 sarvabhayebhyaḥ svāhā | atha vidyā yogā prayoktī   
tanauśī svāṃvadhnīyādrakṣa bhavati | oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya vyāghracarma   
vāsaḥ saṃniṣasmāya muktāṭṭahāsāya mana 2 satyaṃ kṛt saṃnidhiṃ kuru 2 sasa   
2 dhara 2 svāhā | idaṃ maṃtraṃ savotsādana yogeṣu prayogaṃ kārayennaraḥ |   
evametena yogena śāntirbhavati nānyathā | oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya   
karālarūpiṇe pracaṇḍāyoccāṭaya amukasya mūlaṃ vandha 2 mara 2 daha 2 paca 2   
śighraṃ muccāṭayā hi hu& phaṭ svāhā |   
  
anena maṃtreṇa aṣṭottarāvadhi śatena maṃtritaṃ kṛtvā sarvamuccāṭayati   
kākolūkasya pakṣaṃ tu homena tatkṣaṇā muccāṭayati | oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya   
gara 2 dara 2 bhaṃja 2 kuru 2 moṭaya 2 nagaramaṇḍala patirājñā pacati svāhā |   
anena maṃtreṇa dūṣitāyo hi malaṣṭa satābhimaṃtritaṃ kṛtvā prakṣiped   
goroyacchamudakastaṃ bhavati | viṣonirviṣo bhavati | ataḥ paramaṃ janāni bhavati |   
  
jaṃvūkasya ca varāhasya netranāśā tathaiva ca |   
  
eteṣāṃ ca samāhṛtya matrāṇi rudhiraṃ tathā |  
ādyodyajanamevāsi samaṃ saṃgṛhya samuddharet ||  
  
anenāṃjita netrastu adṛśo bhavati kṣaṇāt |  
ulūkasya ca gṛddhasya tathā mārjāra varāhayoḥ ||  
  
eteṣāṃ netramādāya śrotāṃjanasamanvitaṃ |  
sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ kṛtaṃ sarvamaṃtraṇe yoge cakṣuṣī ||  
  
paśyate dirghamāraghonaṃ rātrau paśyed yathā divā |  
śṛṃgārasyātha vā gṛddhasya mahiṣasya viḍālayoḥ ||  
  
kākaśūkaraṃ yoścaiva netrāṇi tu samāharet |  
srotāṃjanasamāyuktamaṃjayeccakṣuṣīvaraḥ ||  
  
98a)  
  
anenāṃjita netrastu rātrau paśyed yathā divā |  
  
eteṣāṃ yogānāṃ maṃtraḥ |  
  
oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya śivāya jyotiṣānan daso diśa bhavatu svāhā |   
  
ekarāṣito bhūtvā kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ samāhitaḥ |  
kṛtvā pūjāṃ yathāvidhiṃ ekaliṃgamāsthite ||  
  
dyotamāna ca tasyaiva vā pādena dālapidvigāhayet |?  
śmaśāne nirdaheccaiva kharamūteṇa nidhāpayet ||  
  
tamevāgāraṃ saṃgṛhya alaktaṃka saṃpuṭa |  
kāyo nāma ca likhet yasya satvareṇa gṛhyena vā ||  
  
oṃ kāka kṛṣṇājinaṃ amukasya jvaraṃ nāśaya svāhā |   
jaṃvūkavṛkṣamāruhya ayutaṃ japet tat siddho bhavati || oṃ cāmuṇḍe kha 2 khāhi   
2 amukaṃ gṛhe na gṛhāpaya svāhā | anena maṃtreṇa mānuṣasya kapālaṃ   
gṛhya cūrṇī kṛtya cāmuṇḍāyai dhūpaṃ dīyate |   
  
yasya nāmnā saṃgṛhya gṛhyate gugguladhūpena mokṣaḥ |  
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi pādapracāraṇamuttamaṃ ||  
  
sitāyākākajaṃghāyā mūlaṃ saṃgṛhya buddhimān |  
tasya rasaṃ tu saṃgṛhya tila tailena pācayet ||  
  
auṣṭacarma upānākhyaṃ kṛtvā tamabhimaṃtrayet |  
te naivābhyajā tailena yadhyo pāde vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
sarvasibhujavo bhūtvā gavāṃ sthāne nivartayet |  
siddholūkavasā caiva auṣṭacarma upānahet ||  
  
paṃcayojanaṃ gatvā tu punarasāṃtāni vartate |  
bhavate nātra saṃdeho uḍḍīsasya vaco yathā ||  
  
oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya nānā vadacalena cala 2 svāhā |   
  
caturbhuktodhito bhūtvā kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ samāhitaḥ |  
devamabhyarcamīśānaṃ valiṃ dadyād vidhānataḥ ||  
  
vāyavyadiśamaśrito tailāni abhimaṃtrayet |  
tatastu jāyate siddhi uḍḍisasya vaco yathā ||  
  
aṣṭau sahasrameteṣāṃ pūrvameva vidhiyate |  
  
98b)  
  
sarveṣāmeva yogānāṃ sādhanaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ ||  
  
oṃ namo bhagavate rudrāya jñāpaya velāpathacāriṇe aparimita parākramāyakini   
svāhā |   
  
sauvarṇagiri karpāsi kaṭu tailasya saṃkhayā |  
vasāmākṣika saṃyuktaṃ sarvamekatra kārayet ||  
  
kaṭukānyasya saṃgṛhya alakṣitaṃ tu sthāpayet |  
abhimaṃtrā tatastailamāvartyāṣṭa śatāni tu ||  
  
abhyaṃga pādamukhāt sa gached yojanaṃ śataṃ |  
punaḥ khekṣipraṃmrīte saravairo nivartate ||  
  
mṛtakṛkalāsa cūrṇaṃ kṛtya sarāvasaṃpuṭe |  
nidhūmata dahemagnau siddhārthaṃsita cūrṇaṃdaṃ ||  
  
miśrabhasmagṛhītaṃ tu yasya gṛhe vinikṣipet |  
tato mānuṣyanāṃ caiva mohitā bhavati sadā ||  
  
tadeva cūrṇaṃ yasya pāda pāṃśumiśritaṃ saptabhi maṃtritaṃ pathe niṣānayet |  
tadeva cūrṇaṃ ātmendriya miśritaṃ yasmai dadāti sa vaśo bhavati ||  
  
tadeva cūrṇaṃ gośṛṅge prakṣipya nikhanedyasya ṣaṃḍho bhavati |   
tadeva cūrṇaṃ gorocana miśritaṃ tilakaṃ kṛtvā rājapriyo bhavati ||  
  
oṃ namo rudrāya udyādana hana 2 daha 2 paca 2 amukaśīghraṃ vaśamānaya   
svāhā |   
  
kāsmaryāmūlasya gṛhya savarakusumaṃ ketakī sa lakṣaṇaṃ piṣṭvā sa   
bhṛṃgaṃ triphalā yuktaṃ sa tailamācamya ca tasokṣme lohaṃ pradadyā īmaṃ   
valitalagasmā samakasthitaṃ | keśākāsaprakāśaṃ bhramarakulanibhaṃ   
tatkṣaṇādeva kuryāt | aṃjanaṃ padmamūlaṃ nīlotpalamathāpi vā |   
ayoraṃjabhṛṃga rājaṃ patraṃ savarasya ca | etattu kāyike bhaṃge rasataṃ kātha   
saṃyutaiḥ tailasya kuḍavaṃ gṛhya sasairmṛdvagninā pacet | māsārdhe   
kṛśarāhāronasyametat pradāpayet | tataḥ pāda same divase niyataṃ   
kṛṣṇamūrdhvajaḥ | kumāraśca kṣumedhārvā mukhe notpala gaṃdhinā |  
  
99a)  
  
jīvedvarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ valīpalīta varjitaḥ |  
ādāya tila puṣpāṇi sarpirhayakṣaraṃ tathā ||  
  
madhunā saha saṃyuktaṃ śiro lepaṃ pradāpayet |  
lepenānena jāyante keśāhasta taleṣvapi ||  
  
utpalaṃ payasā yuktaṃ māṃsaṃ bhūmau nidhāpayet |  
snehena palitaptaṃ ca keśānāṃ paramaṃjanaṃ ||  
  
utpalāni tilāḥ kuṣṭhaṃ yaṣṭīmadhukameva ca |  
snehena palitaptaṃ ca keśānāṃ raṃjanaṃ paraṃ ||  
  
nāgacūrṇaṃ tataḥ kuryāt mukhtā? cāpi rasāṃjanaṃ |  
anena keśā jāyanta cūrṇaṃ pāda taleṣvapi ||  
  
nīlotpalamusīlaṃ ca candanaṃ nāgakeśaraṃ |  
śāli vā nakha kuṣṭaṃ ca ajakṣīreṇa pācayet ||  
  
tailameti vipakvantu romaraṃjanamuttamaṃ |  
triphalānimva vījāni vacācotpala sāri vā ||  
  
bhṛṃgamadhuka saṃyuktaṃ lohacūrṇaṃ tilasya ha |  
ājamāhiṣa gavyādi navanītaṃ samāharet ||  
  
lohabhāṇḍe samāloḍyamāsaṃ bhūmau nidhāpayet |  
anenamakṣaṇācchīrṣerdanāarddharoma saṃbhavet ||  
  
paritīnikaromaṃ ca vadhirāṃ savṛconnayet |  
nīlakeśīkasaṃdhanya?taṃḍūlaiḥ sarvataṃ dahe ||  
  
chiroveṣṭitayā taṃtu kṛṣṇataṃḍula sarvatu |  
dahe chirovisthita pātaṃ tu kṛṣṇa taṇḍula sarvatu ||  
  
dahecchrirovisthitapāta kṛṣṇaḥ syāttriphalākṣikaḥ |  
manaśilā ca tailaṃ ca keśāni gukṣayetmahaṃ ||  
  
pṛkārānāsane śreṣṭaṃ keśānāṃ ca vivardhanaṃ |  
bhallātakaṃ viḍaṃgāni rajasela mayorajaḥ ||  
  
sauvaccalasamāyuktaṃ tilān kṛṣṇāstu dāpayet |  
kalkavānavaśirolepānnirmale sthāpayet tataḥ ||  
  
mūrdhataścaiva vadhvā tu keśānāṃ raṃjanaṃ paraṃ |  
kākahṛdayā sa triphalā bhṛṃgarājarasāni tu ||  
  
tulyabhāgāni etāni lepanaṃ tu tathaikatā |  
tailamebhirvipacyaṃ tu keśānāṃ dīrghakārakaṃ ||  
  
kuṭilākarāstathā keśāḥ karṇotpala samaṃnibhāḥ |  
  
99b)  
  
oṃ kṣipanī utpathasya patha muṃca 2 svāhā |   
  
udakoparijāpyasyedeyaṃ sukhena prasūyate |  
bhuvanasya ca mūlāni śvetaguṃjāyutaṃ tathā ||  
  
samabhāgāni madhunā yoni lepāni sā mukhe |  
sobhanaṃ janayet putraṃ balavīryasamanvitaṃ ||  
  
nīlapuṣpamayāmārgaṃ saunikaṃ cītrakaṃ tathā |  
vacākuṣṭasamāyuktaṃ pītvā nārī prasūyate ||  
  
alāvuvījagopitaṃveta saṃrajani dvayaṃ |  
adho puṣpī vacā vāsā candanāṃścaiva peṣayet ||  
  
etena yonimālepya maithunaṃ ca nisevayet |  
putraṃ janayate hṛdyaṃ yādṛśaṃ manasaḥ priyaṃ ||  
  
prasthaṃ pṛthaga gomūtrasya tailasya kuḍavaśya cet |  
ṛtu snātāpi cennārī api vaṃdhyā prasūyate ||  
  
akṣimahiṣagarbhinyā avimūtraśatāvarī |  
sama bhāgāni sarvāṇi ajasarpiḥ samanvitaṃ ||  
  
ṛtusnātāpī cennārī api vandhyā prasūyate |  
śuklapakṣe vaṭachukta puṣpa yoga samanvitaṃ ||  
  
ṛtusnātāṃbhasā pitvā nārī garbhavatī bhavet |  
aśvagandhakaprāyeta kvathitaṃ sītalaṃ payaḥ ||  
  
pitvā ṣātrā samāśleṣādapi vandhyā prasūyate |  
vījapūraka vījāni cūrṇaṃ vā nāgakeśaraṃ ||  
  
pitvā yenāmamādagarbharatau yāhi samāśrayet |  
śarkarotpalayaṣṭāṃgī raktacandanaśarivā ||  
  
sravamāneṣu garbheṣu yojyaṃ tandula kāriṇā |  
padmotpalasya mūlāni madhukaṃ śarkarāstilāḥ ||  
  
savamāneṣu garbheṣu garbhasthāpanamuttamaṃ |  
  
iti garbhasthāpanam |  
  
madhukaṃ candanaṃ caiva sarpiṣamāmeva ca |  
gūḍha garbhāpi cennārī kṣiprameva prasūyate ||  
  
ājarūḍhasya mūlāni nābhiṃ yoniṃ pralepayet |  
liptamātrā tu yā nārī kṣiprameva prasūyate ||  
  
puṣpena cāturaṃ mūlaṃ pṛṣṇiparṇyāḥ samāhitaḥ |  
  
100a)  
  
visalpakaraṇe harṣe gūḍhagarbhe prasaśpte? ||  
  
panasūrasya patrasya nābhiṃ kalpena lepayet |  
nābhilepa prasiddhārthaṃ garbhasthasya prakarṣaṇaṃ ||  
  
aparāpātane garbhe pippalyādi rajaḥ kṣipet |  
śālimūlākṣa mātraṃ vā pūrvādamlena vā punaḥ ||  
  
kaluṣasya ca mūlena lāṃgulyā vā vṛṣena ca |  
piṣṭena gṛddha sabhāryā yoniṃ nābhiṃ ca lepayet ||  
  
paṃcamūlasya nikvāthaṃ taptalohena saṃyutaṃ |  
sūtikāroganāśāya pivedvātaditāluyā ||

nisvakāṣṭasya dhūpena dhūpayitvā bhagaṃ tathā ||  
  
maithunaṃ yānisaṃvena sā prasūyeta mānuṣi |  
palāśasyāṃkuraṃ yāme peyatpuṣpadaśame dine ||  
  
śravate garbhanārīnāṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā |  
lohitapittatagaramaricaṃ pipalī samaṃ ||  
  
etāni samabhāgāni madhunā yoni lepayet |  
divālepamidaṃ kṛtvā rātrau mithuna gāminī ||  
  
bhagena lubhate nārī poṣīnnityaṃ? prasūyate |  
gośṛṃgaṃ vṛhati bhogaṃ sahadevīṃ priyaṃgukaṃ ||  
  
mayūrāṇḍarasāṃścaiva ekatra paripeṣayet |  
etena yonimālepya maithunaṃ yāni secate ||  
  
tāsāṃ dhārayataṃ garbha yadi parākrama prajā |  
vatigairikasyākṣamātrapiṇḍamālepya snāpayet ||  
  
tiṣya nakṣatrapānena yoni gacchati prasūyate |  
gairikaṃ ca haridrāṃ ca śūkṣmalepā pradāpayet ||  
  
atikrānta tṛtīye tu garbhanāśanamuttamaṃ |  
piṣṭaṃ lāṃgalīkāmūlaṃ kulastho?dakasaṃyutaṃ ||  
  
pānaṃ ca sahatīkṣṇena garbhanāśanamuttamaṃ |  
  
iti garbhanāśanaṃ |  
  
citrakasya tu mūlāni kvāthayet mṛdunāgninā |  
bhagaṃ prakṣālayet tena gāḍhatvamupagacchati ||  
  
saurāṣṭri khādiraṃ cūrṇaṃ kvāthayet mṛdunāgninā |  
  
100b)  
  
bhagaṃ prakṣālitaṃ tena gāḍhatvamupajāyate ||  
  
śaṃkhapuṣpīvacāmāṃsī somarāji tathaiva ca |  
navanīte māhiṣakalke gāḍhi karaṇamuttamaṃ ||  
  
tuṃvā patraṃ ca lodhraṃ ca samabhāgāni kārayet |  
dadyāllepaṃ bhagasyadaṃ prabhṛtādhyakṣyatāṃ bhavet ||  
  
yā purohakaṃ cūrṇena bhagamālepayet sadā |  
maithunaṃ tu nisecetaḥ punaḥ kāmyo bhaviṣyati ||  
  
padmena tu tamālena cūrṇaṃ kṛtvā vicakṣaṇaḥ |  
ajākṣīreṇa tatpiṣṭvā guṭikāṃ kārayed budhaḥ ||  
  
daśarātraṃ prasūtā tu yonyāṃ prakṣipyakanyavat? |  
kaumāraṃ vrajate bhāvaṃ yogenānena nityasaḥ ||  
  
palāśoduṃbaraphalaṃ tilataila samanvitam |  
madhunā yoni mālipya gāḍhikaraṇamuttamaṃ ||  
  
iti gāḍhikaraṇaṃ |  
  
mātuluṃgarasaṃkṣaudra aṃjanaṃ kaṇṭhakālikā |  
leparājaṃ pacedena strī cittotmādakālikā ||  
  
koṣṭhikārakrimikuṣṭha viṣṭhaṃ pārāvatasya ca |  
madhuśiriṣavījāni lepoyaṃ smaranāṃtikaṃ ||  
  
dvāvetau leparājānau pradyumne nāvatāritau |  
garbhitā strīṇāmājaṃsinmikaṃ? vyugni sadā ||?  
  
aṃjanaṃ nāgapuṣpaṃ ca devadāru ca śarkarā |  
marīce dvevacākuṣṭhaṃ hastimūtreṇa peṣayet ||  
  
etat pānaṃ pradātavyaṃ yā nārī garbhitā bhavet |  
śatapuṣpaṃ tathā kṣaudraṃ ketakī vṛhatī phalaṃ ||  
  
eṣaḥ lepaḥ prayoktavyo vaśīkaraṇamuttamaṃ |  
sayyādo priyaṃguṃ ca tagare padmakeśaraṃ ||  
  
gomūtraṃ peṣayed yena madhunā saha lepayet |  
lepasvataṃ gāḍhānāṃ vandhakīnāṃ sukhāvahaḥ ||  
  
pippalī saindhavaṃ kuṣṭaṃ sendhavaṃ lavanaṃ tathā |  
manaḥśilā samāyuktaṃ lepoyaṃ maraṇāntitaṃ ||  
  
101a)  
  
pippaliṃ taṃdulaṃ caiva madhumadhukameva ca |  
kapikacchurasaṃyuktaṃ lepoyaṃ maraṇāṃtikaṃ ||  
  
kanakavījaniryāsaṃ madhu pippali taṃḍulaṃ |  
vārtākarasasaṃyuktaṃ lepoyaṃ maraṇātikaṃ ||  
  
oṃ naṭe kucaṭe svakinī svāhā |   
  
brahmadaṃḍī dadhirasapippalīmarīcānī ca |  
eṣalepaḥ prayoktavyāḥ nārīnāṃ hṛdayā kulaḥ ||  
  
oṃ caṃcabhā devīra namostute svāhā |   
  
ātmanastu bhavedduktaṃ ātmakarṇa malāstathā |  
ātmanaṃ ca bhavet śukraṃ phenasyāpi samaṃ bhavet ||  
  
annapānaphalapuṣpaṃ gandhavastra tathaiva ca |  
garbhitāyai pradātavyaṃ vase tiṣṭhati kiṃkaraḥ ||  
  
udbhāntapatraṃ bhramarasya pakṣaṃ dvaurājadaṃttau mṛtakasya mālyam |  
etana nārī sahacūrṇi tāṃgī pathe pathe tiṣṭati rodamānā ||  
  
puṣkarasva tu vījāni pippalī taṃḍulaṃ sadā |  
aṃjanaṃ dhāva puṣpaṃ ca manu vā pānamuttamaṃ ||  
  
ajāmūtraṃ gatamadaṃ pippalīśāli vā madhuḥ |  
garbhitāyai pradātavyaṃ nārīnāṃ pānamuttamaṃ ||  
  
gorocanāḥ kulatyaṃ ca vilvapeśī manaḥśilā |  
etāḥ sarvāsamīkṛtya prakṣipettāmra bhājane ||  
  
saptarātrasthitaṃ tatra tailamenajācayet |  
tattailaṃ bhagasālipya bhaktīramanu gacchati ||  
  
prāptamaithunabhāvā tu patiṃ dāsaṃ kariṣyati |  
kuṃkumaṃ śatapuṣpaṃ ca priyaṃguṃ dve ca locane ||  
  
aśvamūtra samāyuktaṃ avasānāṃ vaśaṃkarī |  
māttuluṃga phalaṃ grāhya soṣayitvā viśeṣataḥ ||  
  
lavanaṃ yacca sāmudraṃ cūrṇaṃ tu tatra saṃnyaset |  
saptarātraṃ caraccaiva ātmamūtreṇa bhāvayet ||  
  
sarāvasaṃpuṭaṃ kṛtvā aṃtardhūmena dāhayet |  
catuṣpathe śmaśāne vā etallavanamuttamaṃ ||  
  
yasya dīyate sa vaśo bhavati nātra saṃśayaḥ |  
  
101b)  
  
oṃ namo bhagavati prītirī svāhā |  
  
svānajihvā vacākuṣṭaṃ mṛtanirmālyameva ca |  
etatmaṃtrasamāyuktamavaśānāṃ vaśaṃkarī ||  
  
oṃ vacakutrāya? svāhā |  
  
aṃjanaṃ haritālaṃ ca vacākuṣṭhaṃ tathaiva ca |  
sūkṣmacūrṇamidaṃ kṛtvā vaśīkaraṇamuttamaṃ ||  
  
oṃ kuṭu 2 svāhā |  
  
etaccūrṇaṃ saptāhaṃ parijāpya strīṇāṃ deyācettonmādakārakaṃ |   
pāsvatapurīṣaṃ ca indragopaṣkarasāṃjanān guggulu tvaktakhaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ vījāni   
kanakasya tu |

dhūpoyaṃ sarvabhāṇḍānāṃ lābhaviṃkraya kārakaṃ ||  
  
oṃ cili 2 mili 2 puttalīke vaśamānaya svāhā |   
  
indrayavaṃ vacāṃ kuṣṭhaṃ tagaraṃ sarpapaṃstathā |  
sūlā nāgapuṣpaṃ ca bhāgaṃ sarjarasasya ca ||  
  
etena dhūpitā patyā śighraṃ gacchati vikriyāṃ |  
durbhagānāṃ ca nārīnāṃ yā nārī na prasūyati ||  
  
saṃgrāme kalahe dhūte? strīṣu rājakuleṣu ca |  
nityaṃ dhūpitamātmāna yadicchedātmanojayaṃ ||  
  
pathyāṃ kṛṣṇavidaṃgayā dhātṛ tailaṃ saśarkarā |  
sarpi taila yutaṃ khādaṃ jalayonābhi bhūyate ||  
  
lohacūrṇaṃ sa viśveta tilān  kṛṣṇayutaṃ yutaṃ |  
dārvī lepaḥ kasoyaṃ syāttriphalājorajastathā ||  
  
vārāhī mūla cūrṇasya śatamadhutattathā |  
kṣīreṇamudgapūṃpena jāṃgalena rasena vā ||  
  
rasāyaṃ nārthinā nityaṃ bhoktavyaṃ śāliṣaṣṭike |  
iṣa kṛṣṇasitopetān yaḥ khādyati tilān svayaṃ ||  
  
puṃsānasya bhavecchardī śukrañcāpi na vekṣayaḥ |  
śatāvarī ghṛtaṃ musta lehaṃ śarkarayā yutaṃ ||  
  
rasamānasya pavatī saṃmṛdutā yonettī yaḥ |  
tilamāṣavidārīnāṃ cūrṇaṃ piṣṭvā suśobhanaṃ ||  
  
rasairikṣurasaikvāpi ucāraṇī hu& svāhā |  
ātmasūtrañca jaṭā kṛtvā anāmikākaṃḍa vāraṇā ||  
  
102a)  
  
karṇabhogātadantā ca sarvametacca vardhate |  
aśvagandhaṃ tilacūrṇaṃ caṃdanaṃ caiva pīṣayet ||  
  
sarṣapaiḥ sahitaṃ kīklaṃ karṇavandhaṃ na sūtakaṃ |  
navanītaṃ vacāmūlaṃ pāsīsaṃ kuru vai pacet ||  
  
padmapatragatāṃ kāṃcalepayet pramadā tanuṃ |  
atha parvata vidāraṇa karmaṇa kramamājñāpayāmi ||  
  
oṃ mahāsenāya mahāvalaparākramāya mahāvināyakāya bhūmividāranāya   
śaktidharāya vidārayan sarvayaṃtraṃ matha 2 tarjaya 2 cūrṇaya 2 pātaya 2 svāhā |   
anena mantreṇa sarṣapamājuramaṃḍikātiyaṃ vajra sūci rākī? kṛtvā   
saptābhimaṃtritaṃ kṛtvā parvataṃ tāḍayet | atha bhūmi vidāraṇa karmakāra   
anena maṃtra vidhānena bhūmiṃ tāḍayet vidārayati | prāsādabhavyā na kartuṃ   
kramaḥ ||  
  
oṃ thaṃ lokāya svāhā |   
  
mṛttikāvalmikaścaiva sarveṣāṃ sahitaṃ tathā |   
saptavāramidaṃ jāpyaṃ tāḍayet prāsādaṃ tatra cūrṇitaṃ bhavati ||  
  
hālāhalasya lāṃgulaṃ karaviraṃ sa citrakaṃ |  
māṣikāmarkaṭī caiva svetā ca gṛhaghodhikā ||  
  
athavā sarvaśāstrāṇi pralepaṃ samudāhṛtaṃ |  
etaicchinnānarāmūlaṃ tūrṇaṃ gacchedayamālayaṃ ||  
  
chuchuṃdarīṃ kṛṣṇasarpaṃ markaṭaṃ darduraṃ tathā |  
hastāhela svatasanābhaṃ kṛkalāsaṃ ca lohitaṃ ||  
  
tāḍalepaṃ pravaktavyaṃ hariṇī laye tu mṛte |  
anena piṣṭhamānastṛ mṛyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
sveta karavīrasya mūlaṃ patraṃ tvacaṃ tathā |  
chuchuṃdarī kṛṣṇasahyaṃ ca madanasya phalāni ca ||  
  
hālāhalasya markaṭasya tathā paṭvindumeva ca |  
etāni samabhāgāni lu?hīkṣīreṇa peṣayet ||  
  
eṣaḥ kāṇḍa viṣaṃ proktaṃ śatrūnāśaṃ vimardanaḥ |  
vidāyatena kāṃḍenadabhānikhaṃḍasannipātanepi saḥ ||  
  
102b)  
  
sarve te nidhanaṃ yāṃti agnidagdhā ivadrumāḥ |  
kṛṣṇasarpaṃsitāṃpiṣṭaṃ pacāso valikā tathā ||  
  
chuchuṃdarī pade sāṣṭau caṣīgṛhagodhikā |  
kṛkalā sa padānyaṣṭau nvagrāhayet ||  
  
lāṃgalīkanavanaṃ daṃḍa phalāsaḥ prakīrtitāḥ |  
etāsodhita kalkaṃ ca śrutvānaka samanvitaṃ ||  
  
gṛhītvā sarvaśāstrāṇi pralepoya padāhṛta |  
vidhāyamanujā śastre prayāṃti yamamaṃdiraṃ ||  
  
kūpavāpītaḍāgānāṃ jalame tena dūṣayet |  
yadi tasya ca dūṣanīyaṃ tathā vakṣyāmi taśṛṇu ||  
  
yasthe kūpo pradātavyaṃ vācyoceva caturgulaṃ |  
  
yaḥ pivet salilaṃ tasya sa gacchedayamadhānikāṃ |  
saraṭaṃ vāyasaṃkūṭaṃ markaṭaṃ cūrṇayet tathā ||  
  
etat yogaṃ pradātavyaṃ bhakṣayeta pradāpayet |  
tata suṣyaṃti gātrāṇi sphuṭaṃti śataso hataṃ ||  
  
pratyānayanavarjitaṃ |  
  
ulūkamastakaṃ gṛhītvā lavanātha pūrayet |  
sthāpayedbhājane tāmre saptāhantu vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
vibhītakasya kāṣṭhena ardhūmena dāhayet |  
tato lavanaṃ ca saṃgṛhya ripau dadyādvicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
unmatto bhavate kṣipraṃ yadi na kriyate kriyā |  
dhibhītakanicatyā jāyate cakṣuṣi ||   
  
iti pratyānayanaṃ ||  
  
mātulī mātuluṃgānī vṛścikāni tathaiva ca |  
hālāhalaviṣaṃ caiva cūrṇaṃ kṛtvā vicakṣaṇaḥ ||  
  
yāne bhakṣe pradātavyaṃ sarvaśatru vināśanaṃ |  
chuchuṃdarī tilāṃścaiva kaṭutailāṃśca mūlaka ||  
  
māse naiva tu taṃ pakṣā bhaved dadyādripo naraḥ |  
māsakena navame gulmaṃ śūlaṃśca jāyate viṣān ||  
  
mayūraṃ karkaṭaṃ māṃsinī tathā hariṇameva ca |  
pippalī śṛṃgaveraṃ ca higusau varcalaṃ tathā ||  
  
103a)  
  
dīpaṃ ca mūlasaṃyuktaṃ kvāthaṣecca vicakṣaṇaḥ |  
etena bhuktimātreṇa śūlamutpādya yojayet ||  
  
vījapūrakaḥ kastūrīkā puṣkarameva ca |  
sauvarcala samāyuktaṃ pratyānayanamuttamaṃ ||  
  
dadyācca śatrave śīghraṃ jalodaravimardanaṃ |  
caturbhirmāsai mriyate yadi na kriyate kriyā ||  
  
dadyāt tasya surārthāya matsyaṃ virohitaṃ budhaḥ |  
vījaṃ puṣkarasoyetaṃ tena saṃpadyate sukhaṃ ||  
  
bhojanaṃ ca pradātavyaṃ jāṃgale narasenaṃ vā |  
kṣīpokṣītvāgasīmūlaṃ sarṣaka ca pasyakasya ca ||  
  
tikṣṇe na sahapātena garbhachidrakaraṃ paraṃ |  
gairikaṃ mātraṃ tu yuvatī puṣpadaṃsanaṃ pivet ||  
  
yā nārī karṣabhānaprasūte kadācana |   
  
niṃvakāṣṭhadhūpena dhūpayitvā kṣauni tasya maithuna sauvasyāḥ |   
  
sānaprasūte kadācana |  
  
bhallātakarasaṃguṃjā tathā maṃḍalakārikāṃ ||  
  
gṛhagodhāsamāyuktaṃ gandhaṃ dadyācca yo naraḥ |  
saptāhājjāyate kuṣṭhaṃ jāyaṃte tīvra vedanāḥ ||  
  
dhātṛpadi samāyuktaṃ śarkarāṃ nimbameva ca |  
kṣīreṇa kvāthayitvā tu dadyātprāsanakaṃ ripau ||  
  
aṣṭame hanyatāt taṃ vaikuṣṭhe nā chrīyate ripoḥ |  
  
pūrvoktena pratyā nayanaṃ kārayet ||  
  
kukuṭamāṃsaṃ godaṃtanmatsyamāṃsaṃstathaiva ca |  
ahinī mocakaṃ caiva tailatailena pācayet ||  
  
ahinīrmocakaṃ caiva tilatailasamanvitaṃ |  
śasyomaṃ ca prayogaṃ ca tasya pānena dāpayet ||  
  
hṛdogajāyate tasya śūlaṃ caiva mudāhṛtaṃ |  
tasya śāntiṃ pravakṣyāmi yena saṃpadyate sukhaṃ ||  
  
mayūraṃ kukkuṭamāṃsaṃ bhakṣyaṃ tasya prapeṣayet |  
ghṛtena sahasaṃyuktaṃ purārogaṃ ca nāśanaṃ ||  
  
jalā hi vadanaṃ gṛhya śoṣayitvā prayatnataḥ |  
tasya muke nikṣipeta sa nābhaṃ ca mahāviṣaṃ ||  
  
103b)  
  
dīyate yasyabho sarva viṣaṃ cāpi ca yodita |  
tatkṣaṇānmṛyate śatruriti śāstrasya niścayaḥ ||  
  
prāsāda mṛttikāṃ gṛhya ahivaktre tu niḥkṣipet |  
vadhniyāt kṛṣṇasūtreṇa tato mārganirodhitaḥ ||  
  
pratyānayanamicchaṃti chālayecca śanaiḥ śanaiḥ |  
mṛttikā sudhitaṃ mārkṣakā pṛṣṇuhalaṃ kurukasya ca ||  
  
samabhāgāni sarvāṇi cūrṇaṃbhiṣak pradāpayet |  
narābhuktāmana chaṃdayati vinasyeti vachurādhayadi na kriyate kriyā |   
kṣīraśarkarātre pivet carinimba patrāṇi bilvapatraṣoḍaśapatra ṣoḍaśabhallātakī   
tathā nyaṣṭau viṃśati tathā |  
  
etaccūrṇī kṛtaṃ deyaṃ bhakṣo na pāne viśeṣataḥ |  
mayūramāṃsaṃ dahilāvya tathā bhṛtīrekākṣinī ca ||  
  
etaddeyaṃ bhakṣaṇe pāne pradāpayet |  
saptāhād bhavedvyādhistasyatīvrā vedanā ||  
  
ulūkasya hṛdayaṃ varāhasya jihvā samanvitaṃ |  
ehibhili vipācayet tene liṃpet svagātrāṇi yasya mardayet ||  
  
tasya kimīti suprajāyate dinatrayena vinaśyati |  
ajākṣīraṃ gavāṃ sarpi jyaṣṭhī madhu samanvitaṃ ||  
  
etat pāne pradātavyaṃ pratyānayanamuttamaṃ |  
śūkarasya tu māṃsāni śaśakasya na kulasya ca ||  
  
samabhāgaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā gajamūtreṇa peṣayet |  
varamātraṃ pramāṇena guṭikāṃ kārayed budhaḥ ||  
  
teṣāṃ madhye na guṭikāṃ prāgīye ca nikarṣayet |  
sasya dadyādimaṃ pāne paṃcarātre vyatikrānte pāṇḍurogena chādyate ||  
  
māsaikena mṛyate kriyate yadi na kriyā |  
lohacurṇaṃ ca gomūtraṃ saptāhāṃ chādayet tataḥ ||  
  
tena bhūṣita mātreṇa tatra saṃpadyate sukhaṃ |  
sarpanirmocanā hiṃgupittaṃ vai nakulasya ca ||  
  
104a)  
  
pāne yasya pradātavyaṃ gala roge bhaveddhruvam |  
amṛtā īśvarī mūlaṃ vacāmaṃkoca pratikāpānaṃ tasya pradāpayet ||  
  
kṛṣṇaścāpuriṣaṃ ca mūlaṃ lāṃgalikasya ca |  
vatsanābhaviṣaṃ caiva śvetaśvānasya grāhayet ||  
  
etad cūrṇaṃ kṛtvā sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ budhaḥ |  
gajānāṃ tathā vādi mahiṣagavāṃ spṛṣya mātreṇa nātra kāryāvicāraṇā ||  
  
athānāt saṃpravakṣyāmi sarveṣāṃ viṣanāśanaṃ |  
yatra sthitaṃ kāritaṃ vā yasya cūrṇaṃ prayacchati ||  
  
gehagodhāyāmapūrasya varāhasya māṃsajaṃ |  
etatsaṃgṛhyavasāṃ samaste candramānotī parīpeṣayet ||  
  
puṣpārke cattathā mūlaṃ hastārke vāpi peṣayet |  
kanyāyāṃ ca gatā madhye śuci śukle ca vāsasā ||  
  
peyamānastatakalka maṃtramena mudīrayet |  
  
oṃ namaḥ puruṣasiddhāya paviṣṭaye namaḥ |  
  
sarvādhipataye agadeśa vidhānāya kuru 2 āsurī tusāyadharmamadharatiṣṭhati 2   
svāhā |   
  
anenaliptamātreṇarānāṃ saṃvājinaṃ |  
sarve te nirviṣabhātti uḍīśasya vaco yathā ||  
  
atha śiraḥ stusya sauvarṇasya ca māsata |  
tayaṃ nyanatakte doguṇākṣatena nārcayet ||  
  
saptāhe ca tatotite ānayecca prayatnataḥ |  
chāyāśuṣkaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā lepo yasya pradāpayet ||  
  
bhakṣayet yastato śṛṃga tasya manayī bhavati |   
visphoṭañca jāyate saptāhena mṛyate dhruvaṃ ||  
  
śirīṣapuṣpa mūlaṃ ca phaṃlaṃ ca tvak tathaiva ca |  
  
ebhirdravyai vimiśrayet |  
  
candanapadmakeśaraṃ deva dārugirīkarṇikā |  
siṃdhuvāra tathā sainyaṃ karkaṭīṃ ca pradāpayet ||  
  
etāni samabhāgāni chāgamūtreṇa peṣayet |  
  
104b)  
  
vadaramātrapumānena guṭikāṃ kārayet tataḥ ||  
  
pāne khānet pradātavyaṃ tena saṃpadyate sukhaṃ |  
bhojanasya pradātavyaṃ śālibhaktaṃ ghṛtaṃ payaḥ ||  
  
yaṣṭī madhughṛtaṃ kṣaudraṃ māne tasya pradāpayet |  
saptarātrāt pramucyeta purābhairava kīrtitā ||  
  
lūtāmarkaṭaguṃjā ca tathā puṃchaṃ kṛkalāśasyasitaṃ tathā |  
vabhavā gṛhagodhāpi sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ kṛtvā pradāpayet ||  
  
tāṣṭāsta phalena vā bhaveta ||   
  
guṃjā markaṭī kṣā? caiva viṣaṃ markaṭakaṃ tathā ||  
vānarāsthi tathā śvetāśca vṛścikāḥ ||  
  
etāni samabhāgāni naramūtreṇa peṣayet |  
adhomukhaṃ mṛtaṃ sarpaṃ yatra daśyeta mānava ||  
  
tasyādhiṣṭhatva guphalāṃ sthāpayenmatimāṃ naraḥ |  
saptarātraṃ trirātragandhaṃ vā tato pralepayet ||  
  
eṣa eva pradātavyaṃ saptarātreṇa mariṣyati |  
pratyānayana punaḥ kṛtvā gokṣīrasarpi rakṣata ||  
  
yutaṃ annapāne dātavyaṃ svastho bhavati naraḥ |  
varāha idāṃ gopītaṃ narasya śoṇitaṃ ||  
  
etaccurṇaṃ samāyukta śirasthāna pralepayet | svastho bhavati |  
matsyapīttaṃ gavāmasthi viṣaṃ markaṭakaṃ tathā ||  
  
vānarāsthi gṛddhā caiva śveta vicchaṃ tathaiva ca |  
etaccūrṇaṃ peṣayitvā pralepayet |  
  
nocetaśṛgālamalaṃ pāne tasya pradāpayet |  
kuśasya mātraṃ samālabdha pṛṣṭhaṃ yadi madhubhasmabhiḥ ||  
  
tasvaiva tasya paṃcarātraṃ ca kuṣṭhaṃ prajāyate |  
pratyānayanaṃ vakṣyāmi śṛṇu caiva samāsataḥ ||  
  
saptavarṇābhagātraṃ ṣaḍaṃ ṣaṃḍaṃ ca jāyate |  
  
mṛyate nātra saṃśayaḥ |   
  
gopitaṃ madanaphalaṃ vacāṃ kūṭaṃ ca candanaṃ |  
śirīṣavījaṃ māṃsīṃ ca sarṣapāṇi tathaiva ca ||  
  
samabhāgaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā ajākṣīreṇa peṣayet |  
tataḥ kuṣṭhādi bhūtānāṃ kṛṣṇāṃjanaṃ pralepayet ||  
  
tena saṃpadyate mokṣaṃ pratyānayanamicchatā |  
  
105a)  
  
saptarātraṃ prayogena tataḥ kuṣṭhādvimucyate ||  
  
kukūṭī caiva gojihvā māṃsaṃ kṛṣṇo ragasya ca |  
kākamāṃsaṃ mahāmāṃsaṃ kṛṣṇoragasya ca ||  
  
haritālaṃ manaḥ śīlā ajākṣīreṇa peṣayet |  
tataḥ jra?guṭikāṃ kṛtvā vadaramātraṃ pramānutaḥ ||  
  
ānaṃ pṛca tataḥ sokṣatāṃ madena payasā api |  
pānena sahadātavyaṃ hṛdrogaṃ tasya jāyate ||  
  
chāgamūtreṇa haritaṃ vyādhākṣīrasameva ca |  
evaṃ pānaṃ pradātavyaṃ hṛdayarogavināśanaṃ ||  
  
odanaṃ ca ajākṣīraṃ saptarātraṃ pradāpayet |  
śaśakasya tu māṃsāni māṃsaṃ kṛṣṇoragasya ca ||  
  
samabhāgaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā sahīkṣireṇa bhāvayet |  
saptarātraṃ sthite tasmiṃ deyaṃ gatvānu lepamoṃ ||  
  
gātraṃ tasya samātreṇa tataḥ kuṣṭhaṃ prajāyate |  
devadāru haridrā devīrajanimadanatva ca ||  
  
piṣṭvā mahīṣamūtreṇa yasya lepaṃ pradāpayet |  
saptarātra prayogena kuṣṭharogāt pramucyate ||  
  
mātuluṃga sa vījāni tapakarakasyāsumo? |  
cūrṇabhāgaṃ samaripau dadāti paraṃ ca sarveṣāṃ yogānāmutpādakaraṇaṃ mahat   
|   
  
kṣīramārjya tathāgavyaṃ pānaṃ tasya pradāpayet ||  
  
pratyānayanametasya munmattī kṛtanāśanaṃ |  
māṃsaṃ vyāghradasyakṣa kṛkalāśasya tathā ||  
  
ulūkamāṃsasamāyuktaṃ sarvamekatra saṃgrahet |  
samabhāgaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā ajākṣīreṇa peṣayet ||  
  
etatpadiṃ pradātavyaṃ guṭikāṃ kārayet budhaḥ |  
kṣīrasaṃyuktaṃ tena bhakṣitamātreṇa saptarātraṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
bhagaṃdarādi rogāni bhaviṣyantiṃ vahuni ca |  
  
etatprātyānayanavarjitaṃ |  
  
vibhālamalaṃ marīcāniṇenitaṃ kṛṣṇa sarpasya |  
naramāṃsaṃ tathā vyāghra viṣamaṃbhakameva ca ||  
  
gṛhagodhāśca paṃcasavikāścadaṃtu usadvi saptāhaṃ sthāpayed bhājane   
śubhe |  
  
sarānāṃ ca phalāgre ca deyaṃ śatru jighāṃsayāḥ |  
vidhāya puruṣākāraṃ sa yāti yamamaṃdiraṃ ||  
  
105b)  
  
pratyānayanaṃ vakṣyāmi yena śāntiḥ prajāyate |  
mayūrapittaṃ saṃgṛhya pittaṃ ca nakulasya ca ||  
  
pippalī sāri vā drākṣā triphalā candanaṃ vacā |  
teṣāṃ dvedhābhibhūtānāṃ ādau yasya mahāsukhaṃ ||  
  
matsyasya viṣaṃ datvā mārayet tatkṣaṇādbudhaḥ |  
ātmanā tu gṛhṇīyād dadyādāpayasyado phalaṃ ||  
  
yaśca bhakṣayate nityaṃ mṛyate tasya māsāni māranīyā bhaṭaḥ |  
saṃyojayet payaḥ sarkarāmiśca cūrṇaṃ saptarātraṃ samyak saṃpadyate sukham ||  
  
patrāṇi śatapuṣpāni aśvapuṣpaṃ tathaiva ca |  
śaśanābhi tathā caiva saṃkocaṃ caiva parṇikā ||  
  
mūlaṃ girikarṇikameva ca |  
  
ātmavījasamāyuktaṃ yasya dīyate budhaḥ |  
sa tasya vaśo bhavati kṣipraṃ puṣpaiḥ sarvavidhikriyā ||  
  
mūlanakṣatre mūlaṃ phalaṃ saṃgṛhya tathā rocana caṃdanaṃ |  
tripuṣpasamāyuktaṃ tilakaṃ rājapūjitaṃ ||  
  
sa tasya vaśyaḥ nātra vicāraṇā |  
mohaye śatrusaṃhāraṃ iti śāstrasa niścayaḥ ||  
  
mūlanakṣatre mūlaṃ saṃgṛhya bharaṇī nakṣatre valkalaṃ citrā nakṣatre yaṃtraṃ   
viśākhā nakṣatre puṣpaṃ jyeṣṭhā nakṣatre phalamenānnakṣatre svetatsaṃgṛhya   
sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ kārayet |   
  
locanālakṣakākarṇaṃ prayogaṃ sarvaśodhanaṃ |   
  
puṣpe vā ādrāyāṃ haste āditye ca yadā tadā tilakaṃ kārayet prājño   
naranārīvasaṃ kuru |  
  
viṣṇukrāntāṃ ca sarpākṣīṃ bhāvayecca punaḥ punaḥ |  
tena kṛtvā tilakaṃ surāsuraṃ mohayet ||  
  
oṃ trailokyamohani sarvabhūtavaśaṃkarīṇi hrī& svāhā |  
  
aṣṭottara śataṃ paṭhaṃti surāsuravaśamānayati |  
narasya locanaṃ gṛhya dviradasya madena tu ||  
  
bhāvayitvā tu maṃtreṇāṣṭottara śataṃ priye |  
pāne vilepa dhūpāni sa vaśo bhavati kṣipraṃ dhanadaḥ prāṇado bhavet ||  
  
priyaṃgukalikāmiśraṃ guggulaṃ dhūparodhitaṃ |  
kṛtvā aṣṭaśataṃ caiva śubhagaṃ saṃprajāyate ||  
  
106a)  
  
jāti kālikā miśrāṇimadhvā jātināhuteḥ |  
śubhagatvaṃ mavāpnoti rūpaṃ hīnopi yo naraḥ ||  
  
aghoreṇa kṛtaṃ homaṃ lavaṇe tilamiśrite |  
saptāhā ghāti sa dveṣamāyāti yātri kāyiṇenagarvitāḥ ||  
  
rājikālavane caiva madhukṣīraṃ ghṛtaplutaṃ |  
gomayena samāyuktaṃ pūrvokta maṃtreṇa hunet ||  
  
śarṣapaṃca kṛte sādhyaṃmiti śāstrasya niścayaṃ |  
strīyāmaṣṭapuruṣasya pādapāṃśuṃ samāharet ||  
  
śaśigrahaṇe homayet |  
  
aṣṭasahasraikaṃ hutvā yasya nāmnāya paurṇātaśīghramākarṣayati ||  
  
śmaśānāṅgā rasaṃ gṛhya caturdaśyāṃ ca buddhi *? |   
striyo vā puruṣasyāpi ākṛtiṃ ca samālikhet ||  
  
tasya hṛdaye ca ārūhya sahasraṃ parijapyate |  
pūrvaṃ maṃtraṃ mahābhāga sādhyanāmavidarbhitam ||  
  
āditya grahane tadvarjayitvā prayatnataḥ |  
raktakaravīra kusumena tāḍayet ||  
  
śirasāṃ bhūṣivikeśādi kīrṇaṃ ca strī ca nagnā caiva samākulā ca dhātu   
maṃtraṃ japyese karpitā rūpase viyutā ||  
ānaye nitare tu svāmuṃ hṛtāghana saṃśayaśapūrtajorīya raktā ca saha devī   
tathaiva ca ||  
  
sahadevā samāyuktaṃ grāhya somaparvaṇi |  
maṃtreṇānena tajjapyaṃ rocanā yojitena ca ||  
  
tilakaṃ kārayed vidvān strīpumān vaśamānayet |  
somarājīṃ vacāṃkuṣṭaṃ śmaśānāṃgārameva ca ||  
  
cūrṇīkṛtya prayatnena guṭikāṃ kārayennaraḥ |  
puṣpe phale ca mūle ca vaśī kṛtvā rāja pūjyo bhavati ||  
  
pūrvokta maṃtreṇāṣṭottara śata nāma japet |  
athoccāṭanaṃ pravakṣyāmi saṃkṣepānna tu vistarāt ||  
  
sūryagrahaṇa saṃprāpte lāṃgalīmūlamuttamaṃ |  
śmaśānāṃgārasaṃyuktaṃ devadhvajasamanvitaṃ ||  
  
tasya bhāvī kṣipraveśma maṃtreṇānena buddhimān |  
  
oṃ hu& phaṭ amukaṃ mohayastaṃ bhaya uccāṭaya hu& phaṭ svāhā ||  
  
106b)  
  
anena maṃtreṇa ekaviṃśati vārāṇi abhimaṃtrā yasya gṛhe nikhanet sa   
uccāṭayati sarṣapaṃ | pretakeśāsthi śivanirmālyameva ca |   
  
vibhītakāsthi saṃyuktaṃ sthāpayedyasya veśmani |   
maṃtraḥ tasya pravakṣyāmi uccāṭana karaṃ paraṃ ||   
  
oṃ hā& hu& hu& hu& phaṭ svāhā |  
  
ayaṃte rājate maṃtraṃ sugopitaṃ prakaṭi kṛtaṃ |  
lakṣajāpena saṃsiddhye sarvakarmāni kārayet ||  
  
asiddha kurute karma kiṃ punaryastu sādhayet |  
ādityādi mukho bhūtvā sahasraṃ parijapyate ||  
  
saptarātra prayogeṇa śatrumuccāṭayeddhṛtaṃ |  
sakṛtvāduritametaṃ ripunāma vidarbhitaṃ ||  
  
uccāṭanakaraṃ jayaṃ saptajaptena saṃśayaḥ |  
siddhimaṃtramidaṃ kāryamasiddhasya vidhismṛtam ||  
  
ripornāma samuccārya arcane maṃtra saṃpuṭaṃ |  
yajamānasya krodhā viṣṭena cetasā ||  
  
dakṣiṇāni mukho bhūtvā ripumuccāṭayaṃt kṣaṇāt |  
raktakaravīreṇaṃ raktena kusumena homamācaret ||  
  
sahasrā uccāṭayati śatruṃ aptopi gacchati |  
athānyacca pravakṣyāmi yogaṃ bhuvi sudurlabhaṃ ||  
  
ye uccāṭayeta vā pravardha vāla darpitaṃ |  
sadyomyo vāhane sārddha svajane parivārake ||  
  
maṃtrarājaṃ purāproktaṃ rājo nāma vidarbhitaṃ |  
uccāṭanakaraṃ homaṃ lakṣajāpyaṃ prakartavyaṃ śmaśāne vā vadhiradhiḥ |   
daśāṃśahomabhāveṣṭodyaguggulu rājīkā | tataḥ prabhāta samaye sarveṣāṃ   
asthisaṃyutāṃ caturdikṣu diśi nyasya prakṣipecca diśo daśaḥ ||  
  
śīghramuccāṭayedrājā vinādravyeṇa suvrataḥ |  
pūrvokta maṃtraṃ saṃśodhyaṃ tataḥ karmasamārabhet ||  
  
dakṣanāḍī pravāhena uccāṭana kriyāṃ kuru |  
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi viśeṣoccāṭanaṃ mahat ||  
  
pūrvāmaṃtreṇa buddhijñā hi maṃtreva samārabhet |  
  
107a)  
  
catuṣpathe kuṇḍaṃ kṛtvā kākapakṣa ulūkayoḥ ||  
  
saṃpūrṇahomena tatkṣaṇe uccāṭanaṃ bhavet |  
athavātena siddhye taṃ upāyaṃ śṛṇu tatvataḥ ||  
  
mahāputtalikā kāryārti nāmaṃ samālikhet |  
tasya putuyasthāni saṃkṣipya ripusaṃkṣaye ||  
  
tanmaṃtreśca dine śīghraṃ kuru uccāṭanaṃ dhruvaṃ |  
athavā māyet śatru pravṛddha bala darpitaṃ ||  
  
maṃtro nyāsaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣva pārthivātmaja |  
karpājanāpitta saṃgṛhya ripornāma vigarbhitaṃ ||  
  
adhomukhaṃ ca tat kṛtvā bhasmanātha prapūrayet |  
nadī tīre samāsādhya dedīṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ ||  
  
vidyādhvaka pānasthāpya tato homaṃ tu kārayet |  
rājikālavanaṃ caiva viṣaṃ nāgarameva ca ||  
  
saptarātra prayogena avasya mṛyate punaḥ |  
pūrvokta maṃtrarājena saptarātraṃ ca homayet ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ pitta māyūraṃ ca samārabhet |  
sahasramaṣṭottaraṃ dattaṃ āyasā nirmitāya ca ||  
  
saptarātra prayogena avaśya mṛyate punaḥ |  
pūrvokta maṃtrarājena saptanābhaṃ ca homayet ||  
  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ pitu maṃjulaṃ ca samārabhet |  
sahasramaṣṭottare datta āyasā nirmitāya ca ||  
  
dakṣiṇābhimukho bhūtvā muktakeśaḥ kṛṣṇavāsā svadakṣa nāḍī pravāhena   
homavidhimācaret ||  
  
tatparortho sthātavyaṃ māyūraṃ kuṇḍapārśvataḥ |  
anenaiva tu maṃtreṇa mārayecchatru dāruṇān ||  
  
oṃ hu& hu& kṣā& rāṃ amukaṃ māraya rāṃ kṣāṃ hu& hu& svāhā |  
  
eṣā saptadaśī vidyā akṣare samudāhṛtā |  
māraṇe sarvabhūtānāṃ maṃtre trailokyaṃ sa carācaraṃ ||  
  
ādāpadaṃ ca duṣṭātmā deva brāhmaṇa dūṣakaḥ |  
mātṛhāpi tṛhā caiva nityaṃ sā parāyanaḥ ||  
  
śaśakamāraye rāja na vidviṣṭovasadājane |  
anyathā naiva kartavyaṃ aparārdha śatairapi ||  
  
prathame mohitaṃ caiva dvitīye mayūraṇaṃ |  
  
107b)  
  
uddhṛte tṛtīye uparīṣṭhastu caturthe ca dhṛti ||  
  
paṃcame bhagnakaṃdastu ṣaṣṭhe mūrdhita retasaḥ |  
saptame mṛyate bhūmyāṃ mṛyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||  
  
atha prayogaṃ pravakṣyāmi yatsurairapi durlabhaṃ |  
staṃbhane sarvabhūtānāṃ saṃkṣepena vadāmyaham ||  
  
viṣṇukrāntā ca sarvākṣī nāgaparṇī valā tathā |  
utpādyat puṣpanakṣatreṇaṃ maṃtrena na sādhakaṃ ||  
  
kāryāṇi kṛṣṇapakṣe ca āditasya dine tathā |  
nikṣipedari gehe sarvamauṣadhī maṃtra saṃyutānāṃ nāśeṣiyena vadāmyahaṃ   
viṣṇukrāntā |  
  
oṃ ṣajya hu& hu& hu& amukaṃstaṃ bhaya 2 hu& hrī& ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ phaṭ |  
  
anena maṃtreṇa staṃbhayati na cāsyadi ekodeya na caika pravivodhakaṃ |  
svaninīdhau mahāmaṃtraṃ staṃbhayed vilvayoni vā ||  
  
paṭhite siddhiśuddhiṃ ca sadyaḥ pratyayakārakaḥ |  
māhiṣaṃ navanītaṃ ca sindūrakanakaphalaṃ ||  
  
sudarśano nīlapuṣpī nāgītyā ca mahekamāyāṃti niścalo yate mahī   
pratyāyanavimaḥ malakākṣīraka na bhavati |  
  
sarpākṣi jñāna jihvā ca madanasya phalāni ca |  
godhākapinākalaṣāsthi kṛkalāsaṃ ca lohitaṃ ||  
  
etatsarvaṃ vasā gṛhya sūṣkaṃ cūrṇaṃ tu kārayet |  
mahātailena saṃmiśraṃ yasya lepaḥ pradīyate ||  
  
pūrvokta maṃtrasahite narasya staṃbhanaṃ bhavet |  
pratyānayane ca ye maṃtrā na buddhyate sadā ||  
  
māmahīṣī yatsusānāṃ staṃbhanaṃ yadi kārayet |  
tadāhaṃ kārapiṣyaṃti krīḍārthaṃ maniṣibhiḥ ||  
  
gojihvā sālaparṇi ca tathā saṃkoca patrikā |  
vajrī kṣīraṃ tu ruskaṃ ca śatruparṇī tathaiva ca ||  
  
saṃgṛhya samabhāgāni suṣkaṃ cūrṇaṃ tu kārayet |  
śisumārasya tailena miśrayecca prayatnataḥ ||  
  
taile naiva ca saṃśiktā proktaṃ maṃtrayojitaṃ |  
  
108a)  
  
staṃbhanaṃ sarvago mahiṣādi catuṣpadāṃ samaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
uṣṇodakena prakṣālya pratyānayanadariṇa |  
evaṃ ca svastha māyāṃti gomahiṣapaśujātayaḥ ||  
  
triśūlakā ca tathā gaurasarṣapau vibhītakā |  
sthi sindūraṃ tiktālāvukameva ca ||  
  
uṣṇodakena sādhyasya maṃtreṇānena sādhaka |  
  
oṃ hu& kra& hastaṃbhana svāhā |

maṇḍuke jalasarpābhyāṃ carmasaṃgṛhya bhāvayet ||  
  
sarātodhatuṣakāyamaṃtraṃ caiva vivodhayet |  
oṃ jalayāsi sarvalokavidhāraṇī maṃtra staṃbhanastaṃbha svāhā ||  
  
jale yathā svecchayā jala calavarttiṣvīti |  
māṃsīkanakapuṣpāni saptaparṇī vacā tathā |  
  
makarapittasaṃyuktaṃ śuṣkaṃ cūrṇaṃ tu kārayet |  
saralepamedhāvi saṃviśeṣacca hutāsane ||  
  
oṃ namayopanidīyani staṃbhani rīṃ rīṃ rūṃ rūṃ hu& svāhā |

nāgārīmūlakāyuktā sarpasthāpi mukhe kṣipet ||  
  
sasarpaḥ staṃbha pāyāti prasupta vatiṣṭati |  
  
oṃ hu& koṭarākṣi vagalāmukhi dayadīrgha sāpini gatiṃ staṃbhaya svāhā |  
  
kumārī varjanī mūla śarapuṃkhī sahaikatā |  
eṣa dhūpa prayogena sarpāṇāṃ kuṇḍavandhanam ||  
  
iti sarpastaṃbhanaṃ |  
  
devadeva namastubhyaṃ bhairavaṃ bhairavānanaṃ |  
senānī staṃbhanaṃ vakṣye ca bhairavena yathoditaṃ ||  
  
108b)  
  
svayaṃbhu jantuke liṃge devāle keśavethavā |  
tatra sthitvā japellakṣaṃ dyekaṃ vibhuḥ samāhitaḥ ||  
  
navākṣaraṃ mahāmaṃtraṃ pravakṣyāmi nibodhataḥ |  
  
oṃ saṃ raṃ kṣaṃ saṃ laṃ vaṃ dhaṃ krīṃ svāhā |  
  
eṣa te maṃtrarājoyaṃ duṣṭaśatrunivāraṇaḥ |  
bhaṃjakaśca prasaṃtyevaṃ svasainyaṃ parirakṣati ||  
  
japitavyaṃ prayatnena sadā vijayavardhanaṃ |  
smaraṇāt maṃtrarājasya bhayarogāvivarjitaḥ ||  
  
mahābhaye samutpanne pīlīgāya mayaṃ śubhaṃ |  
tato gṛhyaparigṛhya pralipedvasudhātalaṃ ||  
  
aṣṭapatraṃ svaitapadmaṃ ālikhecca tathāmunā |  
caturdikṣūtha kalasaṃ sthāpitavyaṃ matimānnaraḥ ||  
  
paṃcaratna samāyuktaṃ dviroṣaddhi samanvitaṃ |  
jayati vījasaṃtā ca tathā vacā parājitā ||  
  
sahadevī lakṣmaṇā caiva śaṃkhapuṣpī ca saptamī |  
aṣṭau ca soma rājī ca kalaśābhyantare kṣipet ||  
  
śvetavastra paricchannaṃ divyagandhānu lepayet |  
bhūtapallavasaṃyuktaṃ tatramaṃtraṃ ca vinyaset ||  
  
maṇḍale pūjaye devaṃ tattan maṃtraiśca pūjayet |  
jāpya tasyāgrataḥ kāryo home caiva niraṃtaraṃ ||  
  
raktapuṣpai ca tato devaṃ saṃpūrṇa bhairavaṃ vibhum |  
devaṃ devīṃ namaskṛtya rajasārdhanaṃ ||  
  
akṣetrānudakaśaramiśrāṃ snāstu sarvān visecayet |  
athā gajāṃstathālokā udakenāpi siṃcayet ||  
  
dhanuṣaṃ varjarīṃ khaḍgaṃ gadāṃ kṛṣṇaṃ ca muttamaṃ |  
abhiṣīcya mahātmānaṃ śatrusainyakṣayaṃ bhavet ||  
  
anena vidhināyasturavāgaṃ kuryāttu mānavaṃ |  
saṃbhave ativārājñā śatrukṣayaṃkarā ||  
  
parasainyaṃ staṃbhayati yadi indra samoripuḥ |  
  
atha vetālasādhanaṃ |  
  
mṛtakasya ca sāṃgṛhya rocanāṃ bhasma eva ca |  
kākolūkasya pakṣāni dahitvā bhaṃjanaṃ budhaḥ ||  
  
109a)  
  
kartavyaṃ caiva medhāvī maṃtreṇānena maṃtritaṃ |  
  
oṃ kṣā& kro& svāhā |

vada teṣāṃ prakartavyaṃ mayātava mahātmanaṃ |

japitaṃ ca jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ arddharātreyati krāṃte ete āgachati tu saḥ ||

vicaret pṛthivī sarvāṃ kāmadeva ivāparaḥ ||  
  
mohani saṃpravakṣyāmi trailokyeṣu suviśrutāṃ |  
yā jñātvā sarvasatvānāṃ śubhagatvaṃ prajāyate ||

phalau budhaḥ |

109b)  
  
subhagaḥ sarvalokaiko naronārī pravartate |  
śatru ca mitratāṃ yāti kiṃ kurvanna vidhiyate ||  
  
duṣṭa caureṣu rājasu sarpavyāghra vṛthakādiṣu |  
sarve te vaśamāyāṃti ājñāṃ kurvaṃti nityasaḥ ||  
  
oṃ bhave bharokṣa bhūkṣo bhayamohaya sarvasasvaṃ vaśamānaya kuru me hīṃ   
mohinīye svāhā |  
  
idaṃ mūlamaṃtraṃ | asya jāni bhavaṃti | oṃ bhūte iti hṛdayaṃ | oṃ bhūge bhaga   
iti śiraḥ | oṃ khaṃ bhakṣau bhayaśikhā | oṃ sarvatva ca mama kuru kavacaṃ | hrī&

kṛtvā japet |   
  
ekaliṃgajapellakṣaṃ sūcirbhūtvā samāhitaḥ |  
raktatamālapuṣpāṇi trimadhubhāvitāni ca ||  
  
homenā yute naikena siddhirbhavati īpsitā |  
khāne pāne sahate kāmān karoti karmasiddhyati ||  
  
tasi acirāt sidhyaṃti sādhakasya na saṃśayaḥ |  
siddhārthāt maṃtrayitvā tu maṃtritvā sammataṃstrīyā ||  
  
śirasi saṃvidhātavyaṃ puṣpe mūle punarvasau |  
vaśī bhavati sā nārī ātmanā ca dhanena ca ||  
  
athavā puruṣe kuryān maṃtranāmnorabhedataḥ |  
trisaptaka prayogena dāsatvaṃ puruṣaṃ nayet ||  
  
rājñāṃstu purato rājāppaśalyocāri sādhakaḥ |  
aṣṭottara śate jāpye vaśo bhavati nānyathā ||  
  
athānya ddhamamānasya rasyādau samupāharet |  
svāmi padena tilakaṃ sarvopadrava nāśanaṃ ||  
  
athāsya prayogāni bhavaṃti sarvasiddhayaḥ |  
duṣṭānāṃ caiva nārīnāṃ madagarvena garvitaḥ ||  
  
vaśīkaraṇa hetvarthaṃ śṛṇuṣvāṃ mimāṃ sudhī |  
vāmapādodbhavāṃ pāśu vāmahastena vāharet ||  
  
saptābhimaṃtritaṃ kṛtvā tilakaṃ kārayennaraḥ |  
śāstrī bhavati vasyā yatpādādha tata samudbhavaṃ ||  
  
sugopyaṃ ca imaṃ yogaṃ na dadyādyasya kasyacit |  
  
110a)  
  
satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyaṃ bhairavamaṃtranaṃ tathā ||  
  
na deyaṃ duṣṭa satvānāṃ āgame gopayet sadā |  
śāstra bhaktāya pradātavyaṃ anyathā naiva kārayet ||  
  
puruṣavaśīkaraṇe dakṣiṇa pādapāṃśu gṛhītyāṣṭādārāgnākarā varāgnau

dhruvaṃ |

evaṃ dhyānaṃ purā śaṃbhoḥ kṛtvā sarvaṃ samārabhet |  
homāvasāne punaḥ sthānaṃ dvitīyaṃ ca nivodhataḥ ||  
  
śatroḥ saṃcitya kṛṣṇavarṇaṃ muktakeśaṃ cātmānaṃ |  
vaddho vai kālapāsena tādyaṃ māno mahāvalaiḥ ||  
  
puruṣai sarvasadṛṣṭastasthānānnipate vahiḥ |  
sanitvā puruṣa dvāraṃ saṃkṣipto giriṃ madhyataḥ ||  
  
evaṃ dhyānaṃ prakartavyaṃ śatrutulyo viyoripuḥ |  
ṣaṭpiṃḍadhvaṃ sanatsthānāt kiṃ punaḥ smānaṃ vānapi ||  
  
oṃ ṣādū? pūjyaṃ tu mahākālaṃ kābhīṣama paramahāvikārālaṃ   
amusārūmārūṣaṣaḥ ||  
  
oṃ lavalā amisītiṣṇosīdaṃdāgrīdehṛdayemasyadahagātrāni dahanaga tathāni
